{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 22:46:23","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 22:46:23","title":"The 5 Best Pull-up Alternatives (How to Do Pull-ups Without a Bar)","link":"https://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=3841278","description":"<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3841296\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/kermit-pink-panther-hanging.jpg\" alt=\"A picture of Kermit hanging with Pink Panther, probably trying a pull-up alternative.\" width=\"727\" height=\"333\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/kermit-pink-panther-hanging.jpg 727w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/kermit-pink-panther-hanging-300x137.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/kermit-pink-panther-hanging-713x327.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/kermit-pink-panther-hanging-610x279.jpg 610w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/kermit-pink-panther-hanging-600x275.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 727px) 100vw, 727px\" /></p> \n<p><b>So you want to do a pull-up but don’t have a bar?</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Or maybe you just don’t quite have the strength yet to hoist yourself up?</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Either way, no problem!</span></p> \n<p><b>We’ve been teaching people how to do pull-up alternatives in our </b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><b>Online Coaching Program</b></a><b>, with “no-bar pull-ups”. Today, we’ll show you all these tried and trusted workarounds.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> We help people get their first pull-up, and we're really good at it. Learn more: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><b>Here’s what we’ll cover:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=3841278#pull-up-alternatives\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How to do pull-ups without a bar (5 pull-up alternatives)</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=3841278#first-pull-up\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The 6 best pull-up alternative exercises (How to get your first pull-up)</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=3841278#easiest-pull-up\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">What is the easiest type of pull-up? (Start with chin-ups)</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=3841278#do-pull-up\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When should I do my pull-up alternatives? (Next steps)</span></a></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let’s get started!</span></p> \n<p><span id=\"more-3841278\"></span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"pull-up-alternatives\"></a>How to Do Pull-ups Without a Bar (5 Pull-up Alternatives)</h2> \n<p><iframe title=\"No chin-up bar?? No problem! Five alternatives!!\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/7RzPW-nVfuk?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><strong>The video above comes from <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/prime-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Nerd Fitness Prime</a>, as part of the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/the-nerd-fitness-chin-up-challenge/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Chin-up Challenge</a> we are currently hosting.</strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Coach Jim walks you through 5 different levels of pull-up alternatives, depending on your experience level and what items you may have lying around the house.</span></p> \n<p><b>Pull-up Alternative #1: <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Doorway Rows</span></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our first alternative is to simply use your doorway for </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/inverted-row-are-you-missing-out-on-this-great-exercise/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">bodyweight rows</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3841279\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/doorway-row-jim.gif\" alt=\"A gif of Coach Jim showing you a doorway row, our first pull-up alternative.\" width=\"460\" height=\"255\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">To perform a doorway row:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Stand in front of your doorway and grab both sides.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Place your feet a little closer to the doorway, so you’re leaning back.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Sit back so you put weight on your arms.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pull yourself forward.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That’s it. The more you lean back, the tougher this will be.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">To start, you can also just hang back to start building some “pull” strength.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3831706\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/hang_doorway.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"459\" height=\"258\" /></p> \n<p><b>Pull-up Alternative #2: <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Towel Doorway Rows</span></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our next alternative is to do doorway rows, but this time using a towel.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3831705\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/row_doorwaytowel.gif\" alt=\"A towel can help you do a bodyweight row, as shown here.\" width=\"460\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The towel might help you lean back even further, creating a more challenging exercise.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Take a towel, and fold it twice lengthwise. Then take your long, folded over towel, and tie it around the door on the handle opposite side of you.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Make sure the door opens AWAY from you. You don’t want the door accidentally opening, which could cause an unexpected tumble.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you have your towel secured around the doorknob, perform rows by using each side of the towel.</span></p> \n<p><b>Pull-up Alternative #3: <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Inverted Rows with Chairs</span></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For this pull-up alternative, you’re gonna need two sturdy chairs and a broomstick (or dowel).</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’ll be combining them together, Voltron style, to form our own row station:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3831702\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/row_dowel.gif\" alt=\"This gif shows Jim doing a row on chairs\" width=\"459\" height=\"258\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The important thing here is the setup. Give your newly created station a few gentle pushes to check the integrity of the structure. Only when you feel confident should you <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/inverted-row-are-you-missing-out-on-this-great-exercise/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">start performing inverted bodyweight rows</a>.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Pull-up Alternative #4: <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Towel Pull-ups</span></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Now, we’re gonna start doing some actual pull-ups…with towels.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3831693\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/chinup_towel.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"460\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can either use a couple of sturdy handtowels or washcloths.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Tie an overhand knot in the corner of both towels, which will be used as your anchor.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Then place these knots over a door and close it. Make sure the knots are secure before you start doing your pull-ups.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Again, you’ll also want to make sure the door opens AWAY from you.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Doing towel pull-ups is going to be a great way to </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-improve-your-wrist-mobility-and-grip-strength/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">improve your grip strength</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, although if you find them a little too tough, you can use a stool to support your feet as you lift. This will help as you build strength.</span></p> \n<p><b>Pull-up Alternative #5: <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Strap Pull-ups</span></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You may or may not have some Forearm Forklifts hanging around, but if you do, you’ll have the perfect equipment for a pull-up alternative.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Forearm-Forklift-Appliances-Mattresses-L74995CN/dp/B008ASBLJI\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Forearm Forklifts</a> are made to help you and a friend lift heavy furniture or equipment, but Coach Jim has discovered they’re also pretty useful for doing pull-ups.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3841284\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/doorway-chin-up-straps.gif\" alt=\"This gif shows Coach Jim using Forearm Forklift straps to do this pull-up alternative.\" width=\"460\" height=\"255\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They have loops designed to hold your arms, which makes them easier to grip than a towel.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Tie a knot in them just like you would with a hand towel and use it to anchor against your door.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><em>For more ideas on how to train with items you may have around the house, check out&nbsp;</em><em><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-a-home-gym-the-ultimate-guide-for-garage-gym-ideas/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">How to Build a Home Gym (When All Equipment is Sold Out)</a>.</em></p> \n<h2><a name=\"first-pull-up\"></a>The 6 Best Pull-up Alternatives (How to Get Your First Pull-Up)</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3841297\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mouse-hanging.jpg\" alt=\"This is a picture of a mouse hanging, who is trying to get his pull-up alternative.\" width=\"647\" height=\"368\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mouse-hanging.jpg 955w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mouse-hanging-300x171.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mouse-hanging-713x405.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mouse-hanging-768x437.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mouse-hanging-610x347.jpg 610w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mouse-hanging-600x341.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 647px) 100vw, 647px\" /></p> \n<p><b><i>This section is taken from our guide “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Get Your First Pull-up.</a>”</i></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you can’t quite hoist yourself up yet, don’t fret!</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’re going to work on increasing your “pull” muscles through a series of pull-up alternatives.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">First up…</span></p> \n<h3><b>Level 1 Pull-up Alternative: <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-bent-over-row-the-ultimate-guide-for-dumbbell-and-barbell-row-training/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Bent-Over Dumbbell Rows</a></b></h3> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3635721 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/dumbbell-row.gif\" alt=\"This pull exercise can help you build muscles so you can eventually do pull-ups!\" width=\"398\" height=\"224\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Bent-over dumbbell rows:&nbsp;</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">8 reps each arm (or as many as you can do)</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rest for a 2-minute break</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Do another set</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Repeat until you hit 3 sets</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-much-weight-should-i-be-lifting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">What weight should you start out with initially?</span></i></a></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whatever allows you to get to at least 5 reps a set.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you can do 3 sets of 8 reps (each arm), it’s time to pick up a heavier dumbbell.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This will allow you to get stronger and stronger.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you can lift a 25-pound (10kg) dumbbell or heavier, consider moving up to the next level.</span></p> \n<h3><b>Level 2 Pull-up Alternative: Inverted Bodyweight Rows</b></h3> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3585382 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/steve-inverted-row-1.gif\" alt=\"The inverted row is a great way to develop your &quot;pull&quot; and back muscles.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/inverted-row-are-you-missing-out-on-this-great-exercise/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Bodyweight rows</a> are the PERFECT precursor to pull-ups </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">– they work the same muscles, and have you lifting your own bodyweight, just at a different angle.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our goal here will be to work towards a lower and lower angle, increasing the difficulty of the movement.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So at first, we’ll do rows with the bar higher up:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3585378 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-incline-inverted-row.gif\" alt=\"Start with inclined inverted rows for your pull-up workout. Then drop lower for more required effort.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Then we’ll progress to getting the bar lower:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3585379 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-bodyweight-row.gif\" alt=\"Add bodyweight rows to your workouts\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As soon as you’re doing bodyweight rows where your body is at a 45-degree angle or lower, you can progress to the next level.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<h3><b>Level 3 Pull-up Alternative: Assisted Pull-ups</b></h3> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">At this point, you are going to start actually doing pull-ups…with a little bit of assistance.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’ve got a few options for you.</span></p> \n<p><b>#1) Assisted Pull-ups with Chair</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3585411 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/assisted-pull-up-chair.gif\" alt=\"A chair can be a great tool to help you get your first pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Either one foot or two on the chair, depending on your needs. Your feet are ONLY there for support, use your upper body as much as possible.</span></p> \n<p><b>#2) Assisted Pull-ups with an Exercise Band</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3585413 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/assisted-pull-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"Staci using a band for an assisted pull-up, a great exercise for a bodyweight circuit.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can get different types of exercise bands with different levels of strength, or a variety pack for easy progression.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Put your foot in the exercise band and pull yourself up.</span></p> \n<p><b>#3) Assisted Pull-ups with a Partner</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3585414 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/pull-up-friend.gif\" alt=\"A friend can be a great asset when you're trying to do a pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Have a friend hold your feet behind you and help you complete each rep. Have them use the least amount of help possible to get you through your workouts.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you’re comfortable doing a form of assisted pull-ups, and can do about 10 repetitions, it’s time to advance to the next level.</span></p> \n<p><b>This is probably the TOUGHEST level before getting your pull-ups. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you get stuck on “assisted pull-ups” and “assisted chin-ups”, you’re not alone. This is where most people get stuck.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We work hand-in-hand with people like you to get them their first pull-up in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Online Coaching Program</a>. If you don’t know how to fit these movements into your workouts, or you just want somebody to give you the exact workout to follow every day, we got you!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> No guesswork. No confusion. Just a workout program that’s customized for you. </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h3><b>Level 4 Pull-Up Workout: Negative Pull-Ups</b></h3> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3585415 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/negative-pull-up.gif\" alt=\"Staci jumping up to do a negative pull-up., a great movement until you can bring regular pull-ups into your circuit.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Our next level on our path for a pull-up is what we call “negative pull-ups.”</strong></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grab onto the bar with an overhand grip</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Jump so your chest is touching</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Slowly lower yourself under control until you’re at the bottom of the movement.</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As you continue to lower yourself down, you’ll build strength, eventually creating enough muscle so you can pull yourself up.</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you want more specific instructions on any of these levels or movements, check out our guide “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Get Your First Pull-up</a>” for more</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"easiest-pull-up\"></a>What Is the Easiest Type of Pull-Up? (Start With Chin-Ups)</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3655962\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/pull-up-vs-chin-up.jpg\" alt=\"Staci showing a pull-up to the left and a chin-up to the right.\" width=\"498\" height=\"373\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/pull-up-vs-chin-up.jpg 990w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/pull-up-vs-chin-up-300x225.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/pull-up-vs-chin-up-768x575.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/pull-up-vs-chin-up-713x534.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/pull-up-vs-chin-up-600x449.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 498px) 100vw, 498px\" /></p> \n<p><b>The easiest pull-up variation for you to attempt will likely be the chin-up.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That’s why we’re hosting a </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/the-nerd-fitness-chin-up-challenge/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Chin-up Challenge</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, because we feel Rebels will have an easier time lifting themselves up with this variation, compared to a traditional pull-up.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For reference:</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A </span><b>CHIN-UP</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is when your hands are facing towards you:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585418\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/chin-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"A chin-up is a pull-up, but with your hands facing towards you.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A </span><b>PULL-UP</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is when your hands are facing away from you:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585416\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/pull-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"The classic pull-up\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>Chin-ups are generally easier to perform than pull-ups,</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> because the wider grip of a pull-up isolates your lats, which means you get less assistance from your biceps.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Start with chin-ups</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Once you get comfortable doing them, you can then work on more advanced variations. For ideas here, check out our guide </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-do-a-proper-pull-up-and-why-you-need-to-do-them/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How to Do a Pull-up</span></i></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"do-pull-up\"></a>When Should I Do My Pull-Up Alternatives? (Next Steps)</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3749633\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-spider-man.jpg\" alt=\"There are a lot of versions of Spider-Man out there.\" width=\"604\" height=\"316\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-spider-man.jpg 2043w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-spider-man-300x157.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-spider-man-768x402.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-spider-man-713x373.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-spider-man-600x314.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 604px) 100vw, 604px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Generally, you want a 48 to 72 hour resting period before returning to train the same muscle group.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So take at least a day off before working on your “pull” muscles again.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This allows the area to heal properly so you can grow stronger.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When we designed a training routine for </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/prime-overview-page/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Nerd Fitness Prime</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> members for part of the </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/the-nerd-fitness-chin-up-challenge/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Chin-up Challenge</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, we aimed for three workouts a week.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re trying to </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">get your first pull-up or chin-up</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, this would be a good goal.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So for example, you could do:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Monday:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Bodyweight Rows</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Wednesday:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Chin-up Negatives</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Friday:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Dumbbell Rows</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You could also do Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Even just working out Monday and Thursday – twice a week pull-up training – would allow you to see some great progress.</span></p> \n<p>Feel free to do whatever works best for you.</p> Squats?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587905 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-effective.png\" alt=\"As this sign shows, the squat is a super effective exercise.\" width=\"510\" height=\"173\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-effective.png 510w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-effective-300x102.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 510px) 100vw, 510px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Squats are one of the most foundational functional movements in our lives.</strong>&nbsp;Let’s talk about the benefits and why you should be squatting all the time.</p> \n<p><strong>#1) We’re designed to squat:</strong> We’ve been squatting since we&nbsp;were&nbsp;babies, but as we get older and sit in unnatural positions all day, our squat form goes from perfect to terrible.</p> \n<p>Crap.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em>In many countries, people often sit in a full squat for hours at a time.&nbsp;</em></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587297\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/third-world-squat-713x475.jpg\" alt=\"In many parts of the world, a squat is a normal position to sit in for hours. \" width=\"335\" height=\"223\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/third-world-squat-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/third-world-squat-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/third-world-squat-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/third-world-squat-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 335px) 100vw, 335px\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">From an evolutionary standpoint – it makes sense that we are genetically designed to, and can be really good at – squatting. </span></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Before modern-day furniture and technology you didn’t stop sitting in a full squat once you got older like we do today…you continued squatting your entire life.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">That’s why squatting is one of the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-ultimate-guide-for-functional-fitness-exercises-and-workout-plans/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">key moves for functional fitness</a>.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>#2) Squats are a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-12-best-compound-exercises-for-beginners-how-to-train-efficiently/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">compound movement</a> that recruits most of our muscles –</strong> this means it’s a movement that uses multiple muscle groups and joints (your hip and knee joints) to complete.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3587301\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat.gif\" alt=\"The squat movement as shown here.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>A simple bodyweight squat</strong> – which I’m demonstrating above –</span>&nbsp;uses almost every <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-ultimate-guide-for-the-best-core-exercises-how-to-strengthen-your-core/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">muscle in the core</a> and lower body.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">If you add a dumbbell or barbell into the equation, I would even argue that they use <em>every single</em> major muscle group to complete.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3632262\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/goblet-squat.gif\" alt=\"The goblet squat is a great way to build muscle for women.\" width=\"359\" height=\"202\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">In addition to every muscle in your “legs,” you need your hips, your back and core, your shoulders and arms. Nothing is left out with this monster movement.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Because of the utilization of a large amount of muscle groups, squats cause your body to increase our anabolic hormone production, helping us <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/lose-weight-and-build-muscle-or-do-one-then-the-other/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">lose fat and build muscle</a>.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=21628#footnote-1\" id=\"refmark-1\"><sup>[1]</sup></a></span></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>#3) Squats will help strengthen your bones and your muscles (and your knees!), and can also increase flexibility</strong>.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Increasing the strength in your knees and hips (and entire body) reduces your chance of injury while doing both athletic movements and everyday life things (such as shoveling the driveway or standing up and sitting down).</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And by learning to squat deeply, safely, you’re improving your range of motion and helping make you antifragile and protecting yourself against future injury. </span></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Bazinga!</span></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587345\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/bazinga.gif\" alt=\"Sheldon knows how amazing squats are for you, as demonstrated by this clever smile. \" width=\"259\" height=\"361\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><b>If your goals are to:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Build muscle and get stronger, squats will get you there faster.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Lose weight and get ‘toned,’ squats will get you there faster.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Look better naked, squats will get you there faster.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Get healthier and happier, squats will get you there faster.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Feel like an absolute badass in the gym, squats will get you there faster. </span></li> \n</ul> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>In short, squats are amazing</strong>.</p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(see what I did there?)</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">My name is Staci Ardison, I’m a </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Senior Coach</a>&nbsp;at Nerd Fitness, and my life has been absolutely transformed by barbell training, which is why I’m so excited to share this guide with you.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Back in 2011, I could <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/female-powerlifters-meet-staci-ardison/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">barely pick up a pink dumbbell</a>, and now I regularly compete in powerlifting competitions. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here I am squatting 253lbs for 3 sets of 5 at a bodyweight of 150 pounds:</span></p> \n<blockquote style=\"color: #c9c8cd; font-family: Arial,sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: 17px; text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://www.instagram.com/p/BzJYS5igP8Q/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">A post shared by Staci Ardison (@staciardison)</a> on <time datetime=\"2019-06-25T20:47:56+00:00\">Jun 25, 2019 at 1:47pm PDT</time></p> \n </div> \n</blockquote> \n<p><script async=\"\" src=\"//www.instagram.com/embed.js\"></script></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I am so excited to teach you how to squat today, as I’ve taught tons of <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">coaching clients</a> how to get started too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Want to learn to squat heavy like Coach Staci? Learn more about our online strength coaching program! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Let’s start off by taking a look at the bodyweight squat – the first move you should master before you add weight.</p> \n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><a name=\"proper_squat\"></a><strong>How to Do a Bodyweight Squat With Proper Form</strong></h2> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587906 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-sequence-539x600.jpg\" alt=\"This series of photos shows you how to do a proper squat.\" width=\"539\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-sequence-539x600.jpg 539w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-sequence-269x300.jpg 269w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-sequence-600x668.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-sequence.jpg 713w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 539px) 100vw, 539px\" /></strong></span></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>The setup for the squat exercise is incredibly simple.</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li dir=\"ltr\">Stand with your feet slightly wider than your hips.</li> \n <li dir=\"ltr\">Your toes should be pointed slightly outward – about 5 to 20 degrees outward (the wider your stance, the more you’ll want to rotate your feet outward).</li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3588108\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-feet-713x301.png\" alt=\"Your heels should be slightly wider than hip width apart, with your toes pointed outward\" width=\"713\" height=\"301\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-feet-713x301.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-feet-300x127.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-feet-768x324.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-feet-600x253.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<ul> \n <li dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Look straight ahead and pick a spot on the wall in front of you.</span></li> \n <li dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Look at this spot the entire time you squat, not looking down at the floor or up at the ceiling.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>I go over the setup and the full movement in this video:</strong></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Staci Demonstrates A Proper Bodyweight Squat | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/32vfud6KWSk?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>1) </b><strong>Put your arms straight out in front of you, parallel to the ground.&nbsp;</strong>Keep your chest up and proud, and your spine in a neutral position.</p> \n<p><b>2) Your weight is on your feet – it should be on the heels and the balls of your feet,</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> as if they were pasted to the ground. You should be able to wiggle your toes the entire movement (though that’s not a part of squatting!).</span></p> \n<p><b>3) Keep your entire body tight the entire time, your core flexed like you’re bracing to be punched in the gut!</b></p> \n<p><b>4) Breathe deeply into your stomach, break at your hip and push your butt back.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;Keep sending your hips backwards as your knees begin to bend. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s important to start with your hips back, and not by bending your knees.</span></p> \n<p><b>5) As you squat down, focus on keeping your knees in line with your feet. </b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Many new lifters need to focus on pushing their knees out so they track with their feet. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When your knees start to come inside the toes, push them out (but not wider than your feet).<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=21628#footnote-2\" id=\"refmark-2\"><sup>[2]</sup></a></span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Make sure your knees aren’t moving inward toward each other through the movement – this is very common.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3587420\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-713x377.jpg\" alt=\"Make sure you go deep enough with your squats!\" width=\"713\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-300x159.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-600x317.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>6) Squat down until your hip joint is lower than your knees (what we call “parallel” in the squat game). </b>Note: if you THINK you might not be squatting deep enough, you probably aren’t!</p> \n<p><b><img class=\"wp-image-3587418 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Squat-not-deep-enough.jpg\" alt=\"Keep going when doing your squat.\" width=\"200\" height=\"350\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Squat-not-deep-enough.jpg 215w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Squat-not-deep-enough-171x300.jpg 171w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px\" /></b></p> \n<p><b><img class=\"wp-image-3587419 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-good.jpg\" alt=\"Your squat should go about this low.\" width=\"204\" height=\"292\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-good.jpg 262w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-good-209x300.jpg 209w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 204px) 100vw, 204px\" /></b></p> \n<p><strong>Once at the bottom, it’s time to stand back up from your squat:</strong></p> \n<p><b>7) Keeping everything tight, breathe out and drive through your heels</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> (keep the balls of your feet on the ground as well).</span></p> \n<p><b>8) Drive your knees outward (away from each other) the same way you did on the way down,</b> and squeeze your butt at the top to make sure you’re using your glutes.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>Here is a video from us nerds at Team Nerd Fitness (with instructions from Jim, lead trainer at our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\">1-on-1 Online Coaching Program</a>) that will teach you good form on a&nbsp;bodyweight squat, including all the mistakes NOT to make:</strong></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"How to Do a Proper Bodyweight Squat | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/cB0cOX7gePg?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>Once you can do multiple sets of 15+ deep bodyweight squats with proper form, it’s time to move onto barbell squats!</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you are confident in doing bodyweight squats and want to work up to a barbell squat, follow our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Gym Workout Level 4 Program</a>, which includes dumbbell goblet squats, a good stepping stone to barbell squats:</span></p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_dr4dyi2cum dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/dr4dyi2cum/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p><b>The majority of the population has some sort of mobility issue (including myself!) that they are working on fixing.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We have LOTS of <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 coaching clients</a> who are new to squatting, and it often comes down to ankle flexibility and hip mobility. </span></p> \n<p><em><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you spend all day, every day, sitting in a desk chair, this might be you.</span></em></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you want us to help you fix your squat depth and start getting stronger, that’s what we’re here for!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Learn how to squat deep, properly and safely. Learn more about how our coaching program can help: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"barbell_squat_setup\"></a>How to Set Up Properly For The Barbell Back Squat</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3587447\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/barbell-squat-713x535.jpg\" alt=\"The barbell squat as shown here is a great way to get strong.\" width=\"713\" height=\"535\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/barbell-squat-713x535.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/barbell-squat-300x225.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/barbell-squat-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/barbell-squat-600x450.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/barbell-squat.jpg 1920w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>#1) Find your squat rack! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’ll look something like this, with an unattached barbell:</span></p> \n<p><strong>A. Squat Stand:</strong><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587722\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-stand-467x600.png\" alt=\"If you find a squat stand like this in your gym you are good to squat!\" width=\"388\" height=\"499\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-stand-467x600.png 467w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-stand-234x300.png 234w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-stand-600x771.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-stand.png 699w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 388px) 100vw, 388px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>B. Power Cage/Squat Rack:</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3588116\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-Rack-383x600.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"383\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-Rack-383x600.png 383w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-Rack-191x300.png 191w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Squat-Rack.png 417w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 383px) 100vw, 383px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>C. Half Rack (Least favorite*):</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3588117\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Half-Rack.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"308\" height=\"343\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Half-Rack.png 497w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Half-Rack-270x300.png 270w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 308px) 100vw, 308px\" /></p> \n<p><em>*I don’t like Half-racks without adjustable safety bars – if you want to squat deep the barbell might hit the immovable bars! Not cool. Aim for the A or B options if you have the choice!</em></p> \n<p><strong>Note: a squat rack is NOT the same thing as a Smith Machine, where the barbell is attached to the machine, and slides up and down two bars:</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3584079\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/smith-machine.jpg\" alt=\"Don't use the Smith Machine, unless it's for inverted rows at the gym.\" width=\"375\" height=\"500\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/smith-machine.jpg 375w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/smith-machine-225x300.jpg 225w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 375px) 100vw, 375px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>You do NOT want a Smith Machine. </strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You need a completely unattached barbell in order to do a barbell squat properly and safely. Don’t squat in a Smith Machine. </span></p> \n<p><strong>#2) </strong><b>Set the height of the bar to be about the same height as your collarbone. </b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not sure how to set the height of the bar? I got you:</span></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\">\n  <iframe title=\"102 - Squat Rack Intro Video\" src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/embed/iframe/56bylxp1ok?dnt=1&amp;videoFoam=true\" allow=\"autoplay; fullscreen\" allowtransparency=\"true\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" class=\"wistia_embed\" name=\"wistia_embed\" allowfullscreen=\"\" msallowfullscreen=\"\" width=\"100%\" height=\"100%\"></iframe>\n </div> \n</div> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If your options are either too high or too low, it’s always best to set the pins slightly lower than you need them.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You don’t want to have to get up on your toes to rack/unrack the bar, especially as the weight gets heavier.</span></p> \n<p><b>#3) Decide if you are going to do a high bar squat, or a low bar squat. Either is fine, but there IS a difference:</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587725 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/high-vs-low-bar-squat.jpg\" alt=\"These two photos show the high vs low bar grip for squat\" width=\"712\" height=\"190\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/high-vs-low-bar-squat.jpg 712w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/high-vs-low-bar-squat-300x80.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/high-vs-low-bar-squat-600x160.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 712px) 100vw, 712px\" /></strong></span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The “Low Bar Back Squat” is the most common form done by beginners, general lifters, and powerlifters. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s also the form taught in </span><em><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B006XJR5ZA/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B006XJR5ZA&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=nerdfitn-20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Starting Strength</span></a></em><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, one of the best books for beginners on the market. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So we’ll be focusing on that version for the rest of this section:</span></p> \n<p><b>#4) </b><b>Always squat with just the bar</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong> to start</strong> – </span><b>as we discuss in “</b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2014/02/06/strength-training-101-how-much-weight-should-i-be-lifting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><b>How much weight should I be lifting</b></a><b>,” </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">even if you’re planning on squatting 500 lbs, always start with just the bar!</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"barbell_squat\"></a>How to Do a Proper Barbell Back Squat, Step By Step</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3587901\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-low-bar-713x293.jpg\" alt=\"Here's how to properly do a barbell squat\" width=\"713\" height=\"293\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-low-bar.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-low-bar-300x123.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-low-bar-600x247.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>1) Facing the bar, step under it,&nbsp;and put your hands around it on either side of you.&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For this type of squat in our example, we are going to want a thumbless grip, so that our wrists are properly aligned with our forearms.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3587729\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-thumbless-grip-1.jpg\" alt=\"This photo shows the squat grip we will start with.\" width=\"357\" height=\"187\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-thumbless-grip-1.jpg 357w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-thumbless-grip-1-300x157.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 357px) 100vw, 357px\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The width of your grip will be dependent on flexibility, but generally a narrower (hands closer to your shoulers) grip will help create a meaty shelf for you to place the bar on the muscles in your upper back.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you lack the flexibility for the narrower grip (which is super common), start out wider, then slowly bring it in as you get more flexible.</span></p> \n<p><b>See the difference here between a “high bar, wrapped grip” (Left) and “low bar, thumbless grip” (right):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3587732\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-grip-examples.jpg\" alt=\"Here are the two common grips for your barbell squat.\" width=\"712\" height=\"190\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-grip-examples.jpg 712w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-grip-examples-300x80.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-grip-examples-600x160.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 712px) 100vw, 712px\" /></p> \n<p><b>And now time to DO A BARBELL BACK SQUAT!</b></p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_4miki3c9of dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/4miki3c9of/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p><strong>Definitely watch the video above and listen to the instructions, and then read this description when you need to restart:</strong></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">With the weight on your shoulders, step back from the supports.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your feet should be slightly wider than hip-width apart.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;Your toes should be slightly pointing outward.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Flex your stomach, squeeze your glutes, inhale deeply into your stomach.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Move your butt back, squat down slowly.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Continue to drop until the tops of your legs are parallel or lower (the crease of your hip is below your waist).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Explode back up to the starting position.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">After your set is complete, walk carefully forward to return the weight to the rack, and lower it down safely onto the supports.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">High five yourself, you just did a barbell squat!</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>Not sure if you squatted deep enough?</strong> </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Record yourself! 95% of the people I see doing squats in a gym don’t go deep enough!</span></p> \n<p><b>Nervous about squatting correctly? </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yes, I am a mind reader, and yes we can help you!</span></p> \n<p><b>If you want an expert to check your squat form check out our </b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><b>1-on-1 Coaching program</b></a><b>.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Our coaching app lets you record and send a video of your movement directly to your coach, who will provide specific feedback and build a custom program just for you.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>Interested?</strong> Click below to jump on a free call with our team to see how our online coaching program will get you the results you’re after:</span></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3547192 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-01-CheckForm-web75-713x403.jpg\" alt=\"Nerd Fitness Coaching Banner\" width=\"713\" height=\"403\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-01-CheckForm-web75-713x403.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-01-CheckForm-web75-300x170.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-01-CheckForm-web75-768x434.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-01-CheckForm-web75-600x339.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-01-CheckForm-web75.jpg 900w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Let us check your squat form! We’ll also build you a killer strength training program. Learn more: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><b><a name=\"bail_out_of_squat\"></a>How To Bail Out of a Squat Safely</b></h2> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\">\n  <iframe title=\"103 - Dumping Weight Safely Video\" src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/embed/iframe/mam9psd1he?dnt=1&amp;videoFoam=true\" allow=\"autoplay; fullscreen\" allowtransparency=\"true\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" class=\"wistia_embed\" name=\"wistia_embed\" allowfullscreen=\"\" msallowfullscreen=\"\" width=\"100%\" height=\"100%\"></iframe>\n </div> \n</div> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<p><b>If you are going to squat, you have to know how to “fail” at squatting safely! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">After all, there’s nothing more scary than being stuck in the bottom of a squat movement and not knowing how to get out of there!</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A squat is very different from a barbell deadlift in that aspect: if you fail on a deadlift, you just don’t pick up the weight. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you fail on a squat, you’re trapped under a bar with potentially a lot of weight on it.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This can lead to SERIOUS injury. So please, learn how to bail out of a squat safely before you start attempting to do heavy barbell squats.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This will help give you the confidence to push yourself and get stronger!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Want help getting strong as hell? Let our coaches build a custom strength program for you: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2>7<a name=\"squat_mistakes\"></a>&nbsp;Common Mistakes When Doing Squats</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3587894\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-mistakes-1-713x402.png\" alt=\"As these two photos shows, keep your feet planted while you are doing your squat.\" width=\"713\" height=\"402\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-mistakes-1-713x402.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-mistakes-1-300x169.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-mistakes-1-600x339.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-mistakes-1.png 714w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>The squat is a basic movement, but those new to lifting often fall victim to a handful of common mistakes.</strong></p> \n<p>Let’s take a look at some of the big problems and how to fix it!</p> \n<p><strong>#1) Coming up on your toes with your knees forward during your squat</strong></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">It’s important to keep your <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">heels on the ground the entire time</span> you’re squatting.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">You should be driving down through your heels, and in order to do that, they need to be on the ground!</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">While some of your weight will be on the balls of your feet, you never want all of your weight to be on the balls of your feet or your toes.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">You should be able to lift your toes up off the ground and wiggle them at any point and it shouldn’t change anything about your squat.</p> \n<p><b>#2) Not going deep enough on your squats</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587420 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-713x377.jpg\" alt=\"Make sure you go deep enough with your squats!\" width=\"713\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-300x159.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-depth-600x317.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Your squat should hit at least parallel (middle image above) – where your hip joint goes below the knee.</strong></p> \n<p>Depending on what you’re training for, you can go lower, but in order to maximize the muscles worked in the squat, it needs to be done to at least parallel or lower (you can see lower in the upper right image).</p> \n<p>If you squat above parallel (a partial squat) you’re leaving the hamstrings out of the movement. This puts more pressure on the knee – the force put on your knee is actually reduced as you drop below parallel.</p> \n<p><em>Unfortunately, there’s a&nbsp;lot of misunderstanding&nbsp;about squats and knee issues.</em></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>The deeper the squat, the more glutes that are activated as well.</strong> Deeper is typically harder, both strength and flexibility wise.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">However, depending on your goals, squatting to parallel may make more sense.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">If you’re struggling hitting depth there could be many causes – you could have poor ankle mobility, tight hip flexors and/or hamstrings, weak glutes, or poor pelvic alignment (among many other things).</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is something we work closely with our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">coaching clients</a> on, and often prescribe ankle and hip mobility drills to help clients reach proper depth on squats! </span></p> \n<p><b>#3) Knee Positioning&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3587895\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-knee-position.jpg\" alt=\"Don't let your knees cave in like this during your squat.\" width=\"196\" height=\"307\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-knee-position.jpg 196w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-knee-position-192x300.jpg 192w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 196px) 100vw, 196px\" /></p> \n<p>When you squat, you want your knees to track along with your toes.</p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This means if you are looking down at your knees and feet, your knees should be aligned at the same angle as your feet throughout the movement.</span></p> \n<p>Everyone’s exact positioning is going to be slightly different, but they should not be on the outside or the inside of the foot.</p> \n<p><strong>#4) Back Positioning&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3587896\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-back-position.jpg\" alt=\"Don't let your back cave in like so when doing squats. \" width=\"257\" height=\"306\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-back-position.jpg 257w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-back-position-252x300.jpg 252w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 257px) 100vw, 257px\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your chest should be up </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">and shoulders should be back</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, like you’re King Kong about to pound your chest proudly. </span></p> \n<p>Your body should stay in this position the entire time.</p> \n<p>You don’t want your shoulders to round forward, but you also don’t want to hyperextend your back either.</p> \n<p>Keeping your spine in a neutral position <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">will help your spine safe and build a strong foundation throughout the heavy squat movement.</span></p> \n<p><strong>#5) Head Positioning&nbsp;</strong><strong><br /> </strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3587897\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-head-position.jpg\" alt=\"Don't let your head come up like so during your squat movement.\" width=\"253\" height=\"306\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-head-position.jpg 253w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-head-position-248x300.jpg 248w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 253px) 100vw, 253px\" /></p> \n<p>Many coaches will tell their lifters to look up, as that is the direction in which you want to be moving, but this is actually the last thing you want to do.</p> \n<p>Take a second quick and look at the ceiling (I’ll wait! 🙂 ).</p> \n<p><strong>Now, see that position your <b>neck vertebrae are in</b>?</strong> That is a very unsafe position for your spine to be in, especially when more weight starts getting included in the equation.</p> \n<p>You also don’t want to be looking directly at the floor.</p> \n<p><strong>Look straight out in front of you the entire time,</strong> with your head in a “neutral” position. Your chin should be in a position where you could hold a tennis ball between your chest and your chin.</p> \n<p><strong>#6) Attempting to keep your shins vertical.</strong></p> \n<p>Unless there is a current underlying knee issue that would cause additional pain – <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">the shin can and should go past vertical in the squat</span>. This will often allow a deeper squat which will build more strength and stability in the knee.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3756889\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/steve-bodyweight-squat.gif\" alt=\"Rebel Leader Steve doing the bodyweight squat\" width=\"460\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p>A forward lean in the shins is also present when we engage in any number of daily activities such as walking up steps or standing up from a chair. Squat as deep as you are able, but do not focus on holding a vertical shin.”</p> \n<p><strong>#7) Too much weight on the heels/on the outside or inside of feet during your squat</strong></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">When trying to fix coming up on your toes, or your knee positioning, it is common for people to focus so much on keeping their weight on their heels that they forget to keep the balls of their feet on the ground!</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Some of your weight will still be on the ball of your foot – if you are truly only having weight on your heels, it’s pretty hard to balance.</p> \n<p><em>To the same effect, if the inside of your foot or the outside of your foot comes up off the floor, this is also not a good thing!&nbsp;</em></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How do you know if you’re making these mistakes? Simple! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Record yourself doing squats. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I do. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And so does anybody else who is serious about improving their squats.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Often we look VERY different than we think we look when doing an exercise, so having a video of the movement is often the only way we can improve.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you can’t self-diagnose your squat challenges, let us help!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3550367\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-24-BenchPress-web75-1-713x403.jpg\" alt=\"Nerd Fitness Coaching Banner\" width=\"713\" height=\"403\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-24-BenchPress-web75-1-713x403.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-24-BenchPress-web75-1-300x170.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-24-BenchPress-web75-1-768x434.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-24-BenchPress-web75-1-600x339.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-24-BenchPress-web75-1.jpg 900w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></a></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Let us check your form and teach you to squat properly! Learn more about our Coaching Program: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><b><a name=\"box_squat\"></a>Squat Variations for Beginners (Box Squat):</b></h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3587908 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-box-713x403.png\" alt=\"Squatting on a box like so is a great way to start squatting. \" width=\"713\" height=\"403\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-box-713x403.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-box-300x169.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-box-768x434.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-box-600x339.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-box.png 1387w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><b>In this section, we’re going to go over some squat variations to help you improve your form and build confidence before hitting the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">free weights section of the gym</a>. </b></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>If you’re struggling to do a squat correctly, don’t fret!</strong></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><b>I’m going to teach you about…</b></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><b>BOX SQUATS!</b></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Squatting to a box will help teach you to sit back and keep your weight on your entire foot, instead of squatting with your knees forward and up on your toes.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Squatting back to a box is also great for people who have bad knees and can’t do bodyweight squats anymore.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><b>You can do box squats with a barbell as well, but for this explanation, we’re just going to keep it simple with bodyweight box squats. </b></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>In order to do this, find a box or a chair that is the right height so when you sit on it, you are at parallel with your squat.</strong></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Your options include things like step stools, milk crates, or the smallest box at the gym (there’s usually a set of plyo boxes, and the shortest is around 10″.)</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3587867\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/box-squat.gif\" alt=\"Using a box to squat like so is a great way to start bodyweight squatting. \" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>The lower the box, the more it will help you develop stronger hips and low back</strong> – the box at exactly parallel will help you more with quad strength.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">Set up exactly as if you were going to do a regular bodyweight squat, only standing about a foot in front of the box.</p> \n<p><strong>1) Breathe in deeply, brace your core, move butt back, and keep your knees in line</strong> tracking in the same direction as your toes and squat back until you sit completely on the box.</p> \n<p>Don’t plop back on the box, make it slow and deliberate while keeping your entire body tight.</p> \n<p><strong>2) Now, don’t move! Think about your positioning:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>Are your back and core still super tight?</li> \n <li>Is your weight on your heels and your mid foot?</li> \n <li>Is your head in a neutral position?</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Great, now stand up by driving your hips upward, don’t let your weight shift forward and onto your toes (drive through your heels!), shoulders and chest up, knees out keeping them lined up with your toes.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em>For your first few, feel free to sit on the box while you evaluate your positioning, but as you get better at them, sit back and then quickly stand up again.</em></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>You know you’re doing a good squat when&nbsp;</strong>you can stand back up from the bottom of a squat position without having to lean forward and use momentum to get up.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">You can squat, touch your butt to the box, and then stand back up without having to shift your weight around!</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">KEEP THAT BUTT BACK!</p> \n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><a name=\"front_squat\"></a>How to Perform a Front Squat</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3602685\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Front-Squat-Bar-Location-713x383.png\" alt=\"Staci doing a front squat\" width=\"649\" height=\"349\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Front-Squat-Bar-Location-713x383.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Front-Squat-Bar-Location-300x161.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Front-Squat-Bar-Location-768x413.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Front-Squat-Bar-Location-600x323.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Front-Squat-Bar-Location.png 880w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 649px) 100vw, 649px\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>If you’re up for a similar-but-different squat, try…</strong></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>The barbell front squat!</strong></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3756986\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/barbell-front-squat.gif\" alt=\"Coach Staci performing the barbell front squat\" width=\"548\" height=\"308\" /></p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">A front squat moves the weight from behind you to in front of you, which requires different muscles and mobility in different places.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\">I personally alternate front squats and back squats on my leg days.</p> \n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em>Make sure you read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">full guide on how to do a proper front squat</a>.&nbsp;</em></p> \n<p><strong>I know all of this can be overwhelming, so the important thing is that you START!</strong>&nbsp;I realize I sound like a broken record at this point, but I really want you to begin strength training today.</p> \n<p>We created our free guide, <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><em>Strength Training 101: Everything You Need to Know</em></span>, just for that purpose. I’d love to send it to you, because I know it’ll help you overcome any fears and confusion and have you getting stronger TODAY</p> \n<p>Get it when you sign up in this box below – I’m excited to hear what you think of it!</p> \n<div class=\"nf-in-post-signup-leadin\"></div>\n<div class=\"nf-in-post-signup one-column split yellow-cta strength-101 shortcode-form-13 \">\n <div -CoachingBanner2019-01-CheckForm-web75-713x403.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn68@2020_4/2020/08/24/14-46-27-968_56208a3d6e843421.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-mistakes-1-713x402.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn51@2020_3/2020/08/24/14-46-37-826_af944f97dc42b8fe.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-knee-position.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn92@2020_5/2020/08/24/14-46-36-759_29f8863aca1c854d.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-back-position.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn60@2020_4/2020/08/24/14-46-36-292_9d40d4ccc1b98d5a.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-head-position.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn91@2020_2/2020/08/24/14-46-39-860_b9f36b660a985311.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/steve-bodyweight-squat.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn92@2020_6/2020/08/24/14-46-39-985_310354e61cd84b9f.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-24-BenchPress-web75-1-713x403.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn88@2020_4/2020/08/24/14-46-30-682_93498b09f471f0da.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/squat-box-713x403.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn56@2020_5/2020/08/24/14-46-29-069_bd8cf81f5fdfcafd.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/box-squat.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn88@2020_6/2020/08/24/14-46-40-787_ebc73d9ae03a823a.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Front-Squat-Bar-Location-713x383.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn60@2020_1/2020/08/24/14-46-40-741_a6f381317a7922d4.webp","https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/barbell-front-squat.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn56@2020_3/2020/08/24/14-46-40-239_064e298d href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">workout routine</a> is a great idea!</span></p> \n<p>This is one of our
