exercise as a stepping stone to help people <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">get their first pull-up!</a></p> \n<a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> A custom workout program designed for your goals. Learn more: </button> </a> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you do proper bodyweight rows, you build strength and muscle in your back, your biceps, your forearms, your grip, and even your core.</span></p> \n<p><strong>As part of our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Strength 101 series</a>, this guide will cover everything you need to know about this awesome exercise:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#inverted_row\">What is an inverted row or bodyweight row?</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#how_to_do_inverted_row\">How to do an inverted bodyweight row properly (with video).</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#progress_rows\">How to progress with inverted bodyweight rows.</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#inverted_row_workout\">When should I do inverted rows in my workout?</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#table\">How to do bodyweight rows at home with your kitchen table.</a></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span id=\"more-3667\"></span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"inverted_row\"></a>What is an Inverted Bodyweight Row?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3578068 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/staci-doing-ring-row-713x401.jpg\" alt=\"If you have gymnastic rings you can do an inverted bodyweight row like Staci here. \" width=\"713\" height=\"401\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/staci-doing-ring-row-713x401.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/staci-doing-ring-row-300x169.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/staci-doing-ring-row-768x432.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/staci-doing-ring-row-600x337.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/staci-doing-ring-row.jpg 957w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>You’ve probably heard of the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-bent-over-row-the-ultimate-guide-for-dumbbell-and-barbell-row-training/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">regular barbell row</a>.</strong>&nbsp;You pick up a barbell, bend over at the waist (keeping your back straight), and pull the weight up towards your chest.</p> \n<p>It looks something like this:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3677425\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/barbell-row-staci.gif\" alt=\"With proper form, there's nothing dangerous about the bent-over row.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>This can be a great exercise, but improper form could cause complications or <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">you might not have access to a barbell and plates.</span></p> \n<p><strong>Luckily, the bodyweight row (or inverted row) takes care of all of that.</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585405\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/overheand-row.gif\" alt=\"Alternate between an overheand and underhand bodyweight row.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>By the way, I’ll be using “bodyweight row” and “inverted row” interchangeably in this article.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#footnote-1\" id=\"refmark-1\"><sup>[1]</sup></a></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">To-may-to, To-mah-to.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#footnote-2\" id=\"refmark-2\"><sup>[2]</sup></a></span></p> \n<p>When doing this movement, you only need a bar to lean back from and your body weight. There’s also no extra stress on your back, like with a traditional barbell row.</p> \n<p>As an added bonus, you get a decent <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-ultimate-guide-for-the-best-core-exercises-how-to-strengthen-your-core/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">core workout</a> too.</p> \n<p><em>And there was much rejoicing.&nbsp;</em></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3584487\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/Final-Fantasy-Victory.gif\" alt=\"These final fantasy characters think bodyweight rows are great.\" width=\"342\" height=\"263\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Think of it like this: “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/what-do-you-bench-strength-training-101-the-bench-press/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">bench press</a>” is to “pushing” as “inverted row” is to “pulling.”</strong></p> \n<p><em>Balance FTW!</em></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><strong>Why the inverted bodyweight row&nbsp;is so great:&nbsp;</strong></span></p> \n<p>I’m a huge fan of <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-12-best-compound-exercises-for-beginners-how-to-train-efficiently/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">compound exercises</a> (like the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">squat</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-the-deadlift/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">deadlift</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">pull-ups</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">push-ups</a>), and I’m also a huge fan of exercises that don’t require expensive machines or lots of extra bells and whistles.</p> \n<p><strong>An inverted row works all of your pull muscles:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of your back muscles</li> \n <li>Your biceps</li> \n <li>Your forearms</li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-improve-your-wrist-mobility-and-grip-strength/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Your grip</a></li> \n <li>All the stabilizer muscles in between that make those muscles work together.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>If you’ve been doing <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/what-do-you-bench-strength-training-101-the-bench-press/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">bench presses</a> regularly, start doing an equal amount of work with your pull muscles to stay in balance and away from injury.</p> \n<p><strong>Oh, and if you want to eventually <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">be able to do pull-ups </a>THIS is the exercise you need to add into your routine until you can do a full pull-up.</strong></p> \n<p>Speaking of which, if you are just getting started with bodyweight rows <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">and want to one day do a pull-up</span>, let us help!</p> \n<p>We’ve created custom workout programs for men and women of all ages that have helped them get their first pull-up! And I want to help you get there too! Click in the box below to get the details:</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3550389\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-30-Ad1a-Pullup-web75-713x403.jpg\" alt=\"Christina learned to do pull-ups with NF Coaching\" width=\"541\" height=\"306\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-30-Ad1a-Pullup-web75-713x403.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-30-Ad1a-Pullup-web75-300x170.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-30-Ad1a-Pullup-web75-768x434.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-30-Ad1a-Pullup-web75-600x339.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-30-Ad1a-Pullup-web75.jpg 900w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 541px) 100vw, 541px\" /></a></p> \n<a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Get your first pull-up ASAP! Work with our amazing coaching program: </button> </a> \n<h2><a name=\"how_to_do_inverted_row\"></a>How To Do An Inverted Bodyweight Row</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585379\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-bodyweight-row.gif\" alt=\"Add bodyweight rows to your workouts\" width=\"533\" height=\"300\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Let’s start with the people who have access to a gym (<a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3667#table\">see a no-gym variation here</a>):&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><b>How to do an inverted row or bodyweight row:</b></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Set the bar (or your rings) around waist height. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The lower the bar, the more difficult the movement becomes.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Position yourself under the bar lying face up. </b><strong>Lie on the floor underneath the bar </strong>(which should be set just above where you can reach from the ground).</li> \n <li><strong>Grab the bar with an overhand grip<b>, slightly wider than shoulder-width </b> (palms facing AWAY from you).</strong></li> \n <li><strong>Contract your abs and butt, and keep your body a completely straight line.</strong> Your ears, shoulders, hips legs, and feet should all be in a straight line <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> (like you’re doing a plank)</span>.</li> \n <li><strong>Pull yourself up to the bar until your chest touches the bar.</strong></li> \n <li><strong>Lower yourself back down with proper form.</strong></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If this movement is TOO difficult, no big deal, we&nbsp;</span>just need to back up a few steps.</p> \n<p>Set the bar higher so that when you lean back, your body isn’t down on the ground; maybe it’s only at a 45-degree angle.</p> \n<p><em>We’ll walk you through a row progression right here.</em></p> \n<p><strong>Here’s Staci again demonstrating it at a higher angle:</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585378\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-incline-inverted-row.gif\" alt=\"Start with inclined inverted rows for your pull-up workout. Then drop lower for more required effort.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>By setting the bar higher, it takes more of your body’s weight out of the equation. </strong></p> \n<p>As you get stronger (and/or <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-not-suck-at-losing-weight/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">lose weight</a>), you’ll be able to drop the bar until you’re parallel when pulling yourself up.</p> \n<p>I grabbed a video of <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Senior Coach</a> Staci from Team NF demonstrating a bodyweight row with <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/lord-of-the-rings-how-to-get-in-great-shape-using-gymnastic-rings/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">gymnastic rings</a>, but the instruction you’ll get in the video will really be helpful too.</p> \n<p><strong>How to do a bodyweight row with explanation:</strong></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"71 - Ring Row Video\" src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/embed/iframe/q9t1tnbfpt?dnt=1\" allow=\"autoplay; fullscreen\" allowtransparency=\"true\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" class=\"wistia_embed\" name=\"wistia_embed\" allowfullscreen=\"\" msallowfullscreen=\"\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\"></iframe><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<p><b>Here are some tips and tricks for doing a proper inverted bodyweight row:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Don’t let your butt&nbsp;sag </strong>(squeeze your buttcheeks, flex your stomach, and keep your body rigid from head to toe).</li> \n <li><strong>Don’t flail your elbows. </strong> Grab the bar with your hands a little closer than you would if you were doing a bench press, and keep your elbows at that angle from your body.</li> \n <li><strong>Pull the bar towards the middle of your chest.</strong> Don’t pull the bar up towards your throat, or down towards your belly button. Right in the middle!</li> \n <li><strong>Keep your abs tight. </strong> Keep your abs tight throughout the whole routine. Your body should be a straight line the whole time, and the only thing moving is your arms.</li> \n <li><strong>Pull your shoulder blades&nbsp;<b>down and back towards each other through the movement</b>.&nbsp;</strong><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Don’t shrug your shoulders. Imagine you’re trying to pinch a pencil between your shoulder blades to keep it from falling! </span></li> \n <li><strong>GO all the way.</strong> Don’t half-ass it. Lower yourself until your arms are completely extended, and raise yourself until your chest touches the bar.</li> \n</ul> \n<a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Need help getting better at bodyweight rows? Let our coaches check your form! </button> </a> \n<h2><a name=\"progress_rows\"></a>How to Progress with Inverted Bodyweight Rows</h2> \n<p><strong>Let’s provide a blueprint on how you can level up your inverted bodyweight rows.</strong></p> \n<p><strong>#1) Doorway Rows</strong></p> \n<p>At first, just start doing some rows in your doorway:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3794600\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/doorway-row.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>This will help you start training your “pull” muscles.</p> \n<p><strong>#2) Towel Rows</strong></p> \n<p>Still utilizing your doorway, you can use a towel to lean back even further to increase the challenge here:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3831705\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/row_doorwaytowel.gif\" alt=\"A towel can help you do a bodyweight row, as shown here. \" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>Coach Jim walks you through setting up your towel row in this video, “<em>No chin-up bar?? No problem! Five alternatives!!</em>”</p> \n<p><iframe title=\"No chin-up bar?? No problem! Five alternatives!!\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/7RzPW-nVfuk?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><strong>#3) Inverted Row (High)</strong></p> \n<p>Next, try doing an inverted row, but set the bar high so it’s easier to perform:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585378\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-incline-inverted-row.gif\" alt=\"Start with inclined inverted rows for your pull-up workout. Then drop lower for more required effort.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>#4) Inverted Row (Low)</strong></p> \n<p>Once your inverted rows become easy, lower the bar to increase the challenge:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585379\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-bodyweight-row.gif\" alt=\"Add bodyweight rows to your workouts\" width=\"533\" height=\"300\" /></p> \n<p><strong>#5) Elevated Inverted Row&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p>If you place your feet in the air, you’ll make this exercise even tougher:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3775708\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/elevated-feet-row.gif\" alt=\"Raising your feet will make rows more challenging.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>#6) Inverted Row (Weighted)</strong></p> \n<p>If you really want to up the difficulty of your inverted rows, try doing it with a little bit of weight attached to you:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3835074\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/weighted-bodyweight-row.gif\" alt=\"Steve doing a weighted row\" width=\"481\" height=\"271\" /></p> \n<h2><a name=\"inverted_row_workout\"></a>When Should I Do Inverted Bodyweight Rows?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585375\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/steve-inverted-row.gif\" alt=\"Inverted rows are a great exercise to work on doing your first pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>If you are <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">building your own workout plan</a>, you can mix Inverted Bodyweight Rows in wherever you normally do your pull exercises (pull-ups, pull-downs, rows, etc.).</strong></p> \n<p>When I go into a gym, my time is extremely limited, and I’m working <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">towards developing strength</a>.</p> \n<p>Here’s a sample two day split for me:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Day A: </strong><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Squats</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/what-do-you-bench-strength-training-101-the-bench-press/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">bench press</a>, inverted rows, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-do-a-perfect-dip-no-tobacco-required/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">dips</a></li> \n <li><strong>REST DAY:</strong> OFF</li> \n <li><strong>Day B: </strong><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-the-deadlift/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Deadlifts</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-the-overhead-press/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Overhead Press</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-do-a-proper-pull-up-and-why-you-need-to-do-them/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Pull-Ups (or chin-ups)</a>, Planks (Floor Swipes).</li> \n <li><strong>REST DAY:</strong> OFF</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Both days work my full body, I can do a full routine in less than 40 minutes, and I’m building strength.</p> \n<ul> \n <li>If you can’t do dips on Day 1, you can do <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">push-ups</a>.</li> \n <li>If you can’t do pull-ups on day 2, you can substitute <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">assisted pull-ups</a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585413\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/assisted-pull-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"Staci using a band for an assisted pull-up, a great exercise for a bodyweight circuit.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>On the rows, aim for 3 sets of 10.&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We cover this in our “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-correct-number-of-reps-per-set-in-the-gym/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">sets and reps</a>” article, but you can never go wrong with 3 sets of 10! </span></strong></p> \n<p>If you can’t do that, do 3 sets to however many reps you can do, and build your way up to 3 sets of 10.</p> \n<p>Once you can do that, put your feet up on a chair, throw some weights in a backpack, put it on reverse (so the bag is hanging in front of you), and then do the rows.</p> \n<p><strong>You got this!</strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Overwhelmed? <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">I personally know how that feels</a>. It can be scary embarking on a strength training practice for the first time. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Are you doing your moves correctly? Should you be lifting more weight or less? What do you eat to reach your goals?</span></p> \n<p><b>We created the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Nerd Fitness Coaching</a> program to tackle these questions directly. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your own</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> coach will get to know you, build a program based on your experience and goals, and check your form on each movement (via video)</span><b>:</b></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3548590 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad1-InvertedRow-web75-713x403.jpg\" alt=\"Nerd Fitness Coaching Banner\" width=\"713\" height=\"403\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad1-InvertedRow-web75-713x403.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad1-InvertedRow-web75-300x170.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad1-InvertedRow-web75-768x434.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad1-InvertedRow-web75-600x339.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad1-InvertedRow-web75.jpg 900w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></a></p> \n<h2><a name=\"table\"></a><b>HOw to Do Inverted Bodyweight Rows at Home</b></h2> \n<p><iframe title=\"How to Do a Bodyweight Row | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/OYUxXMGVuuU?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>Just because you don’t have access to a gym doesn’t mean you can’t work out your back, you just need to get VERY creative. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Here’s how you can do Inverted Bodyweight Rows at Home:</b></p> \n<p><strong>PATH ONE: </strong><strong>Use your kitchen table. </strong> Or your desk. <em>Be very careful with this one</em>.</p> \n<p>Lie underneath your table so your head and shoulder are sticking out above it.</p> \n<p>Grab the table edge with an overhand grip, and pull yourself up (just like it’s explained above).</p> \n<p><em>Warning, don’t pull the table over with you, and make sure you don’t break the thing!</em></p> \n<p><strong>PATH TWO: Get a really thick wooden dowel or pipe</strong>, something strong enough to support your weight. Lie it across two of your kitchen chairs, and then lie down underneath it.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3831702\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/row_dowel.gif\" alt=\"This gif shows Jim doing a row on chairs\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>Make sure it’s sturdy, and the bar isn’t going to break/move on ya, and pull yourself up.</p> \n<p><strong>Don’t forget, you want to stay in balance.</strong></p> \n<p>If you don’t have a <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2YednCI\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">pull-up bar</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/lord-of-the-rings-how-to-get-in-great-shape-using-gymnastic-rings/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">gymnastic rings</a>, find a way to do some bodyweight rows whether it’s between two chairs or under a table.</p> \n<p>You’re smart, get creative!</p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This should allow you to start mixing in bodyweight rows into your <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Strength Training Routine</a>! </span></p> \n<p><strong>Any more questions about the inverted bodyweight row? </strong></p> \n<p>Leave em below!</p> \n<p><strong>-Steve</strong></p> \n<p><strong>PS:&nbsp;</strong><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>Our certified <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">NF instructors</a> can build you a custom plan for your lifestyle and goals</strong>. Instead of worrying about what to do next, simply follow the workouts and nutrition your coach has programmed.</span></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3548592 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad2a-InvertedRow-web75-713x403.jpg\" alt=\"Nerd Fitness Coaching Banner\" width=\"713\" height=\"403\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad2a-InvertedRow-web75-713x403.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad2a-InvertedRow-web75-300x170.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad2a-InvertedRow-web75-768x434.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad2a-InvertedRow-web75-600x339.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-22-Ad2a-InvertedRow-web75.jpg 900w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></a></p> style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Alright buckeroo, let’s do this thang!</span></p> \n<h2><span id=\"more-3749577\"></span><a name=\"why\"></a><strong>Why Is Training Your Core Muscles Important?</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3749585 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-ninjas.jpg\" alt=\"Being a ninja for sure requires a strong core.\" width=\"801\" height=\"374\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-ninjas.jpg 906w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-ninjas-300x140.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-ninjas-768x359.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-ninjas-713x333.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/lego-ninjas-600x280.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 801px) 100vw, 801px\" /></p> \n<p><b>You use your core muscles for just about everything:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Getting out of bed in the morning? Not without a sturdy core.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pushing a grocery store cart across the parking lot? Your core will make that happen.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fighting off ninjas who just discovered your secret identity? Karate kicks require a strong core.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3749586 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/kung-fu-kick.gif\" alt=\"Lots of core work taking place here.\" width=\"420\" height=\"178\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You get the gist.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So what exactly do we mean when we say “core”?</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Contrary to popular belief, your core isn’t just your abs.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3749587 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/muscles-of-the-core-diagram.jpg\" alt=\"A front and back image of the core muscles.\" width=\"650\" height=\"328\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/muscles-of-the-core-diagram.jpg 739w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/muscles-of-the-core-diagram-300x151.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/muscles-of-the-core-diagram-713x360.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/muscles-of-the-core-diagram-600x303.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Some of the muscles found in your core include:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b>Erector spinae: <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">this is the muscle around your spine and helps you stand up straight.</span></b></li> \n <li><b>Rector abdominis: <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">better known as your “abs.”&nbsp;</span></b></li> \n <li><b>Obliques: <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">these are found on the sides of your torso and help you twist (and shout).</span></b></li> \n <li><b>Gluteal muscles: <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">also known as your “glutes” or “butt” or “bum” or “ass” or – okay, you get the point –&nbsp; which connects your legs to your core.</span></b></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You might also hear your core referred to as your “trunk.” Same thing.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The core muscles really are the foundation of the human body. And much like building a house, when it comes to fitness, you need to start with a strong foundation.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is why we focus on building a strong core with each of <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">our coaching clients</a>.&nbsp;</span><br /> <a name=\"whatare\"></a></p> \n<h2><strong>What Are the Best Core Exercises for Beginners? How Can I Strengthen My Core at Home?</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3749588\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/mario-gang.jpg\" alt=\"Jumping and smashing blocks wouldn't be a bad core workout, but maybe not for beginners.\" width=\"804\" height=\"355\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/mario-gang.jpg 910w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/mario-gang-300x133.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/mario-gang-768x339.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/mario-gang-713x315.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/mario-gang-600x265.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 804px) 100vw, 804px\" /></p> \n<p><b>If you’re just starting your fitness journey, we won’t make you jump into the deep end quite yet.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>Here are the </b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>Best Core Exercises for Beginners</b></span><b>:</b></p> \n<p><b>#1) Plank</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3674917 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/steve-plank.gif\" alt=\"A plank, like so, is a great way to engage your core.\" width=\"468\" height=\"263\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your entire core is engaged in a plank, as you stabilize yourself in a straight line (don’t sink)!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you can’t quite support yourself into a full plank, have no fear, you can start with…</span></p> \n<p><b>#2) Knee Plank</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3594852 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/knee-plank.gif\" alt=\"If you can't do a normal plank, start with doing them on your knees until you can advance.\" width=\"478\" height=\"269\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Just like a regular plank, but you have your knees for support. Start with these until you can do the real thing.</span></p> \n<p><b>#3) Hip Bridge</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3622875 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/hip-bridge.gif\" alt=\"Raising your hips of the floor, like so, is how you do the bridge bodyweight exercise.\" width=\"419\" height=\"236\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The hip bridge will activate the glutes and the rest of your core as you bring your body up.</span></p> \n<p><b>#4) The Hollow Body Hold</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3615795 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/hollow-body-3.png\" alt=\"The hollow body is a great exercise to practice doing a handstand.\" width=\"506\" height=\"246\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/hollow-body-3.png 506w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/hollow-body-3-300x146.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 506px) 100vw, 506px\" /></p> \n<p><b>The hollow body is one of the best ways to engage the midsection and stabilize the body. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We utilize the hollow body exercise as part of our strategy for <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-handstands/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">getting your first handstand</a>.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you get comfortable holding the position, try…</span></p> \n<p><b>#5) The Hollow Body Rocking</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3615802 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/hollow-body-2.gif\" alt=\"Extending your arms will up the difficulty of this handstand workout.\" width=\"425\" height=\"239\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">These 5 exercises will go a long way towards developing serious core strength.</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Steve, these moves are easy peezy. What are some advanced core exercises?”</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I thought you’d never ask.</span><br /> <a name=\"the\"></a></p> \n<h2><strong>The 5 Best Core Exercises</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3673394 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/camp-barbell.jpg\" alt=\"Barbell training is very important, which is why we covered it at camp!\" width=\"799\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/camp-barbell.jpg 5168w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/camp-barbell-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/camp-barbell-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/camp-barbell-713x476.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/camp-barbell-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 799px) 100vw, 799px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Now the real fun starts.</b></p> \n<p><b>Here are <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">The </span></b><b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">5 Best Core Exercises</span>:</b></p> \n<p><b>#1) Squats</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3673401 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/staci-back-squat.gif\" alt=\"The back squat will help you transform into a superhero.\" width=\"398\" height=\"224\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Squats? Yes, squats.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Squats train just about every muscle in your core (and lower body). Your core is engaged as you stabilize yourself up and down. If you don’t currently train with squats, start with a simple assisted bodyweight squat:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3746069 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/assisted-bodyweight-squat.gif\" alt=\"Coach Staci showing you the an assisted bodyweight squat\" width=\"398\" height=\"224\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can also read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">full guide on how to perform squats</a> to level up your game.</span></p> \n<p><b>#2) Deadlifts</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3673403 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/staci-deadlift-3.gif\" alt=\"I promise you, learning how to deadlift will change your life.\" width=\"398\" height=\"224\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’re big fans of the deadlift around these parts. Not only is it a core exercise, but it’s really an EVERYTHING exercise (lower body, core, and upper body).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/female-powerlifters-meet-staci-ardison/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Senior Coach Staci</a> credits performing deadlifts to her visible abs:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3635731 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/staci-before-today-2.jpg\" alt=\"You can see that Staci has changed the way she looks from strength training!\" width=\"396\" height=\"395\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/staci-before-today-2.jpg 1000w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/staci-before-today-2-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/staci-before-today-2-300x300.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/staci-before-today-2-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/staci-before-today-2-600x600.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/staci-before-today-2-100x100.jpg 100w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 396px) 100vw, 396px\" /></p> \n<p>If you want a strong core, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-the-deadlift/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">start performing deadlifts</a>.</p> \n<p><b>#3) Push-ups</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3674909 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/steve-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Here Rebel Leader Steve shows you the classic push-up.\" width=\"416\" height=\"234\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Just like how a plank forces you to stabilize your core, a push-up will do all that and more as you push yourself up and down.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How’s your push-up form? Most people do them incorrectly. </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3652754\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey.png\" alt=\"As you can see, you want your arms to be like an arrow, not a T when doing push-ups.\" width=\"729\" height=\"521\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey.png 996w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-300x214.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-768x549.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-713x510.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-600x429.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 729px) 100vw, 729px\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Read our full guide on <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">how to do a proper push-up</a> to hone in your technique.</span></p> \n<p><b>#4) Pull-ups</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3585416 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/pull-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"The classic pull-up\" width=\"428\" height=\"241\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yes, pull-ups are an upper-body exercise. But you’ll engage your core as you hoist yourself up. The more you keep your body in control (don’t flail about as you go up and down), the more you’ll train your core.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Can’t do a pull-up yet? No problem, read “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">How to Get Your First Pull-Up in 30 Days</a>.”</span></p> \n<p><b>#5) Knees to Elbow</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3623200 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/elbow-to-knee.gif\" alt=\"If you have a bar to hang from, you can try this core bodyweight exercise.\" width=\"396\" height=\"223\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This will challenge your core like you wouldn’t believe. The slower you go, the more intense it will be.</span></p> \n<p><b>Bonus Core Exercise: Toes to Bar</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-3623211 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/toes-to-bar.gif\" alt=\"This is an advanced move, but is a great core bodyweight exercise.\" width=\"398\" height=\"224\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is an advanced move, but a great core exercise that only requires <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B002YQUP7Q/ref=oh_aui_search_detailpage?ie=UTF8&amp;psc=1=nerdfitn-20&amp;linkId=a50dc69466ff1e4b7beae056e5441765\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">a pull-up bar</a>!</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Are you doing these moves correctly? A good way to check would be to record a video of yourself and match it against the gifs and videos here. If they look close, you’re doing great!</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The other option would be to have a trained professional review your form, which we can do in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Online Coaching Program</a>!</span></p> \n<p><b>Our spiffy mobile app lets you send a video of your training directly to your coach, who will provide feedback so you can perfect your technique.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They’ll also build a workout program that’s custom to your situation, which can improve your core strength!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Have a Nerd Fitness Coach build you a core workout and check your form! Click here to learn more! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><a name=\"situps\"></a></p> \n<h2><strong>Why You Shouldn’t Do Sit-Ups</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3749589 size-full\" title=\"Some cartoon characters doing sit-ups. \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/doing-sit-ups.png\" alt=\"As we'll discuss, this scene was avoidable.\" width=\"512\" height=\"156\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/doing-sit-ups.png 512w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/doing-sit-ups-300x91.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 512px) 100vw, 512px\" /></p> \n<p><b>You may have noticed that we haven’t covered sit-ups in our guide on the best core exercises.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is 100% intentional. You don’t need to do sit-ups.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In fact, there’s an argument you SHOULDN’T do sit-ups at all.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Sit-ups can be hard on your back.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=3749577#footnote-1\" id=\"refmark-1\"><sup>[1]</sup></a> They’re also an incomplete exercise, as they don’t work out your entire core (stomach AND lower back).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So skip the sit-ups and crunches.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re gonna do a crunch for your core exercise, go with a Reverse Crunch:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3623145 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/reverse-crunch.gif\" alt=\"The reverse crunch is a great way to engage your core during your bodyweight workout.\" width=\"469\" height=\"264\" /><br /> <a name=\"burns\"></a></p> \n<h2><strong>“What Exercise Burns the Most Belly Fat?” (Best Core Exercise for Weight Loss)</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3617641 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1.jpg\" alt=\"Buddha isn't trying to lose weight. But he's also zen about you trying to.\" width=\"802\" height=\"337\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1.jpg 2048w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-300x126.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-768x322.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-713x299.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-600x252.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 802px) 100vw, 802px\" /></p> \n<p><b>There’s a common belief that if you simply do enough crunches or sit-ups, you’ll get a flat stomach.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I hate to break it to you, but this isn’t true.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s something I bring up in the article: “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/can-you-actually-banish-belly-fat/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Can You Actually Banish Belly Fat?</a>”&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>You cannot spot reduce fat on your body:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not on your thighs.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not on your love handles.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not on your stomach.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is why the Thighmaster is a joke:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3602485 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/thighmaster.gif\" alt=\"Out of all the exercise equipment out there, the Thighmaster is probably the least effective.\" width=\"480\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Depending on your age, weight, sex, and genetic makeup, your body will lose fat in a certain order, from certain parts of your body, that you can’t control.</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are some things to consider:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b>Everybody has abdominal muscles. <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yep, even you! They might be tiny, or weak, but everybody has 6-pack abs. They might just be hidden under a layer of fat. No judgment, just reality.</span></b></li> \n <li><b>Fat does NOT turn into muscle – they are two different things. <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Like oil and water, fat sits on top of muscle. You could have ridiculously strong abs ready to pop out, but if they are buried under a lot of fat, no amount of exercise will give you a flat stomach or make those abs pop, because it doesn’t address the fat on top of your muscles.</span></b></li> \n <li><strong>A flat stomach only appears when you have a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/body-fat-percentage/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">low enough bodyfat percentage</a>.</strong> <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The reason there are 1,000,000,000 ab workouts on YouTube is that people know there’s BIG money in the ab-industry for people desperate to get a flat stomach! And ab exercises are much easier to market as exciting than “eat better, get strong, move more, for a long long time.”</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So if you want a flat stomach or six-pack abs, we need to create a plan for sustainable weight loss.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I know, WAY EASIER SAID THAN DONE.</span></p> \n<p><b>Have no fear, I have a couple resources for you:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-lose-weight-without-dieting-5-rules-of-weight-loss/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">How to Lose Weight Without Dieting (The 5 Rules of Weight Loss)</a>: <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">you’ve probably been on a diet before. You might even be on a diet right now. We discuss why they generally don’t work (temporary changes create temporary results) and provide a less conventional but more permanent solution (tiny changes for the win).</span></b></li> \n <li><b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Our 1-on-1 Online Coaching Program</a>: <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">many of our clients spent years yo-yoing their weight, going from one diet to another. It’s only when working with one of our coaches that they were able to <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-christina-lost-50-pounds-31-total-inches-and-did-her-first-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">achieve sustainable weight loss</a>.&nbsp;</span></b></li> \n</ul> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Want to lose weight without hating life? Learn how we can help. </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><a name=\"build\"></a></p> \n<h2><strong>How to Build a Core Workout (Next Steps)</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3616371 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/handstand-landscape.jpg\" alt=\"Today we teach you how to do a handstand!\" width=\"799\" height=\"216\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/handstand-landscape.jpg 1920w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/handstand-landscape-300x81.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/handstand-landscape-768x208.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/handstand-landscape-713x193.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/handstand-landscape-600x162.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 799px) 100vw, 799px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Now that we know how to perform the best core exercises, you know what time it is?</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s my favorite time.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s time to <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">build a workout routine</a>!</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3604351 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/apes-dancing.gif\" alt=\"Let's start bodyweight training!\" width=\"457\" height=\"257\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Woot.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I generally recommend beginners strength train two to three times a week with a full-body workout.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>We’re going to make sure our full-body workout hits the following:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Quads (front of your legs).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Butt and hamstrings (back of your legs).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Chest, shoulders, and triceps: (“push” muscles).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Back, biceps, and grip ( “pull” muscles).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Core (abdominals and lower back).</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We just went over what you should do for that last segment, “core”.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">What should you do for the others?</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> For ideas, read our guide: “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">How To Build Your Own Workout Routine</a>.”</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That will help you build a practice to grow strong.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Don’t get startled by my comment that you should train “two to three times a week.” If you can only do a full-body workout once a week, that’s WAY BETTER than none a week.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you get the practice going, we can always work to increase the frequency later.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The most important thing you can do today is start:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3750164\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/mario-kart-start.gif\" alt=\"If you wanna win a race, you need to start it!\" width=\"416\" height=\"233\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Want a little help getting going? The perfect next step on what you should do now?</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">No problemo!</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are 3 options on how to continue with Nerd Fitness:</b></p> \n<p><b>Option #1) If you want step-by-step guidance on how to lose weight, eat better, and get stronger, check out our killer <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 coaching program</a>:</b></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3574583\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1.jpg\" alt=\"Your NF Coach can help you lose weight and get healthy!\" width=\"1311\" height=\"401\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1.jpg 1311w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-300x92.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-768x235.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-713x218.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-600x184.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1311px) 100vw, 1311px\" /></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Our coaching program changes lives. href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/?p=1310713#get_started_bodyweight_training\">How to get started with bodyweight training.</a></li> \n</ul> \n<p>Let’s jump right in!</p> \n<p><span id=\"more-1310713\"></span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"what_is_bodyweight_training\"></a>What Is Bodyweight Training?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-1310947 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Rings.jpg\" alt=\"Campers using bodyweight training at Camp NF. \" width=\"680\" height=\"415\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Rings.jpg 680w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Rings-300x183.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Rings-160x98.jpg 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 680px) 100vw, 680px\" /></p> \n<p><em>“Use your body to improve your body.”</em> <em>– Something some zen master said at some point probably</em></p> \n<p><strong><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Bodyweight training</span> means doing any exercise that leverages your own bodyweight to build strength and muscle, burn fat, and become more resilient.</strong> Now, you might think that’s just basic stuff like <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">push-ups</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">squats</a>. Those things ARE bodyweight movements, and absolutely crucial to building a healthy foundation.</p> \n<p>Hidden in plain sight however, your own body’s weight is actually a complete training system waiting to be used. +5 points to Gryffindor for you being a complete training system.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3836268\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/snape-clap.gif\" alt=\"A gif of Snape clapping for bodyweight training\" width=\"371\" height=\"237\" /></p> \n<p>You can use your body’s weight as a centerpiece in your training routine for decades to come, like me:</p> \n<blockquote class=\"instagram-media\" style=\"background: #FFF; Today, we’ll take you through exactly how to get started.</p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">The best part</span>: since bodyweight training scales in difficulty and has plenty of variety, it truly can be used from Level 1 to Level 50.</p> \n<h2><a name=\"bodyweight_vs_weight_machines\"></a>Is Bodyweight Training Better Than Weight Machines?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-1310965 \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pushups_kid.jpg\" alt=\"A picture of two people doing bodyweight push-ups. \" width=\"660\" height=\"440\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pushups_kid.jpg 1280w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pushups_kid-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pushups_kid-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pushups_kid-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pushups_kid-160x107.jpg 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 660px) 100vw, 660px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Your body is a complex piece of machinery that has been fine-tuned over thousands of </strong><strong>generations.</strong> Think of yourself as Human Ver. 100000000.0.0.1. We’ve been doing “bodyweight training” as a species since our days as cavemen and cavewomen – except back then it wasn’t called training, it was called “life” and there was no spandex:</p> \n<p><strong>Things like:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>Sitting in a deep squat around a campfire with our tribe.</li> \n <li>Crawling under and over things as we encountered obstacles in nature.</li> \n <li>Pulling ourselves up into a tree or over a cliff to escape danger.</li> \n <li>Pushing ourselves up onto a ledge or platform to get a better view.</li> \n <li>Swinging from vine to vine as King of the Jungle. (Okay maybe not this one).</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Because we’ve had to adapt to do all of those things to survive, our bodies LOVE the idea of working with all of our muscles and bones and joints in unison to accomplish movements or overcome obstacles. If you’ve ever heard the term “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-ultimate-guide-for-functional-fitness-exercises-and-workout-plans/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Functional Fitness</a>,” that’s what we’re talking about here.</p> \n<p>It’s the reason we <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2013/01/24/rage-against-the-machine-how-to-switch-from-exercise-machines-to-free-weights/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">rage against the machines</a>&nbsp;in the gym – cue “Bulls on Parade” – they often create imbalances and other weird problems through isolation and non-functional movement.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3761080\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/chest-press.gif\" alt=\"A typical machine exercise found here.\" width=\"193\" height=\"344\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Think of it this way</span>: Cavemen didn’t pick up various rocks to isolate their triceps muscles or do “curlz for the cavegurlz.” And they certainly didn’t lie on a bench at a 30-degree angle while doing log presses to emphasize their upper pectoral muscles before going to kill a gazelle.</p> \n<p>Instead, men and women did whatever they needed to do in order to survive — and their bodies adapted as a result.</p> \n<p>If you’ve been reading Nerd Fitness for a while, you know I’m a fan of this quote from the trainer of the actors in the movie 300: <em>“Appearance is a consequence of fitness.”</em></p> \n<p>Bodyweight exercises tap into our full, natural anatomy. Movements like <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">squats</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">push-ups</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">pull-ups</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-do-a-perfect-dip-no-tobacco-required/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">dips</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/inverted-row-are-you-missing-out-on-this-great-exercise/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">rows</a> are <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-12-best-compound-exercises-for-beginners-how-to-train-efficiently/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">compound exercises</a> that recruit all the muscles in our body and teach them to work in unison.</p> \n<p>When you do bodyweight training, your body becomes more efficient working as a unified organism: all of your muscles, tendons, joints, and bones get strong as hell together — and safely.</p> \n<p><strong>Plus, you get to master your body like a freaking Jedi.</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3616309\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/luke-handstand.gif\" alt=\"Luke rocks one arm handstand, but he also has the force. And yoda.\" width=\"540\" height=\"229\" /></p> \n<p>We know that <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-where-do-i-start/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">strength training</a> — with your bodyweight or with free weights — also happens to burn plenty of calories and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-building-muscle-and-strength/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">builds muscle</a> and strength. So it doesn’t matter if you’re male or female, young or old — bodyweight strength training can help you build a body that looks good and feels good. In fact, as you get older one of the best ways to feel young is to stay strong! Just ask our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2016/04/19/am-i-too-old-to-get-in-shape/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">older rebels</a>.</p> \n<p>Period. Exclamation point! Loud noises!</p> \n<h2><a name=\"where_bodyweight_exercises\"></a>Where Should I Perform Bodyweight Exercises</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-1310962 \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pullup_bar_forest.jpg\" alt=\"A pull-up bar in the forest, which means you can do bodyweight training here. \" width=\"858\" height=\"483\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pullup_bar_forest.jpg 2048w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pullup_bar_forest-300x169.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pullup_bar_forest-768x432.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pullup_bar_forest-713x401.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/pullup_bar_forest-160x90.jpg 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 858px) 100vw, 858px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Bodyweight training can be done ANYWHERE.</strong></p> \n<p>Read that sentence one more time. Crap, there goes that excuse for not exercising! You always have your body with you, which means you always have the ability to exercise, even if it’s just for a few reps here and there.</p> \n<p><strong>You can always improve yourself physically. Anytime. Anywhere. Whether you’re:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-stay-in-shape-while-traveling/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Traveling around the world</a></li> \n <li>Hunkered down in a bunker <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2011/01/17/how-to-survive-a-zombie-apocalypse/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">during the zombie apocalypse</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2011/03/10/angry-birds-workout-plan/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Stuck in a cubicle</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2010/12/20/the-20-minute-hotel-workout/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Living in a hotel</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2009/12/09/beginner-body-weight-workout-burn-fat-build-muscle/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Training in your living room</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2012/04/12/playground-workout/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Near a playground</a></li> \n <li>On Mars. Once Elon Musk sends me there.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Seriously, <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">right now</span> you can just drop down and do some (knee/wall) push-ups.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3671456\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/wall-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Push-ups like this can be done anywhere there is a wall.\" width=\"360\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>I’ll wait.</p> \n<p>You didn’t do them, did you?! You sandbaggin’ son of a biscuit… you SAILOR you.</p> \n<p>Even if you DIDN’T do them, you weren’t completely overwhelmed at the idea of doing a few reps!</p> \n<p><strong>My point is this:</strong> You don’t need access to a gym to get in great shape. You simply need to know a few moves — which we’ll teach you below — and you can train anywhere.</p> \n<h2><a name=\"progress_bodyweight_training\"></a>How to Progress with Bodyweight Training</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-1310945 \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Handstand.jpg\" alt=\"At Camp NF, people did handstands, like so.\" width=\"675\" height=\"450\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Handstand.jpg 800w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Handstand-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Handstand-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Handstand-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Camp_Handstand-160x107.jpg 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 675px) 100vw, 675px\" /></p> \n<p>Although bodyweight exercises are a bit tougher to visualize as a scalable activity compared to weight lifting (where you just put more weight on the bar), with just a little bit knowledge bodyweight training is like improving a particular skill tree in video games.</p> \n<p><strong>For example, in the push-up you might start on your knees:</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3746077\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/knee-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Rebel Leader Steve doing knee push-ups\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Or with your hands on an elevated surface:</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3746078\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/elevated-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Staci showing you an elevated push-up\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>Over time, by slowly adjusting the angle you are manipulating your bodyweight, you can effectively change the difficulty of an exercise to make it more challenging. With a tougher angle, you have to move a higher percentage of your bodyweight, and thus more strength is needed!</p> \n<p>I guarantee you can train with just your bodyweight for the next 20 years and you will not reach a “MAX LEVEL” screen.</p> \n<p><strong>Here’s what an oversimplified progression tree for the squat might look like:</strong></p> \n<p>#1) Assisted Bodyweight Squat</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3746069\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/assisted-bodyweight-squat.gif\" alt=\"Coach Staci showing you the an assisted bodyweight squat\" width=\"400\" height=\"225\" /></p> \n<p>#2) Bodyweight Squat</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3756889\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/steve-bodyweight-squat.gif\" alt=\"Rebel Leader Steve doing the bodyweight squat\" width=\"400\" height=\"225\" /></p> \n<p>#3) Assisted One Leg Squat</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3595104\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/assisted-one-legged-squat.gif\" alt=\"A small stool can help when you first start doing one legged squats!\" width=\"400\" height=\"225\" /></p> \n<p>#4) One Leg Squat</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3594768\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/pistol-squat.gif\" alt=\"The one legged &quot;pistol&quot; squat is a great advanced bodyweight movement.\" width=\"401\" height=\"226\" /></p> \n<p>Show me somebody that has advanced to the end of one or more&nbsp;bodyweight skill trees, and I’ll show you somebody that is in peak physical condition (and looks damn good too!).</p> \n<p>Once you learn the progressions, it’s just like adding points to a skill tree or leveling up a skill to unlock the next one in a video game. You start at the base exercise, get stronger and better, and then rank up when that movement becomes too easy. Gamification ftw.</p> \n<p>There’s always a new skill to work on, a new challenging variation, the next level in the skill you’re working on.</p> \n<h2><a name=\"build_muscle_bodyweight_workout\"></a>Can You Build Muscle With Only a Bodyweight Workout?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-1310833 \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Jim_Handstand.jpg\" alt=\"Coach Jim doing a handstand on stacked chairs. \" width=\"492\" height=\"656\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Jim_Handstand.jpg 720w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Jim_Handstand-225x300.jpg 225w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Jim_Handstand-450x600.jpg 450w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Jim_Handstand-120x160.jpg 120w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 492px) 100vw, 492px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Bodyweight training can help you build a great physique.&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p>If you’re like me (and the other 7.2 billion people on the planet), you might look at gymnasts or see what Coach Jim is doing in that photo above and say “holy crap I wish I had a body like that” or “dang, would be cool to do that, but not me.”</p> \n<p>If you happen to be somebody who is stockier or heavier, you might look at a bodyweight-training-Jedi and say “I can’t train like them, because I’m not built like them. <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-lose-weight-without-dieting-5-rules-of-weight-loss/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">I need to lose weight</a> first before trying to those things”</p> \n<p>You’ve got it backwards.</p> \n<p><strong>They look like they do precisely because they train like that!</strong></p> \n<p>In fact, we have TONS of success stories from people in our community, male and female who have transformed thanks to bodyweight training. Yours truly included!</p> \n<p><strong>Some people use the training to slim WAY down, others like me, use it to pack some muscle on (click on each photo for the story!):</strong></p> \n<p><img they can also do some pretty cool party tricks – like Jim doing one-arm handstands:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3836490\" doing handstands on stacked chairs anytime soon, or busting out one-handed handstands, but it’s amazing to know what our bodies are capable of when we train them with conviction and follow the right progressions!</p> \n<p>If you’re somebody who scrolls through Instagram far too often (like me!), use motivation properly and follow people that inspire you to be stronger, fitter, and better.</p> You look nice today, and those shoes go great with that shirt.</p> \n<p>But you might think you’re too overweight or too old or too [something] and that’s all nonsense. Hogwash. Poppycock. Balderdash.</p> \n<p>Here’s that 57-year-old gymnast again, who is in better shape than 99% of people 25 years younger:</p> \n<blockquote class=\"instagram-media\" style=\"background: #FFF; border: 0; Read the article, and watch the video below, featuring me about 30 pounds lighter and with helmet hair:</p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Beginner Body Weight Circuit Workout | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/qvhHhDNjtxM?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p>(Fun fact, this is our <em>most viewed video</em> on Youtube at 1,400,000 views, and my shorts are on backwards. Professionalism at its finest!)</p> \n<p>If you’re feeling particularly feisty, check out our&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/advanced-body-weight-workout-warning-this-will-kick-your-ass/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Advanced Bodyweight Workout</a> too:</p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Advanced Body Weight Circuit Workout | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/zZKysm4oAvU?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p>Whether you go through those workouts or not, I have a mission for you!</p> \n<p><strong>I want you to master these three moves:</strong></p> \n<p>#1) <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2011/02/15/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The Push-up</a></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3674909\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/steve-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Here Rebel Leader Steve shows you the classic push-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>#2) <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2014/03/03/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The Squat</a></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3584779\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NF-bodyweight-squat.gif\" alt=\"Do a proper bodyweight squat to work out your legs\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>#3) <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/2011/04/25/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The Pull-up</a></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585416\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/pull-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"The classic pull-up\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>or <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/inverted-row-are-you-missing-out-on-this-great-exercise/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Bodyweight Row</a>:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585387\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-bodyweight-row-1.gif\" alt=\"As you get lower, like this, the row will be harder to do. Great way to progress into a pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>If you can do a workout with 3 sets of 10 push-ups, 3 sets of 20 bodyweight squats, and 3 sets of 5 pull-ups, you will be in better shape than 95% of your peers.</p> \n<p>That should get you well on your way to becoming a badass version of you.</p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>Now the only thing left to do is start!</b></span></p> \n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-3802159 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/star-wars-light-speed.gif\" alt=\"&quot;Punch it,&quot; as Han would say.\" width=\"500\" height=\"271\" /></p> \n<p>If you want some help getting going…</p> \n<p><strong><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Here are some options for next steps with Nerd Fitness</span>:&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><b>Option #1)</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> If you want a professional coach in your pocket, who can do video form checks, provide feedback, and adjust your workouts based on the equipment you have available, check out our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Online Coaching Program</a>!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For example, let’s say you find yourself stuck indoors during a pandemic, and you want somebody to custom-build you a workout program based on the equipment and furniture you have. We'll find out!\" width=\"2048\" height=\"815\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-shop.jpg 2048w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-shop-300x119.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-shop-768x306.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-shop-713x284.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-shop-600x239.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2048px) 100vw, 2048px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Ugh, it’s time for yet another attempt at losing weight.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For some, losing weight is as simple as just </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">looking</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> at a vegetable.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For the rest of us mere mortals, it feels like running through quicksand.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3617397\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/quicksand.gif\" alt=\"For some, trying to lose weight is tougher than trying to escape quicksand.\" width=\"294\" height=\"233\" /></p> \n<p><b>Fortunately, helping people lose weight in a way that doesn’t suck is what we do!</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And gosh darnit, we’re really good at it: we have thousands of success stories and 1 million+ people tune in each month for advice on this stuff.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>We help our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Online Coaching Clients</a> lose weight without dieting, and these are the exact tactics we use.</b></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Want to lose weight WITHOUT hating life? Learn how we can help: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><b>I’m going to cover EVERYTHING you need to know about losing weight quickly, sustainably, and without hating everything. Click below for more help:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#diets_dont_work\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Why diets don’t
