work!</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#lose_weight_rule_1\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #1) Lose Weight Without Dieting.</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#lose_weight_rule_2\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #2) Prioritize Protein and Veggies.</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#lose_weight_rule_3\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #3) Know Your Carbs and Fats.</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#lose_weight_rule_4\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #4) Exercise for Weight Loss.</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#lose_weight_rule_5\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #5) Strength Training For Weight Loss.</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#25_tips_to_lose_weight\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">25 tips to supercharge your weight loss.</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#how_fast_lose_weight\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How fast can I lose weight?&nbsp;</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#lose_weight_quickly\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The best way to lose weight.</span></a></li> \n</ul> \n<h2><a name=\"diets_dont_work\"></a>Why Diets Don’t Work</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3617650\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-with-camera.jpg\" alt=\"This LEGO is super bummed that his weight will come back now that he stopped doing the Keto Diet for weight loss.\" width=\"1028\" height=\"520\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-with-camera.jpg 2048w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-with-camera-300x152.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-with-camera-768x389.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-with-camera-713x361.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-with-camera-600x304.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1028px) 100vw, 1028px\" /></p> \n<p><b>If you’re reading this guide, you probably:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Have gone on a diet in the past.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Are on a diet right now.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">From popular ideas like the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-paleo-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Paleo Diet</a> to <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-keto-diet-or-ketogenic-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Keto</a>, or <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-eat-a-plant-based-diet-a-scientific-look-at-going-vegan-safely/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Plant-Based</a> (no prob) to <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-intermittent-fasting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Intermittent fasting</a> (I do it), to terrible ideas like the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/does-the-military-diet-actually-work/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Military Diet</a>, juice cleanses, or the Cabbage Soup Diet, we’re all looking for that master key that unlocks effortless weight loss.</span></p> \n<p><b>Some of these diets are certainly more effective/healthy than others, but they all </b><b>come down to two truths for losing weight:</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Truth #1</span>: Nearly every diet works in the short term.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Truth #2</span>: Nearly every diet fails in the long term.</span></p> \n<p><b>So why does every diet work in the short term?&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3604380\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/pooh-thinking.gif\" alt=\"Pooh wants to lose weight, but isn't sure if a diet will help him in the long term.\" width=\"333\" height=\"180\" /></p> \n<p><b>Every diet you have ever tried has a clever way of restricting calories which leads to weight loss<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-1\" id=\"refmark-1\"><sup>[1]</sup></a>:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-paleo-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Paleo Diet</span></a>: Eliminate everything but veggies, meat, fruit, and nuts.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-keto-diet-or-ketogenic-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Keto Diet</span></a>: Remove an entire macronutrient from your diet (carbs).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-eat-a-plant-based-diet-a-scientific-look-at-going-vegan-safely/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Plant-based Diet</span></a>: Only eat vegetables and foods from plants.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/should-you-try-the-carnivore-diet-5-questions-addressed/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Carnivore Diet</span></a>: Only eat meat! Eliminate everything else.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-intermittent-fasting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Intermittent Fasting</a></span>: Skip an entire meal, or don’t eat for 24 hours.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>99% of the reason why these diets result in short term weight loss is that they get us to eat fewer calories.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>The problems arise when we get to Truth 2:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Nearly every diet fails in the long term.”</span></i></p> \n<p><b>Put another way: “</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Temporary changes create temporary results.”&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If somebody “goes Keto” for 60 days, they’ll probably lose weight, and might even feel healthier.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is cool.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">HOWEVER.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If they spend those 60 days dreaming of carbs, counting down the days until they can “go back to eating like normal,” they will put all of the weight back as soon as they stop their diet.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603657\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/luke-no.gif\" alt=\"The weight loss you obtain through diet will only stick as long as you stay on that diet.\" width=\"504\" height=\"284\" /></p> \n<p><b>This is why I hate the term “diet” or “going on a diet”: In order for a diet to create permanent results, the diet needs to be adopted PERMANENTLY!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You’ll achieve weight loss in the short term with pretty much any diet you pick, as long as it gets you to eat significantly fewer calories.</span></p> \n<p><b>However, today we’re going to focus on weight loss with </b><b>2 important conditions</b><b>:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Permanently:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> No more yo-yo dieting. No more rollercoaster on the bathroom scale.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Enjoyably:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> We’re not miserable and hating our lives while making these changes.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So, as you read about the 5 rules of weight loss below, I want you to be honest with yourself. You need to make changes you can stick with for at least a year.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If a change seems too drastic, or giving up a food seems too scary, make the “win scenario” smaller.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3617677\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/star-wars-good-idea.gif\" alt=\"Yep, small changes will help with sustainability, our goal in weight loss.\" width=\"376\" height=\"213\" /></p> \n<p><b>Here’s how we help our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">coaching clients</a>:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> we work with them to pick ONE change per week that we can implement: one less soda, try one new vegetable, etc.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In other words, we STOP thinking about “<em>How many pounds can I lose in a month?</em>” and instead “<em>What can I do today that isn’t scary, but will make me better off a year from now:</em>“</span></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Want to get in shape? Think in days and years, not weeks and months\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/ieY_8ZL0v78?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Dieting sucks. Let us help you fix your nutrition and lose weight without being miserable: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"lose_weight_rule_1\"></a>Rule #1: Lose Weight Without Dieting</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3617641\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1.jpg\" alt=\"Buddha isn't trying to lose weight. But he's also zen about you trying to.\" width=\"1030\" height=\"432\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1.jpg 2048w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-300x126.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-768x322.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-713x299.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-buddha-1-600x252.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1030px) 100vw, 1030px\" /></p> \n<p><b>There’s only ONE big-ass rule you need to follow when it comes to weight loss:</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Eat fewer calories than you burn.</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(Yes, I realize this article has 5 RULES, but the other 4 all build on this one.)</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Study<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-2\" id=\"refmark-2\"><sup>[2]</sup></a> after study<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-3\" id=\"refmark-3\"><sup>[3]</sup></a> after study<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-4\" id=\"refmark-4\"><sup>[4]</sup></a> shows that our bodies obey the laws of thermodynamics and that in order to lose weight, we need to burn more calories than we consume regularly.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3617690\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/science.gif\" alt=\"Yes, science is great, and the law of thermodynamics can help us understand weight loss.\" width=\"400\" height=\"166\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Every day, our body needs a certain number of calories to carry out its daily functions: making your heart beat, your brain function, getting your body to move, and all sorts of other stuff.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is called your total daily energy expenditure, and you can <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">calculate your TDEE here</a>.&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you </span><b>consume more calories than you burn</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, your body tends to store those extra calories as fat (weight gain).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you </span><b>burn more calories than you consume</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, your body will pull from fat stores for energy (weight loss).</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So, in order for us to lose weight, we need to find a way to tip the energy balance in favor of “burn fat, sucka!”</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618221\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/flame-thrower.gif\" alt=\"We need to tip the equation to burn fat, like we added a flame thrower to the scenario.\" width=\"319\" height=\"223\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Simplifying this really complex topic, we need to eat less and/or move more to get our bodies to start using our fat stores for energy.</span></p> \n<p><b>Unfortunately, that’s where the problems start.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>We humans are REALLY good at:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">UNDERestimating</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> how much </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">we eat</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">OVERestimating</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> how much </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">we burn</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When we accidentally eat more calories than we realize, and then burn fewer calories from exercise than we assume, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">we think we “can’t lose weight”</a> because of our metabolism or genetics.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Nope.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s because we are eating too much.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3617707\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/eagle-shocked.gif\" alt=\"This eagle doesn't want to believe he eats too much for weight loss.\" width=\"460\" height=\"198\" /></p> \n<p><b>And as we lay out in our MASSIVE <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/healthy-eating/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Healthy Eating Guide</a>, the most important factor in nutrition is eating fewer calories than you burn on a regular basis.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The best way to do that is to focus on the right kind of food:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Protein: meat and legumes.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fresh fruits and high fiber vegetables.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Healthy carbohydrates: rice, quinoa.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Healthy fats like almonds and olive oil.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Occasional cheese and dairy.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">These foods tend to be lower in calories than processed foods that have been designed to be overeaten<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-6\" id=\"refmark-6\"><sup>[6]</sup></a></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They fill us up but aren’t overly calorie-dense</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p> \n<p><b>Which means we feel full and yet consume fewer calories than we used to.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If we can do this consistently and sustainably, we will lose weight.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3617706\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/booyah.gif\" alt=\"Woot! A calorie deficit is a sure fire way to sustainable weight loss!\" width=\"390\" height=\"219\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">To drive the point home, here are two foods, both in 200 calorie increments (courtesy of </span><a href=\"https://www.wisegeek.com/what-does-200-calories-look-like.htm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">wiseGEEK</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">):</span></p> \n<p>200 calories worth of a <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">bagel</span>:</p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3611209 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/200-calories-of-bagel.png\" alt=\"This picture shows you 200 calories worth of a bagel, which is about 2/3 of one.\" width=\"515\" height=\"343\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/200-calories-of-bagel.png 780w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/200-calories-of-bagel-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/200-calories-of-bagel-768x511.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/200-calories-of-bagel-713x474.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/200-calories-of-bagel-600x399.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 515px) 100vw, 515px\" /></p> \n<p>…and 200 calories worth of <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">broccoli</span>:</p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3574949 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli.jpg\" alt=\"A pic of 200 calories of broccoli\" width=\"515\" height=\"343\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli.jpg 605w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 515px) 100vw, 515px\" /></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Which one do you think you’ll be more likely to accidentally overeat?&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The bagel, duh. Who eats only 2/3rds of a bagel? Literally zero people.</span></p> \n<p><b>So here’s how we’re going to lose weight: eat fewer calories without realizing it, and then burn extra calories without being miserable:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b>Prioritize protein and vegetables on your plate:<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> target 2 fist-sized servings of vegetables, and 1-2 palm-sized portions of protein on the plate.&nbsp;</span></b></li> \n <li><strong>Learn portion sizes of fat and carbs:</strong> <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you aren’t losing weight, these are the culprits. Cut back on the one you’re eating more of.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li><strong>Exercise for weight loss:</strong><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"> Strength training</a> is the most efficient way to lose fat. Strength train 3x per week, and then mix in fun cardio and move as much as possible.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let’s dig into these 3 things next:</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"lose_weight_rule_2\"></a>Rule #2: Prioritize Protein and Vegetables</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3616724\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png\" alt=\"If your meal plate looks like this, you're doing a lot of the heavy lifting for weight loss.\" width=\"720\" height=\"567\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png 720w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-300x236.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-713x561.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-600x473.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p> \n<p><b>If our plan is weight loss that doesn’t suck, we’re gonna build better meals full of foods that fill us up and make us feel good.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>PART A) PRIORITIZE PROTEIN FIRST</b><b>: Protein is fuel for our bodies to rebuild muscle. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s also delicious and nutritious and can satiate us with an efficient number of calories.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How much protein should you eat? As we cover in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-much-protein-do-i-need-to-eat-every-day-protein-101-guide/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Protein Guide</a>, aim for 1g per lb of bodyweight (2g per kg) every day (with an upper limit of 250g).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Protein can come from any number of sources, including:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Meat (steak, bison, pork).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fowl (chicken, turkey, duck).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Eggs!<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-7\" id=\"refmark-7\"><sup>[7]</sup></a></span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fish and shellfish (salmon, tuna, shrimp).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Legumes (black beans, chickpeas).</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not a meat-eater? </span></i><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-eat-a-plant-based-diet-a-scientific-look-at-going-vegan-safely/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">massive plant-based guide</a>!</span></i></p> \n<p><b>A serving of protein is about the size and thickness of your palm.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3610479 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-713x475.png\" alt=\"A serving of protein should be about the size of your palm, like so.\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-600x400.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>*The 4 oz serving is for an uncooked piece of meat. Cooking reduces about 25% of the weight, bringing it down to about 3 oz.</em></p> \n<p><b>When building a plate, aim for the following amount of protein:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dudes: 1-2 servings (6-8 oz or about 170-228 g): two palms</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dudettes: 1 serving (3-4 oz or about 85-114 g): 1 palm.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>PART B) HALF OF YOUR PLATE SHOULD BE VEGETABLES</b><b>: </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Veggies can be the difference between weight loss success and failure.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603421 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/dancing-broccoli.gif\" alt=\"Vegetables are the key to healthy eating.\" width=\"500\" height=\"261\" /></p> \n<p><b>Vegetables are nutrient-dense but calorie-light, which means you can eat lots of them, you’ll feel full, but you’re unlikely to over-consume calories </b>(<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">remember that mountain of broccoli was only 200 calories!)</span><b>.</b></p> \n<p><b>A serving of veggies is about the size of your fist, and 2 servings of veggies should take up ½ the plate!</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3606769 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-713x475.png\" alt=\"A serving of veggies should be the size of your first (or greater).\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-600x400.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Here’s a quick, non-complete list of veggies that can fill your plate:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Broccoli</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Broccolini</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cauliflower</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Spinach</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Kale</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Spaghetti squash<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-8\" id=\"refmark-8\"><sup>[8]</sup></a></span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Brussels sprouts</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Zucchini</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cucumber</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Carrots</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Onion</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Asparagus</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“But Steve, I don’t like vegetables…yet!”&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That’s cool, I didn’t eat vegetables until I was 22. Now, they’re a main staple of every meal I eat.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If this is you, read our guide on “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/vegetable-haters-how-to-start-eating-vegetables/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">how to make vegetables taste good</a>.”</span></i></p> \n<p><b>RECAP:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> In our quest for weight loss that doesn’t suck, we need to focus on foods that have lower amounts of calories but still make us feel full and satiated and happy. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Always start with protein and vegetables, and then the rest of your plate can have fats and carbs.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Speaking of which…</span></i></p> \n<h2><a name=\"lose_weight_rule_3\"></a>Rule #3: Know Your Carbs and Fat Portion Sizes.</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-13305\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/06/Lego-vs-Bread-Carbs.jpg\" alt=\"This LEGO knows that if you want to lose weight, you have to have portion control of your carbs.\" width=\"590\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/06/Lego-vs-Bread-Carbs.jpg 590w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/06/Lego-vs-Bread-Carbs-300x167.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 590px) 100vw, 590px\" /></p> \n<p><b>If 3/4ths of our healthy plate is occupied by protein and vegetables, where do fats and carbs fit in?&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can still lose weight by consuming fat and carbohydrates, </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">when consumed in the right quantities</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Remember how I said earlier “we <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">UNDERestimate</span> how many calories we eat every day?”&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fat and/or carbs are almost ALWAYS the culprit.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3577086\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/curious-batman.gif\" alt=\"Batman is curious on how carbs and fat factor into weight loss.\" width=\"322\" height=\"222\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let’s discuss.</span></p> \n<p><b>PART C) HEALTHY CARBOHYDRATES FOR THE WIN. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Everybody loves carbs, but most people overeat this macronutrient without realizing it.</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are some examples of healthy carbohydrates that are less likely to be overconsumed:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li>Fruit, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/is-fruit-healthy-for-you/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">fresh or frozen</a>.</li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rice, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/is-rice-healthy-for-me-does-white-vs-brown-rice-matter/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Brown or white.</a></span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Legumes, lentils.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Quinoa.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Potatoes.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Sweet potatoes.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yams.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whole grain bread.</span></li> \n <li>Whole grain pasta.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is a list of REAL foods, minimally processed, that also have plenty of fiber<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-9\" id=\"refmark-9\"><sup>[9]</sup></a>.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>This then puts them in the “healthy carbs” category:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> when consumed in proper proportion, these are great foods that can help you feel full and give you energy and all that jazz.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Just make sure you know your portion sizes! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">EVERYBODY accidentally overeats carbohydrate-heavy foods, even healthy ones, and then wonders </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">why they aren’t losing weight</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p> \n<p><b>To help you get better at eyeballing carb serving sizes:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3606899\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-713x475.png\" alt=\"Showing you a serving of carbs\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-600x400.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1 serving of a starchy carbohydrate is 1 cupped hand (uncooked), or two hands forming a cup (cooked).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are some images to help you learn proper portion sizes (thanks to <a href=\"https://www.safefood.eu/Healthy-Eating/Food,-Diet-and-Health/Eating-In/Serving-sizes.aspx\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">SafeFood</a>):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618226\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/carb-serving-size.png\" alt=\"This picture will help you determine proper serving sizes for carbs!\" width=\"468\" height=\"360\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/carb-serving-size.png 543w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/carb-serving-size-300x231.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 468px) 100vw, 468px\" /></p> \n<p><b>PART D) DON’T FORGET ABOUT FAT!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fat used to be vilified, but now it’s considered a superfood by many.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here’s the truth: fat is neither a superfood nor evil.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603668\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/dr-evil.gif\" alt=\"Fat can be part of a healthy diet, and is not evil, to the frustration of Dr. Evil.\" width=\"443\" height=\"188\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s just a macronutrient that we can eat that can help us lose weight when consumed in the right quantity, or keep us from our goals if we eat too many calories of it.</span></p> \n<p><b>Healthy fat can be found in foods like:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Avocado&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Almonds&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Walnuts</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Macadamia nuts</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Olive oil</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Almond butter&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Peanut butter</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Saturated fats – consumed in moderate quantities<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-10\" id=\"refmark-10\"><sup>[10]</sup></a> – can come from things like:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whole milk</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Full fat dairy</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Coconut oil</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grass-fed butter</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Lard</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fatty cuts of meat</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>To help you gauge: a serving size of fat is roughly the size of your thumb!</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3606783\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size-713x475.png\" alt=\"A serving of fat should be about your thumb!\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size-600x400.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>THIS is a single serving of almonds (162 calories):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603871\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-713x475.jpg\" alt=\"Knowing the correct amount of almonds to eat can help you with your calorie goals.\" width=\"476\" height=\"317\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds.jpg 960w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 476px) 100vw, 476px\" /></p> \n<p><b>THIS is a serving of olive oil (119 calories, taken from <a href=\"http://runtastic.com/blog/en/hand-portion-size/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Runtastic</a>):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3742707\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb.jpg\" alt=\"Your thumb is about one serving of olive oil\" width=\"566\" height=\"260\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb.jpg 995w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-300x138.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-768x353.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-713x327.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-600x276.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 566px) 100vw, 566px\" /></p> \n<p><b>What about cheese?</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Cheese is fine, provided you consume a proper sized portion of it!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is a portion of cheddar cheese (116 calories):</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3618059\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/serving-cheese.png\" alt=\"A serving of cheese is about the size of four dice\" width=\"481\" height=\"331\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/serving-cheese.png 481w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/serving-cheese-300x206.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 481px) 100vw, 481px\" /></p> \n<p><b>So bringing them all together, here’s the healthy plate for weight loss (from our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/healthy-eating/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Healthy Eating Guide</a>):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3616724\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png\" alt=\"If your meal plate looks like this, you're doing a lot of the heavy lifting for weight loss.\" width=\"720\" height=\"567\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png 720w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-300x236.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-713x561.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-600x473.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p> \n<p><b>If you can prioritize protein, fruit, and vegetables, and keep your carb and fat intake under control, you are going to lose weight.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b><i>“But Steve, what about low-fat diets? Low-carb diets? No-carb diets?”</i></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Low carb diets like <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-keto-diet-or-ketogenic-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Keto</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-paleo-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Paleo</a> are all the rage right now, but are they healthy and will they help you lose weight?&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3603654\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/maybe-1.gif\" alt=\"Will a low carb diet help you lose weight? Maybe!\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>Maybe!</p> \n<p>It depends on how your body regulates glucose (blood sugar)<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-11\" id=\"refmark-11\"><sup>[11]</sup></a>:</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Studies show that people who follow </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">EITHER</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> a low-fat </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">OR</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> a low-carb diet will lose weight, as long as they are in caloric restriction and can adhere to the diet for at least a year<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-12\" id=\"refmark-12\"><sup>[12]</sup></a>.</span></p> \n<p><strong><i>So, it comes down to: “which strategy are you more likely to stick with for a year or longer?”</i></strong></p> \n<p>If you think you can go Paleo or Keto or follow another low carb/low fat strategy for over a year, go for it.</p> \n<p>Otherwise, make small changes!</p> \n<p><b>MY ADVICE: Stick with changes that aren’t too scary. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Work on reducing portion sizes or adding a new vegetable each week, and don’t get dogmatic, all-or-nothing about your diet!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you can find a way to reduce your total calorie intake without being miserable, you WILL lose weight over time, AND keep it off.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There’s one other piece of the puzzle I HAVE to address. </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"lose_weight_rule_4\"></a>Rule #4: Exercise for weight loss (Strength training and cardio)</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3617651\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-doing-cardio-for-weight-loss.jpg\" alt=\"For exercises, the important thing is you enjoy it. Like this LEGO enjoys football.\" width=\"1028\" height=\"613\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-doing-cardio-for-weight-loss.jpg 2028w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-doing-cardio-for-weight-loss-300x179.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-doing-cardio-for-weight-loss-768x458.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-doing-cardio-for-weight-loss-713x425.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-doing-cardio-for-weight-loss-600x358.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1028px) 100vw, 1028px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Although exercise isn’t necessary for weight loss (nutrition being the most important part), I would HIGHLY recommend you exercise.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There are three forms of exercise that I’ll cover when it comes to weight loss, and ALL three of them are important:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/25-ways-to-exercise-without-realizing-it/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Fun cardio</a></span>: movement of any kind that gets your heart pumping (good).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/3-hiit-workouts-for-beginners-how-to-start-interval-training/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Interval training</a></span>: variable rate training: “run, jog, run, jog” (better).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Strength training</span></a>: challenging your muscles to get stronger (best).&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>#1) Fun cardio is doing any sort of exercise that gets you off your butt and moving.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3520134 \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Carlton.gif\" alt=\"Carlton knows any kind of movement is beneficial for weight loss, including his signature dance!\" width=\"320\" height=\"241\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It makes our heart healthier, AND it can serve as a reminder that we’re doing things differently now, and that we need to eat better so we don’t ruin our efforts!</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(Whatever you do, DON’T say: “Welp, I exercised – and thus I earned this donut and Coca-Cola” – you’d have been better off NOT exercising and skipping the donut and Coca-cola).</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here are <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/25-ways-to-exercise-without-realizing-it/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">40 fun ways to exercise without realizing it</a>. Feel free to do a fun activity as often as you can!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>#2) High-Intensity Interval Training (HIIT) <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/what-burns-more-calories-cardio-intervals-or-weight-training/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">burns more calories per hour than steady cardio</a>,</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> so you get more “bang for your buck” when it comes to efficiency.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re limited on time and trying to burn more calories, 20 minutes of HIIT burns more calories than 20 minutes of steady jogging.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here are <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/3-hiit-workouts-for-beginners-how-to-start-interval-training/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">3 HIIT workouts</a> you can do today, no gym required!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3588327\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/captain-marvel.gif\" alt=\"Captain Marvel is pumped she doesn't have to head to the gym to do a HIIT workout.\" width=\"480\" height=\"198\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Both of these activities can help tip the energy balance in favor of “weight loss” when combined with calorie restriction.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you’re in a “caloric deficit” for weight loss,</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;the hope is that your body will mostly pull from fat stores, though depending on how you are exercising it will also break down muscle too.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-13\" id=\"refmark-13\"><sup>[13]</sup></a></span></p> \n<p><b>Said again: when you are eating a <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">caloric deficit</span>, your body will pull from both its <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">fat stores</span> AND <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">existing muscle</span> for energy.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3611092\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/surprised-monkey.gif\" alt=\"Yes, if you're not careful you can lose fat AND muscle while losing weight.\" width=\"320\" height=\"218\" /></p> \n<p><b>From a physique and health standpoint, obviously we’d prefer that we don’t break down muscle when in a caloric deficit, and instead get our body to use ONLY fat stores.<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-14\" id=\"refmark-14\"><sup>[14]</sup></a></span></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your goal in fitness shouldn’t only be “weight loss,” despite the common vernacular used.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The goal instead is to <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/body-fat-percentage/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">reduce body fat</a> while also keeping the muscle you have (or even <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-building-muscle-and-strength/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">building more muscle</a>).</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Which brings me to the most important form of exercise for weight loss:</span></i></p> \n<h2><a name=\"lose_weight_rule_5\"></a>Rule #5: Strength Training For Weight Loss</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3569206\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/batman-strength-training.jpg\" alt=\"Of course Batman Strength Trains. Fighting crime is tough work.\" width=\"1027\" height=\"576\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/batman-strength-training.jpg 1024w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/batman-strength-training-300x168.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/batman-strength-training-768x431.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/batman-strength-training-713x400.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/batman-strength-training-600x337.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1027px) 100vw, 1027px\" /></p> \n<p><b>#3) </b><b>Strength training is the prizefighting champion</b><b> when it comes to weight loss.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can find study<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-15\" id=\"refmark-15\"><sup>[15]</sup></a> </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">after study<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-16\" id=\"refmark-16\"><sup>[16]</sup></a> </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">after study<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-17\" id=\"refmark-17\"><sup>[17]</sup></a>&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">that shows you the benefits of strength training for weight management when combined with “calorie restriction.”</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let me explain it here quickly, borrowing from Harry Potter:</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(You know, the wizard.)</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">At the Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry, when each student arrives they put on the “Sorting Hat,” an actual hat that determines which House (group) that child will join for his/her time at Hogwarts.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The hat acts like a traffic director:</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Harry, you will go to Gryffindor! Draco, you will go to Slytherin!”</span></i></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3569208\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/gryffindor-2.gif\" alt=\"Your body is a lot like the Sorting Hat.\" width=\"444\" height=\"180\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your body operates in a VERY similar fashion: every day, it receives new calories (when you eat), and it needs to decide what to do with them!</span></p> \n<p><b>It’ll sort those calories into one of three Houses:</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A: Burn for Fuel.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">B: Rebuild Muscle.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">C: Store as Fat.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There’s a number of calories your body burns each day just existing: to keep your liver functioning, your heart pumping, your brain operating, and so on – it burns a good chunk of calories just keeping the lights on.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3595570\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/heart-pumping.gif\" alt=\"A beating heart requires calories, which factors into your calorie needs.\" width=\"351\" height=\"230\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Here are two quick examples (from our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">TDEE calculator</a>!):</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A 6’, 34-year old male weighing 250 pounds burns 2,300 calories a day just by existing.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A 5’5”, 40-year old female weighing 140 pounds burns 1,350 calories a day just by existing.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>When you start strength training, actual wizardry starts to happen.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you do <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">push-ups</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">pull-ups</a> or do a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-where-do-i-start/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">strength training workout</a>, your muscles are “broken down” during the exercise itself, and then they rebuild themselves stronger over the next 24-48 hours.</span></p> \n<p><b>Guess what happens during those 24-48 hours?</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your body diverts as many calories as possible to “Rebuild Muscle!”</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It also diverts additional calories to “Burn as Fuel” to handle this increased “muscle rebuilding” activity.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Which means two amazing things:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rebuilding muscle is a calorie taxing activity!</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your metabolism is revved up for this period of time, burning more calories than normal.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There are significantly fewer calories available for “Store as Fat.”</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">AND THEN IT GETS BETTER.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618110\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/go-on-gif.gif\" alt=\"This man wants to know more about strength training for weight loss.\" width=\"395\" height=\"217\" /></p> \n<p><strong>When you consume fewer calories than your body burns each day, strength training will cause your body to get even more efficient.&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your body can pull from “Store as Fat” to make sure all the work still gets done, including your daily functions as a human, and rebuilding the muscle.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is the Tri-wizard cup<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-18\" id=\"refmark-18\"><sup>[18]</sup></a></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;of physical transformation victory:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You get stronger and keep the muscle you have.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You burn through the fat you’re trying to get rid of.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You’re <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/lose-weight-and-build-muscle-or-do-one-then-the-other/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">decreasing your body fat percent and keeping your muscle</a> = look good naked.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This would be a “win-win-win” according to Michael Scott, Regional Manager, Dunder Mifflin Scranton.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So NO, you don’t need to lose weight first before you start strength training.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You will lose weight BY strength training (and keep the muscle you have).</span></p> \n<p><b>Here’s how to start with Strength Training:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>No gym? </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Try our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/beginner-body-weight-workout-burn-fat-build-muscle/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">20-minute Beginner Bodyweight Workout Routine</a>.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>Pick one</strong> of our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-where-do-i-start/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">5 Beginner Strength Training Workouts</a>.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>Gym newbie?</strong> Try our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">6-level Gym Strength Training Routine</a>.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>BRINGING IT ALL TOGETHER: </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Doing a strength training workout 3 times per week is the most efficient way to lose the right kind of weight and look better naked.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3615505\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/gonzo-chicken.gif\" alt=\"Gonzo knows strength training will help him lose weight. That's why he recruited his chicken pal!\" width=\"300\" height=\"300\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Adding in intervals or fun exercise on your off days is a fantastic supplemental activity to strength training.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Want help learning how to strength train? </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can absolutely <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">build your own workout</a>, or you can work with </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">one of our coaches</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> who can create a custom program that’s specific to your goals and lifestyle.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’ll even make sure you’re doing the movements correctly via video, because we’re nice like that 🙂</span></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3602791\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d2.jpg\" alt=\"Nerd Fitness Coaching Banner\" width=\"1311\" height=\"401\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d2.jpg 1311w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d2-300x92.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d2-768x235.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d2-713x218.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d2-600x184.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1311px) 100vw, 1311px\" /></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Start strength training safely with our Coaching program! Learn more: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"25_tips_to_lose_weight\"></a>25 Tips to Supercharge Weight Loss</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3569210\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/lego-winner.jpg\" alt=\"This LEGO knows if he follows the tips in this article, he'll gain weight successfully.\" width=\"1028\" height=\"578\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/lego-winner.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/lego-winner-300x169.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/lego-winner-713x401.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/lego-winner-600x338.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1028px) 100vw, 1028px\" /></p> \n<p><b>The 5 Rules Above give you the best chance to lose weight in a way that doesn’t suck.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>Changing your nutrition is like playing a video game:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> if you attack too many high-level bad guys at once, you’re going to lose.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618123\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/game-over.gif\" alt=\"Making too many changes at once is a sure fire way to lose momentum in weight loss.\" width=\"387\" height=\"332\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Instead, you’re better off picking 1-2 smaller bad guys (changes) that you know you can win, and level up slowly.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">THAT’S how you make changes that stick.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">No more <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">temporary</span> dieting for <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">temporary</span> results!&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Permanent changes</span> create <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">permanent results</span>.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are 25 other quick tips that are supplementary to the above important ones!</b></p> \n<p><b>1) Consider low-carb OR low-fat diets. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Studies show BOTH low-carb and low-fat diets will result in weight loss, IF you can stick with it.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-19\" id=\"refmark-19\"><sup>[19]</sup></a> </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Many people tend to have more success faster on low carb, but they’re also more likely to abandon the diet. You don’t need to do <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-keto-diet-or-ketogenic-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Keto</a> or <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-paleo-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Paleo</a> if you don’t want to, and instead, just work on reducing carbs overall.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3618228\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/kimmy-word-up.gif\" alt=\"Kimmy is relieved she doesn't have to do strict Keto for weight loss.\" width=\"245\" height=\"245\" /></p> \n<p><b>2) Consider intermittent fasting. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fasting helps you keep your caloric intake under control by eliminating or narrowing your eating window&nbsp; – it simply means skipping a meal or occasionally doing 24-hour fasts. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It affects men and women differently, but has tons of benefits and is backed by science. Read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-intermittent-fasting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Guide on Intermittent Fasting</a>. I’ve been skipping breakfast since 2014!</span></p> \n<p><b>3) Minimize liquid calories. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Beverages with calories in them are probably sabotaging your weight loss efforts. </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618336\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/super-troopers.gif\" alt=\"It should go without saying that chugging maple syrup will not help with weight loss.\" width=\"405\" height=\"213\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cut out the sodas and lattes and high-calorie smoothies (unless you account for them in your calorie goal!). Stick to sparkling water, black coffee or tea, or other zero-calorie beverages.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>4) Cut back on alcohol. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yes, you can still drink alcohol and lose weight, but you still need to account for the calories, of which there might be many! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And if you make poor food choices while drunk, it’s going to be tough to lose weight. Read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/alcohol/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">guide on alcohol</a> and stick to low calorie beer, whiskey neat, or vodka with club sodas.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618130\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/dog-alcohol.gif\" alt=\"This dog uses plain soda water as his mixer for weight loss.\" width=\"412\" height=\"308\" /></p> \n<p><b>5) Know your condiments and cooking oils. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Just because you’re eating grilled chicken and vegetables doesn’t mean you’re guaranteed to lose weight! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If those foods are smothered in sauces or covered in 1000 calories of healthy olive oil, the calories still count! Keep an eye on the sauces and oils you use to cook with.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>6) Know your next meal. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Most of our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">coaching success stories</a> plan in advance what their next meal is. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Because it’s a pre-made decision, it removes emotion and makes them less likely to make a bad choice while hungry, sad, or angry. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Think of it this way: you can still eat unhealthy foods with this strategy because you plan ahead and can eat a healthy meal before and after. No harm done!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Want help implementing these tactics to lose weight? Learn more about our Online Coaching: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><b>7) Look at restaurant menus before going. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Restaurants give out notoriously large portions of food, often with hundreds of hidden calories. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Give yourself the best chance to succeed by looking up the menu online before going and decide BEFORE you get there. </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618315\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/researching.gif\" alt=\"Do yourself a favor and look at the menu BEFORE you arrive if you're trying to lose weight.\" width=\"292\" height=\"218\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Also, consider taking HALF the entree and boxing it up for an additional meal (A tip we mention in our <em><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-portion-control-how-to-lose-weight-with-portion-control/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Guide to Portion Control</a></em>).</span></p> \n<p><b>8) Eat the same foods over and over. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The healthiest, most successful <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">coaching clients</a> we have tend to eat the same handful of meals over and over. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you learn <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-portion-control-how-to-lose-weight-with-portion-control/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">portion sizes</a> and calorie counts of your favorite meals, you’re much more likely to eat within your goals for the day.</span></p> \n<p><b>9) Learn to batch cook. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-step-by-step-guide-to-meal-planning-and-prep/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">guide on batch cooking</a>! If you can prepare all your healthy meals ONCE at the beginning of the week, you are setting yourself up for success. </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3558839\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/chef_gif-1.gif\" alt=\"Once you get good at batch cooking you'll feel like the Swedish Chef.\" width=\"500\" height=\"200\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Why? Because now your default, easiest, laziest option is to simply reheat and eat the food you have at home – much less work than ordering takeout or driving to fast food! Win-Win-Win. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here’s how I <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/super-simple-batch-cooked-chicken-for-lazy-people/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">batch cook chicken for the week</a>:</span></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Super Simple Chicken For Lazy People | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/oX-wTkhvRjE?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>10) Employ the “Never 2 in a Row” rule. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you ever eat an unhealthy meal, simply make the next one healthy. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">One bad meal doesn’t ruin a day, so letting an unhealthy breakfast derail you for the rest of the day isn’t smart.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Simply eat a healthy lunch and get right back on track.</span></p> \n<p><b>11) Ask “What would Batman do?”</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> If you’re not sure what you should eat, ask what would Batman do. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A study showed that children were more likely to pick an apple instead of candy when instructed to ask this question.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-20\" id=\"refmark-20\"><sup>[20]</sup></a> </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3595569\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/batman.gif\" alt=\"Batman is stoked kids want to eat apples instead of junk food.\" width=\"326\" height=\"274\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And we’re all kids at heart, right?</span></p> \n<p><b>12) Track your calories. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">If you can’t lose weight</a>, it’s most likely because you’re accidentally eating more calories than you realize. Use an app or spreadsheet and track your food for a week. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I bet your intake is 20-40% higher than you realize! You can <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">calculate how many calories you burn every day</a> too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>13) Weigh your food (advanced): </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">STILL not losing weight? It’s time to get your portion sizes fixed too. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Get <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2SVTNGs\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">a cheap food scale</a> and weigh your food for 2-3 days. Doing this, I discovered <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/losing-the-last-20-pounds-7-lessons-learned-while-still-eating-carbs/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">I was eating an extra 400 calories</a> without realizing it.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Struggling to lose weight? Let us help. Learn more about our Online Coaching: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><b>14) Eat more slowly! </b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3611175\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/turtle-eating.gif\" alt=\"Like this turtle, try to eat slow for a weight loss strategy.\" width=\"450\" height=\"253\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If we’re not careful, we can eat more than we realize because we eat too quickly for our body to understand it’s full! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Tactics to help with this include consciously working on chewing your food more frequently before swallowing. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Studies show eating slowly led to decreases in energy intake within meals in healthy women.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-21\" id=\"refmark-21\"><sup>[21]</sup></a></span></p> \n<p><b>15) Use smaller plates and forks!</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> If we have big plates and big utensils, we’re more likely to pile more food on our plate AND consume it more quickly. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Throw out your big plates and get smaller ones. Get smaller utensils, and you’ll trick yourself into eating smaller portions without realizing it.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-22\" id=\"refmark-22\"><sup>[22]</sup></a></span></p> \n<p><b>16) Don’t “Eat AND [activity].” Just “eat.” </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We eat more food if we’re eating while doing something else (watching TV, scrolling through our phones, etc.).<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-23\" id=\"refmark-23\"><sup>[23]</sup></a> </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Why don’t you try JUST eating? Enjoy each bite. Savor the food. Make it an experience. You’ll tend to eat less.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618145\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/arnold-eating.gif\" alt=\"Arnold knows not to watch TV and eat for weight loss.\" width=\"347\" height=\"260\" /></p> \n<p><b>17) <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/snacking/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Stop snacking</a>.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> All calories count. Instead of snacking throughout the day, why not eat 3 regular sized meals that you truly enjoy? </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As we cover in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-intermittent-fasting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Guide to Intermittent Fasting</a>, it doesn’t matter WHEN&nbsp; you eat, it only matters HOW MUCH you eat. Not snacking between meals gives you more leeway during your </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">actual </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">meals!</span></p> \n<p><b>18) Seek professional help!</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> If you have an emotional relationship with food, consider speaking about it with a therapist or doctor. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We believe <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-nerds-introduction-to-mental-health/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">mental health is really important here at Nerd Fitness</a>, and we know food can be an emotional trigger for lots of people that struggle with their weight. You don’t have to do this journey alone!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>19) Fidget more! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">From tapping your toes to getting up frequently, fidgeting (small micromovements) can account for up to 350 additional calories burned per day.<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3661#footnote-24\" id=\"refmark-24\"><sup>[24]</sup></a> It all counts. So get wiggling!&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>20) Move more. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">From parking farther away at the grocery store to taking the stairs instead of the elevator, do whatever you can to MOVE MORE! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Get <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2T2xIpJ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">a cheap fitness tracker</a> and try to get more steps than you normally do. </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3596493\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/portlandia-fitbit.gif\" alt=\"Our Fitbit trackers can help us with analyzing trends and getting in more steps. \" width=\"419\" height=\"236\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Don’t rely on the tracker for calories burned (they’re all notoriously inaccurate), but it’s a great ‘trend tracker.’ Do more than you did before and you WILL get results.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>21) Find ways to exercise in a fun way! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">ANY sort of movement helps, so check out our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/25-ways-to-exercise-without-realizing-it/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">40 ways to exercise without realizing it</a>. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dance, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-nerds-guide-to-yoga-4-movements-to-try-today/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">yoga</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-exercise-with-your-kids-work-out-as-a-family/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">wrestling with your kids</a>, rock climbing, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/hiking/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">hiking</a>, it all counts! Just like your parents told you when you were a kid, “Go outside and play!”</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Exercise doesn’t have to suck.
