Let us build a workout you’ll ACTUALLY do: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><b>22) Get strong as hell.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-where-do-i-start/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"> Pick up heavy weights</a>. </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3581841\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/04/muppet-strength-training.gif\" alt=\"This Muppet knows strength training will help him gain muscle and lose fat.\" width=\"377\" height=\"212\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our bodies have to burn tons of calories to recover from a heavy strength training session. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Plus, you get to keep the muscle you have and burn the fat on top of those muscles. That’s how you <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/lose-weight-and-build-muscle-or-do-one-then-the-other/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">lose weight AND gain muscle at the same time</a>!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>23) Hack your Batcave: </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We are <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-a-batcave-for-habit-change/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">creatures of our environment</a>, so use that to your advantage! <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/willpower/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Stop relying on willpower</a>, and instead get smarter. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Increase the steps between you and the activity you’re trying to avoid (eat junk food), and decrease the number of steps between you and the NEW activity you want to do more of (eat healthy):</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Throw out your junk food so you don’t need to waste willpower not eating it.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Put a bowl of fruit on the counter so your default activity becomes “eat fruit!”</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>24) Surround yourself with <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/support-team/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">people who are healthier than you</a>.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> We’re the average of the 5 people we associate most with. </span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3618146\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/looking-at-each-other.gif\" alt=\"Two people just realizing they are the average of the 5 people they spend the most time with.\" width=\"319\" height=\"176\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Join a running club. Eat lunch with healthier people than you at the office. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We subconsciously adopt the traits of the people around us, so use that to your advantage!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>25) Forgive yourself. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/you-are-flawed-and-so-are-your-heroes/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">We are all flawed</a>. If you eat a bad meal or have a rough weekend, who cares?! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The month is not ruined. Make the next decision a healthy one and get right back on track. Remember “never two in a row.”&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>I know this is a lot to absorb, so don’t beat yourself up if you’re totally overwhelmed!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p>If you want help implementing these tactics and supercharge your weight loss journey, that’s what we do best<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Click below to learn more!</span></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-2945420 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/coach-ad-8-713x296.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"713\" height=\"296\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/coach-ad-8-713x296.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/coach-ad-8-300x124.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/coach-ad-8-768x319.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/coach-ad-8-600x249.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/coach-ad-8.png 1429w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Losing weight doesn’t need to suck. Let us help you on your journey! Learn more: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"how_fast_lose_weight\"></a>How fast can I lose weight?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3617656\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-football-1.jpg\" alt=\"Now you know that any kind of movement is beneficial for weight loss, including tossing a football.\" width=\"1027\" height=\"480\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-football-1.jpg 2047w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-football-1-300x140.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-football-1-768x359.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-football-1-713x333.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/lego-football-1-600x281.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1027px) 100vw, 1027px\" /></p> \n<p><b>There are MANY factors that are involved in <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/just-how-fast-can-i-get-the-body-i-want/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">how quickly you can lose weight</a>, but here are the big ones:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b>How much weight do you need to lose? </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Somebody who needs to lose 250 pounds will be able to lose more weight than somebody who needs to lose 10 pounds, simply because there is more weight to lose.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li><b>How big of a caloric deficit <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">below your TDEE</a> are you doing? <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If somebody normally eats 5000 calories per day and switches to 1500 calories per day, they’ll lose weight faster than if they switched to 4500 calories per day. Now, reducing calories significantly can create all sorts of “I’m miserable and hate everything” feelings as our body learns to stop expecting a ready supply of food and has to start burning fat instead.&nbsp;</span></b></li> \n <li><strong>Are you going <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-paleo-diet-vs-keto-diet-3-lessons-learned/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">low-carb like Paleo or Keto</a>?</strong> <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As you’ll see below, cutting out carbs can create significant weight loss in the first weeks due to a reduction of&nbsp; ‘water weight and bloat.’ But cutting out carbs might also make you miserable!&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>First Week Weight Loss Expectations: </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Depending on how poorly you eat now, if you swap out unhealthy food for protein and veggies – reducing your calorie intake significantly – you might lose upwards of 5-10 pounds (5kg) in your first week.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3601574\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/the-tick.gif\" alt=\"The Tick is stoked you are having losing weight your first week.\" width=\"302\" height=\"237\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s awesome to see the scale drop by that much in the first week, but it’s important to note that this type of weight loss won’t be typical week to week.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you normally eat a lot of carbs and sodium, your body is carrying a lot of extra bloat and water weight. When you switch to mostly protein and veggies, you’ll lose TONS of water weight and some fat initially.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’ve seen many <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Coaching Clients</a> lose 5-10 pounds in their first week, again mostly due to the reduction of water weight with <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">SOME</span> fat loss.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>First Month Weight Loss Expectations:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Depending on how strict you are with your nutrition – you can lose 1% of your body fat, or 1-3 pounds per week after that (heavily dependent on how much weight you have to lose).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We have seen people (who have a lot of weight to lose) lose 20 pounds in their first month, mostly due to large water weight reduction in the first week, with a steady consistent drop after that.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(Curious how quickly you can lose weight? Use our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Total Daily Energy Expenditure TDEE Calculator</a>.)&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There’s nothing wrong with losing weight quickly, provided you’re doing it in a healthy, SUSTAINABLE way – like following the rules and strategies laid out in this article.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><strong>Quick weight loss doesn’t guarantee long term success.&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It comes down to making PERMANENT changes! </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If somebody reduces their calorie intake by 1000+ calories a day, they might be so damn hungry and angry all the time that they abandon their journey after a week or two. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is bad news bears.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3618147\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/bad-news.gif\" alt=\"Malcolm just realized temporary changes create temporary results. \" width=\"345\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They would have been better off reducing their calories by 200 calories a day for 6 weeks, and then by another 200 6 weeks later, and so on.</span></p> \n<p><b>We want sustainable changes, and sustainable weight loss, creating permanent progress.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So it doesn’t really matter how much weight you lose in your first week or first month, but rather how much weight you have lost after 1 year, and how you feel after that year.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As we cover in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">“Why can’t I lose weight?” guide</a>, this is a lifelong journey, and one you should be thinking about as a lifestyle adjustment and not a temporary diet change.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Put your focus on building the habits and fixing your environment. Focus on the changes you can make on a day to day basis, and with each meal.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And over time, your weight WILL drop in a way that’s sustainable and healthy. &nbsp; </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"lose_weight_quickly\"></a>How to Lose Weight Quickly</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3617658\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/running-beach-1.jpg\" alt=\"Move wherever, even on the beach, it'll help you lose weight.\" width=\"1024\" height=\"344\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/running-beach-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/running-beach-1-300x101.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/running-beach-1-768x258.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/running-beach-1-713x240.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/running-beach-1-600x202.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></p> \n<p><b><i>“STEVE JUST TELL ME EXACTLY WHAT TO DO TO LOSE WEIGHT QUICKLY.”</i></b></p> \n<p><b>Fine! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But you don’t need to yell at me like that!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Here’s what I would do if I needed to lose weight quickly but ALSO didn’t want to hate life:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Focus MOST of my effort on <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/healthy-eating/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">building a healthy plate</a>.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cut out all <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/snacking/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">snacks between meals</a>. Focus on making better meals.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cut way back on booze and only drink zero-calorie beverages (black coffee, sparkling water).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Learn to <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/vegetable-haters-how-to-start-eating-vegetables/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">cook a veggie</a> or two and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/protein-shakes-for-newbies-what-to-buy-when-to-drink/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">prioritize protein</a>.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Strength train</a> 3 days per week, probably following <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">THIS gym routine</a>.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/25-ways-to-exercise-without-realizing-it/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Move as much as possible</a>, tracking my steps with a Fitbit.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">If the scale doesn’t go down</a>, start tracking calories and measuring food.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>I’ll leave you with some final words of wisdom: this is NOT all or nothing. </b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you can implement just ONE change and stick with it, that’s a victory. That’s better than doing 10 things and giving up after a month.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I realize I threw a LOT of information at you, but I hope you can implement this stuff in your day-to-day decisions, because these rules WILL change the scale, and they WILL change your life.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>If you are looking for more guidance, support, and instruction, we have 3 options for you to level up:</b></p> \n<p><b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">#1) JOIN OUR COACHING PROGRAM</span>:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> We provide nutritional guidance, constant feedback and support, customized workouts for your goals, and keep you accountable wherever you are.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We are really good at this stuff and would love to help you reach your goals. </span></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"><img class=\"size-full wp-image-3379893 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/coaching.png\" alt=\"Our coaching program helps people start losing weight\" width=\"512\" height=\"154\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/coaching.png 512w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/coaching-300x90.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 512px) 100vw, 512px\" /></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Our Coaching program changes lives. better at push-ups.</span></a></li> \n</ul> \n<p>Let’s jump right in!</p> \n<p><span id=\"more-8109\"></span></p> \n<h2><b><a name=\"push_up_set_up\"></a>How to Set up for a Proper Push-up (Staging)</b></h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3583871 size-large\" title=\"Screen shot 2011-02-15 at 11.37.34 PM\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-front-713x409.png\" alt=\"Steve is setting up a proper push-up in this photo.\" width=\"713\" height=\"409\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-front-713x409.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-front-300x172.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-front-768x441.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-front-600x345.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-front.png 949w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>When it comes to push-ups, your form is crucial.</strong>&nbsp;Each push-up needs to be done with proper form so that your total reps measured from workout to workout are on equal footing.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3583748\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/push-up.gif\" alt=\"This gif shows Staci doing a push-up in perfect form.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p>If you did 20 push-ups two days ago, and then today you did 25 push-ups by only going down halfway, sticking your ass up in the air, etc., it’s absolutely impossible to tell if you got any stronger.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3583873 size-full\" title=\"Screen shot 2011-02-15 at 11.36.38 PM\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-side.png\" alt=\"Another angle of showing how to setup a proper push-up.\" width=\"687\" height=\"352\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-side.png 687w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-side-300x154.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-side-600x307.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 687px) 100vw, 687px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Here’s how to get into proper push-up position:</b></p> \n<p><strong>1) On the ground, set your hands at a distance that is slightly wider than shoulder-width apart.&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p>Draw a straight line from your chest/nipple down to the floor – it should be directly over your thumbnail.</p> \n<p>Depending on your strength and experience, your hands should be angled in a way that feels comfortable to you. For me, my hands are set up so that my middle finger points straight up and away from me.</p> \n<p><strong>2) To alleviate wrist pain</strong> (if you have <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-improve-your-wrist-mobility-and-grip-strength/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">poor wrist flexibility</a>) do your push-ups holding onto push-up handles (so your wrists aren’t as compromised), or a bar:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3746078\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/elevated-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Staci showing you an elevated push-up\" width=\"451\" height=\"254\" /></p> \n<p>If you’re hardcore, you can do them on your knuckles (as long as you’re on a semi-soft surface like grass or carpet<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;or broken glass. Wait, scratch that last one</span>).</p> \n<p><strong>3) Your feet should be set up in a way that feels right and comfortable and in balance.</strong> For some, that might be shoulder-width apart.</p> \n<p>For others, it might be with your feet touching. Generally speaking, the wider apart your feet, the more stable you’ll be for your push-ups.</p> \n<p><strong>4) Think of your body as one giant straight line&nbsp;</strong>– from the top of your head down through your heels. Your butt shouldn’t be sticking way up in the air or sagging.&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You’re essentially holding a plank throughout the entire movement.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3674909\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/steve-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Here Rebel Leader Steve shows you the classic push-up.\" width=\"459\" height=\"258\" /></p> \n<p><strong>5) If you have a problem getting the proper form with your body, try this:&nbsp;</strong>clench your butt, and then tighten your abs as if you’re bracing to get punched.</p> \n<p>Your core will be engaged, and your body should be in that straight line. If you’ve been doing push-ups incorrectly, this might be a big change for you.</p> \n<p>Record a video of yourself to make sure you’re doing it correctly.</p> \n<p><strong>6) Your head should be looking slightly ahead of you, not straight down.</strong></p> \n<p>I read somewhere that said “if you’re doing them right, your chin should be the first part of your head to touch the floor, not your nose.”</p> \n<p>Looking up helps you keep your body in line, but feel free to look down if that helps you concentrate more.</p> \n<p><strong>7) At the top of your push-up, your arms should be straight and supporting your weight.</strong>&nbsp;You’re now ready to do a push-up.</p> \n<p><b>8) I want to draw special attention to that first step with hand position: </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">nearly EVERYBODY does push-ups with their arms out far too wide and their shoulders flared. This is bad news bears.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><strong>If I was looking down at you from above, your arms and body should form an ARROW, not a T.</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3652754\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey.png\" alt=\"As you can see, you want your arms to be like an arrow, not a T when doing push-ups.\" width=\"839\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey.png 996w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-300x214.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-768x549.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-713x510.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Pushups-good-bad-v3-grey-600x429.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 839px) 100vw, 839px\" /></p> \n<p><em><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>WARNING:</strong> If you have been doing push-ups with your arms flared, doing them with proper form will be significantly more difficult!</span></em></p> \n<p><b>If you struggle with your push-up form, you’re not alone!</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As I said in the intro, 95% of people do push-ups incorrectly, which is why it’s a huge focus of ours in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Coaching Program</a>: helping people get confident with doing them with proper form.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let us check your push-up form via video, create a workout program that fits your lifestyle, and even help you make better food choices. We’d love to help!</span></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3574583\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-713x218.jpg\" alt=\"Your NF Coach can help you lose weight and get healthy!\" width=\"765\" height=\"234\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-713x218.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-300x92.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-768x235.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1-600x184.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-00-Main-2d1.jpg 1311w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 765px) 100vw, 765px\" /></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Our coaching program is changing lives. Learn how we can change yours: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><b><a name=\"do_a_push_up\"></a>How to Do a Proper Push-Up (Correct Push-Up Form with Video).</b></h2> \n<p><iframe title=\"How to Do a Proper Push Up | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/8V-ZUMvQKr0?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><strong><b>In the 5-minute “Perfect Push-Up” video above,</b> featuring yours truly and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">two of our coaches</a>, we take you through EACH of the steps of a push-up, including some variations!</strong></p> \n<p><strong>Here’s how to complete one perfect repetition of a proper push up:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>With your arms straight, butt clenched, and abs braced,</strong> steadily lower yourself until your elbows are at a 90-degree angle or less. Depending on your level of experience, age, and flexibility, 90 degrees might be the lowest you’re able to go. Personally, I like to go down until my chest (not my face), hits the floor. That way, I know I’m going the same distance each and every time.</li> \n <li><strong>Try not to let your elbows go flying way out with each repetition.</strong>&nbsp;Keep them relatively close to your body, and keep note of when they start to fly out when you get tired.</li> \n <li><strong>Once your chest <b>(or nose/chin) </b>touches the floor (or your arms go down to a 90-degree angle)</strong>, pause slightly and then explode back up until you’re back in the same position.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3583878 size-large\" title=\"Screen shot 2011-02-15 at 11.36.53 PM\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-down-713x315.png\" alt=\"Once you get down like so for your push-up it's time to...push...up.\" width=\"713\" height=\"315\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-down-713x315.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-down-300x133.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-down-600x265.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-down.png 763w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p>Do as many as you can until you start to feel your form slip (even slightly); you are done for that set.</p> \n<p><b>Here’s why you should focus on form over quantity:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li>10 good push-ups and 5 crappy ones are tough to quantify against eleven good push-ups.</li> \n <li>If you can only do 10 of something, write down your results and aim for 11 next time.</li> \n <li>Perfect form allows you to keep track of your improvements week over week.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Want to know where push-ups should fall into your workout routine?</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> I have three options!</span></p> \n<p><b>1) Work with your coach to have push-ups become part of your workout routine! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re in the “I just want to be told what to do every day” crowd, check out our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Online Coaching Program</a>!</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Click here to learn how our coaches can build you a workout routine! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<p><b>2) Do them as part of our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/beginner-body-weight-workout-burn-fat-build-muscle/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Beginner Bodyweight Workout Routine</a>! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This workout has been done by hundreds of thousands of people as their first <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">strength training workout</a>.</span></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Beginner Body Weight Circuit Workout | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/qvhHhDNjtxM?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<div class=\"nf-in-post-signup-leadin\"></div>\n<div class=\"nf-in-post-signup one-column split yellow-cta bodyweight shortcode-form-15 \">\n <div class=\"nf-signup-intro\">\n  <div>\n   <span style=\"font-weight:700\">Grab Your Beginner Bodyweight Routine Worksheet. style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>3) Make your own workout with push-ups by following our</strong> </span><b>“<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Build Your Own Workout</a>” guide!</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;It’ll walk you through everything you need to build an exercise program for your goals in 10 steps.</span></p> \n<h2><b><a name=\"train_for_push_up\"></a>How Do You Train to Do Push-Ups? (Where to Start If You Can’t Do a Push-Up.)</b></h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3576035\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/army-LEGO-push-ups-713x400.jpg\" alt=\"These LEGO characters love to stay fit doing the beginner bodyweight workout\" width=\"713\" height=\"400\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/army-LEGO-push-ups.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/army-LEGO-push-ups-300x168.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/army-LEGO-push-ups-600x337.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Don’t worry if you can’t do a push-up yet.&nbsp;</b><b>We have a plan that will help you get there.</b></p> \n<p>You need to start with an easier push movement, and work up to progressively more difficult types of moves that will eventually result in you doing true push-ups.</p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is a similar type of progression we use when helping somebody in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Online Coaching Program</a> develop the proper strength to start doing proper push-ups.</span></p> \n<p><b>We’ll progress from Level 1 Push-ups to Level 4 Push-ups:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Wall Push-Ups: Level 1</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Elevated Push-Ups: Level 2</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Knee Push-ups: Level 3</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Regular Push-ups: Level 4</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><strong>LEVEL 1: HOW TO DO WALL PUSH-UPS</strong></span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>Stand in front of a wall. Clench your butt, brace your abs, and set your hands on the wall at slightly wider than shoulder-width apart.</strong></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">Walk backwards with your feet until your arms are fully extended and supporting your weight (generally one decent sized step back with both feet will suffice). Keeping the rest of your body in a straight line, steadily lower yourself towards the wall until your nose almost touches the wall, and then explode back up to the starting position.</p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3671456\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/wall-push-up.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"360\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><b>HOW TO TRAIN WALL PUSH-UPS: </b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>Do 4 sets of wall push-ups with a 2-minute rest between sets, every other day.</strong>&nbsp;Keep track of how many repetitions you can do WITH PROPER FORM for each set in a notebook for easy comparison to previous workouts. Once you can do 4 sets of 20 repetitions of wall push-ups, you can progress to knee push-ups.</p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>LEVEL TWO:&nbsp;HOW TO DO ELEVATED PUSH-UPS</b></span></p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_x8geaipo1v dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/x8geaipo1v/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong><b>As we demonstrate in this video above from <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/prime-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Nerd Fitness Prime</a>, e</b>levated push-ups are just what they sound like</strong>&nbsp;– your hands are on an elevated surface, whether it’s something as tall as a kitchen table or as low as a few blocks that are inches off the ground. This will depend on your level of strength and experience.</p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>If you’ve just progressed from wall push-ups, pick something that is at a level that’s right for you&nbsp;</strong>– I generally find the back of a park bench or the side of a picnic table to be a perfect height for doing incline push-ups. Like so:</p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Incline Push Up\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/4coDbSYnuh4?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><b>HOW TO TRAIN ELEVATED PUSH-UPS: </b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>Do 4 sets of elevated push-ups with a 2-minute rest between sets, every other day.</strong>&nbsp;Again, keep track of all of your stats for how many proper form repetitions you can do in each set. Once you can do 4 sets of 20 repetitions, it’s time to either move to regular push-ups, knee push-ups, or a lower height for your hands to be supported.</p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you can do 4 sets of 20 repetitions, it’s time to either move to regular push-ups, knee push-ups, or a lower height for your hands to be supported.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>To work on progression, try to doing your elevated push-ups on the stairs in your house.&nbsp;</strong>As you get stronger, you can move your hands to lower and lower steps until your hands are on the ground.</p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>LEVEL THREE: HOW TO DO KNEE PUSH-UPS </b></span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3583789\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/knee-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Knee push-ups like this are a great way to progress to a regular push-up!\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>Once&nbsp;</strong><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>you’re comfortable doing wall or elevated push-ups, proceed to knee push-ups.</strong> Your shoulder and hand placement will look just like a regular push-up (an “arrow”, not a “T”), but you’ll stabilize yourself on your knees instead of your feet. As demonstrated here:</span></p> \n<p><strong><iframe class=\"wistia_embed\" src=\"//fast.wistia.net/embed/iframe/wo2mz94445\" name=\"wistia_embed\" width=\"601\" height=\"338\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></strong></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><b>HOW TO TRAIN KNEE PUSH-UPS</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you can do 4 sets of 20 repetitions on your knees, you can start thinking about doing regular push-ups.</span></p> \n<p><b>To recap, if you can’t do a regular push-up, move from:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Wall Push-Ups: Level 1</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Elevated Push-Ups: Level 2</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Knee Push-Ups: Level 3</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Regular Push-ups: Level 4</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>How do I know the above progression will work? Well, it’s the exact plan we use with our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Online Coaching clients</a>!&nbsp;</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We help busy people just like you do push-ups for the first time with tailor-made workout routines.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Plus, our coaching app lets you record and send a video of your movement directly to your coach, who will make sure you’re doing your push-ups </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">safely</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> and </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">effectively</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. </span></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3553281 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-16-Ad1b-ExerciseWithoutRealizingIt-web75-713x403.png\" alt=\"Nerd Fitness Coaching Banner\" width=\"713\" height=\"403\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-16-Ad1b-ExerciseWithoutRealizingIt-web75-713x403.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-16-Ad1b-ExerciseWithoutRealizingIt-web75-300x170.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-16-Ad1b-ExerciseWithoutRealizingIt-web75-768x434.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-16-Ad1b-ExerciseWithoutRealizingIt-web75-600x339.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/NERD-CoachingBanner2019-16-Ad1b-ExerciseWithoutRealizingIt-web75.png 900w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Let us fix your push-up form and help you lose weight. Learn more about our Coaching Program: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><b><a name=\"push_up_variations\"></a>What Are Other Types of Push-Ups? (Push-Up Variations)</b></h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3581356\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/stormtrooper-pushups-713x534.jpg\" alt=\"These stromtroopers need some variety in their push-up routine...if this drill instructor ever lets up.\" width=\"713\" height=\"534\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/stormtrooper-pushups.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/stormtrooper-pushups-300x225.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/stormtrooper-pushups-600x449.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Basic push-ups can get boring…</strong></p> \n<p>Fortunately, there are dozens upon dozens of variations to make things more difficult for you.</p> \n<p><strong>Once you’re cranking out perfect form push-ups like it’s your job,<b><a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=8109#footnote-1\" id=\"refmark-1\"><sup>[1]</sup></a></b> try some of these advanced variations on for size.</strong></p> \n<p><strong>Click on each for a video demonstration (these are some of the push-up variations pulled from <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/prime-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">NF Prime</a>):</strong></p> \n<p><strong>#1) One-legged Push-ups:</strong> introducing some variety and balance by removing one of your legs for less stabilization:</p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_chj5ro64hb dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/chj5ro64hb/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><b>#2) Side-to-Side Push-Ups </b><b>–</b> <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Get into the classic push-up position and move your hands farther apart. Now, lower yourself down towards one arm only – you should feel like you’re supporting a lot of your weight.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">To complete the rep, slide horizontally over to the other arm, and push-up. The farther apart your hands, the higher percentage of your bodyweight will be supported by that side of your chest/shoulder and arm (thus getting harder)!</span></p> \n<p><iframe class=\"wistia_embed\" src=\"//fast.wistia.net/embed/iframe/fqqomxzxvx\" name=\"wistia_embed\" width=\"601\" height=\"338\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>#3) Decline Push-Ups&nbsp;–&nbsp;</strong>these work your shoulders and triceps more so than normal push-ups.</p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_876rx50kbh dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/876rx50kbh/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>#4) Diamond Push-Ups</strong><strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;</strong>keep your arms tight at your side, rotate your hands outward, and keep your elbows tight as you lower your body. Works your triceps like crazy.</p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_ond3at9xht dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/ond3at9xht/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>#5) Dive-Bomber Push-Ups</strong><strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;</strong>funky, difficult, but oh so fun. I’d explain it, but just watch the video</p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_ps0ljzbm6w dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/ps0ljzbm6w/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>#6) Plyometric Push-Ups</strong><strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;</strong>these are brutal and will wear you out just after a few repetitions. Just don’t hurt yourself a<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">nd smash your face during a failed attempt (not that I’ve ever done that. Shut up my face always looks like this)!</span></p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_vouohkrpyz dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/vouohkrpyz/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><b>#7) Handstand Push-Ups – This goes without saying, but you should be able to <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-handstands/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">do a proper handstand</a> before attempting these! </b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Kick up against a wall, and without flailing your elbows way out to the side (which can wreak havoc on your shoulders and elbow joints), slowly lower yourself down until your head touches the ground softly. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Then raise yourself back up.</span></p> \n<p><iframe class=\"wistia_embed\" src=\"//fast.wistia.net/embed/iframe/es85f9meb8\" name=\"wistia_embed\" width=\"601\" height=\"338\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>Rotate some of these advanced push-ups into your workout routine and you’ll be well on your way to a great strength training practice.</b></p> \n<p><b>The coaches in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Coaching Program</a> are all huge nerds who can’t wait to help people like you get strong as hell. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whether you’re working on knee push or trying to nail your first handstand, we can build custom workout programs that fit your lifestyle and align with your goals.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We also provide text support and worldwide accountability to make sure you actually DO your workouts!&nbsp;</span><b>&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Our coaching program doesn’t suck. Learn how we can change your life (seriously): </button> </a> </p> \n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>We also have a comprehensive guide, <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><i>Strength </div>\n    </form>\n   </div></img>\n </div>\n <div class=\"clearme\"></div>\n</div> \n<h2><a name=\"get_better_at_push_up\"></a>How to get better at push-ups</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3583880 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Steve-Push-Ups-Down-713x369.jpg\" alt=\"Notice how Steve's arms are angled like an arrow? This is the correct form for a push-up.\" width=\"713\" height=\"369\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Steve-Push-Ups-Down-713x369.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Steve-Push-Ups-Down-300x155.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Steve-Push-Ups-Down-768x397.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Steve-Push-Ups-Down-600x310.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Steve-Push-Ups-Down.jpg 942w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>So you’ve learned how to do a push-up, you can do a few of them, but you want to get better!&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p>Here are some tips to help you along the way:</p> \n<ol> \n <li><strong>Get healthy!</strong>&nbsp;As you lose weight (<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/healthy-eating/\">which is 80% nutrition</a>!), you will have to move less weight around than before, which will make your push-ups easier to manage.&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Have you had trouble losing weight in the past? Check out our article “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Why Can’t I Lose Weight?</a>” to find out why. </span></li> \n <li><strong>Don’t cheat on the last few&nbsp;push-ups&nbsp;</strong>– when you’re tired, it’s easy to skip out on good form for your last few reps. As soon as you do one bad form push-up, you’re done. Finish up your four sets, write down your numbers, and try to beat those numbers next time.</li> \n <li><strong>When starting out don’t do push-ups two days in a row.</strong>&nbsp;You need to give your muscles time to rebuild and recover – take off at least 48 hours in between your push-up adventure. However, when push-ups became a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/warm-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">warm-up exercise</a> for you – <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">you can do them every day if you want. If you’re advanced, you can consider</span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/that-time-i-did-2440-pull-ups-the-60-day-plp-challenge/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">&nbsp;a PLP program</a>.</li> \n <li><strong>Get enough protein into your system after finishing up your workout</strong>&nbsp;– protein helps rebuild the muscles you just broke down doing push-ups, and it helps them rebuild those same muscles stronger than before.&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-much-protein-do-i-need-to-eat-every-day-protein-101-guide/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">ultimate guide on protein</a>&nbsp;for some tips on how to up your protein intake. </span></li> \n <li><strong>If you can do 4 sets of 20-25 perfect form push-ups no sweat, then it’s time to start looking into push-up variations to keep things interesting.</strong></li> \n <li><strong>Build up your core with&nbsp;planks&nbsp;–&nbsp;</strong>this will help keep your core strong so that it’s not the weakest link in your proper form push-ups.</li> \n</ol> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter  wp-image-3756954\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/front-plank.gif\" alt=\"Coach Staci showing you the front plant\" width=\"451\" height=\"254\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">These 6 tips will be a great addition to your strength training plan. Keep at it and before you know it you’ll be doing one-arm push-ups like Batman.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3581189\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/batman-push-up.gif\" alt=\"One arm push-ups are hardcore, which is why Batman does them.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">What’s that? You don’t have a strength-building plan!!! Well then…</span></p> \n<h2>What’s Your Strength Building Plan?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3583884 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-explode.png\" alt=\"Once you get comfortable with regular push-ups, you can try plyometric push ups like this.\" width=\"700\" height=\"339\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-explode.png 700w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-explode-300x145.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-push-up-explode-600x291.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>It makes me sad when we get emails from people who struggle and try and work hard to get healthier, and to be better at push-ups, and just can’t seem to make any progress.</strong></p> \n<p>If that’s you, <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">you’re not alone</span>!</p> \n<p><b>1) Consider working with an online coach (or in-person trainer). </b></p> \n<p><b>Helping people learn push-ups and other bodyweight exercises is why we built our</b> <strong><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\">1-on-1
