here</a>.&nbsp;</em></p> \n<p>Let’s do this thang.</p> \n<p><strong><span id=\"more-9278\"></span></strong></p> \n<h2><b><a name=\"pull_up_tips\"></a>Tips on How to Start Doing Pull-Ups</b></h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-21826 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Steve-Pull-Ups-713x399.jpg\" alt=\"At Nerd Fitness we encourage everyone to get to their first pull-up!\" width=\"713\" height=\"399\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Steve-Pull-Ups-713x399.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Steve-Pull-Ups-300x167.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Steve-Pull-Ups.jpg 943w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Before we get into exercises to progress into a pull-up, let’s chat about some general strategies:</b></p> \n<p><strong>#1) This should hopefully be obvious, but the more you weigh, the more you have to lift in order to complete a pull-up.</strong></p> \n<p>If you’re truly serious about completing a pull-up, start by getting your diet under control.<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As we say here at Nerd Fitness, 80-90% of weight loss comes down to what you eat (<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/about-2/rules-of-the-rebellion/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">#4 in the Rules of the Rebellion</a>).</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are some</b><b> resources to help you with weight loss:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Tried to lose weight in the past without success?</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> I hear you, weight loss is super tough. Learn why in our article “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Why Can’t I Lose Weight?</a>” for a deep dive into the subject. We also have the 5<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-lose-weight-without-dieting-5-rules-of-weight-loss/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"> Rules of Weight Loss</a> to help you get going.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Not sure what a proper diet looks like?</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Check out our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/healthy-eating/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">guide on healthy eating</a> for a full lesson on nutrition.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Wondering if <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-paleo-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Paleo</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-keto-diet-or-ketogenic-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Keto</a>, or <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-eat-a-plant-based-diet-a-scientific-look-at-going-vegan-safely/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Veganism</a> can help you with weight loss?</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> They </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">might.&nbsp;</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Read our guide on </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/paleo-keto-slow-carb-vegan-how-to-determine-the-perfect-diet-for-you/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">determining</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> the perfect diet (for you).&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>In the above guides, you’ll find me stating that losing weight comes down to eating fewer calories than you burn.</b> Not sure how many calories you need? Check out our guide on <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">calculating your daily caloric requirements</a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>#2) MAKE YOUR “PULL” EXERCISES A PRIORITY.</strong> A lot of people do every other exercise before doing any back-related exercises, if they do any at all.</p> \n<p>After <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/warm-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">warming up properly</a>, your first exercise should always be the stuff that you want to work on the most – in this case it’ll be your back muscles.</p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Until you get your first pull-up done, focus on the back exercises detailed in the levels and workouts below. </span></p> \n<p><strong>#3) The progression below is a path that <b>works for most people</b>, but does NOT need to be followed to a T. </strong></p> \n<p>I give sample sets and reps and when to move up, but if you feel like you can progress sooner or want to try doing full pull-ups sooner than I recommend, that’s OKAY.</p> \n<p>This is the slower progression method, where some people will want to do fewer reps and progress to the next levels sooner – that’s okay.</p> \n<p><strong>I recommend moving up to the next level when you can do 3 sets of 8 reps of a particular exercise. </strong> If you want the <em>accelerated path</em>, move on up as faster as you can do 3 sets of 5 reps. You do you boo.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585369\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/Portlandia.gif\" alt=\"You can follow our path for a pull-up but feel free to make it your own!\" width=\"340\" height=\"191\" /></p> \n<p><b>Want someone to build you a custom made progression plan for doing your first pull-up? </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Online Coaching Program</a> will do just that, plus your coach can review your movements through our app so you’ll know your training correctly and safely.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> You’re not alone on this journey. Let our Online Coaches help you conquer your first pull-up! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"level_1_pull_up\"></a>Level 1 Pull-up Workout: Bent Over Dumbbell Rows</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3584785\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/dumbbell-row.gif\" alt=\"Do a dumbbell row as a great beginner exercise to get strong enough for a pull-up!\" width=\"658\" height=\"370\" /></p> \n<p><strong>We’re going to start with <b>bent over dumbbell rows</b>, the most basic of back exercises, in case you’re starting from ABSOLUTELY square one.</strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>Level 1 Pull-up Workout</b></span><b>:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Bent over dumbbell rows: 8 reps each arm (or as many as you can do)</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rest for a 2-minute break</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Do another set</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Repeat until you hit 3 sets</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-much-weight-should-i-be-lifting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">What weight should you start out with initially?</a></span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whatever allows you to get to at least 5 reps a set</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you can do 3 sets of 8 reps (each arm), it’s time to pick up a heavier dumbbell. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This will allow you to get stronger and stronger.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Make sure you give yourself at least 48 hours until you do the <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Level 1 Dumbbell Rows</span> again, so you can include these dumbbell rows for your workouts on:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Monday</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Wednesday</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Friday</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As soon as you can do 3 sets of 8 reps, it’s time to move up to a heavier dumbbell.</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you can lift&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">a 25-pound (10kg) dumbbell or heavier, consider moving up to the <a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=9278#level_2_pull_up\">next level</a>.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you are a little bit bigger than the average bear, you might want to stick with this step until you lose a little bit more weight and get stronger – maybe go to 35 or 40-pound (18kg) dumbbells.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Want help designing your own workout routine? I’ve got two options for you.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The first is to head over to “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Build Your Own Workout Routine</a>” and get your hands dirty. Our guide will walk you through building a full body exercise program in 10 simple steps.</span></p> \n<p><b>The second is to have a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Nerd Fitness Coach</a> do all the heavy lifting for you (not really, you still have to lift stuff),</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> by having them build you a tailor-made workout routine:</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Click here to have a Nerd Fitness Coach build you a routine to start crushing pull-ups! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"level_2_pull_up\"></a>Level 2 Pull-Up Workout: Inverted Bodyweight Rows</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585382 \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/steve-inverted-row-1.gif\" alt=\"Inverted rows are a great exercise to work on doing your first pull-up.\" width=\"631\" height=\"355\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Body weight rows are the PERFECT precursor to pull-ups</strong> – they work the same muscles, <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">and have you lifting your own bodyweight,&nbsp;</span>just at a different angle.</p> \n<p><b>For this level, we’ll provide you with two options:&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can also make adjustments.</span></b></p> \n<p><b>OPTION A: </b><b>IF YOU HAVE ACCESS TO A GYM OR WANT TO JOIN A GYM</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">:</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can follow the rest of this workout as part of our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">6-Level Gym workout guide</a>, which will help you go from total gym newbie to pull-up progressing badass!</span></p> \n<p><b>At your gym, find your Smith Machine and set the bar at about chest height.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>A higher bar makes the exercise easier to start:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585386 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-incline-inverted-row-1.gif\" alt=\"Start with inclined inverted rows for your pull-up workout. Then drop lower for more required effort.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>And as you get stronger, you can set the bar lower:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585387 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-bodyweight-row-1.gif\" alt=\"As you get lower, like this, the row will be harder to do. Great way to progress into a pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here’s a whole post I did on <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/inverted-row-are-you-missing-out-on-this-great-exercise/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">inverted </a></span></i><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">bodyweight rows.</span></i></p> \n<p><b>Here’s how to do an inverted bodyweight row (here is a video demonstration with gymnastic rings, but you can start with a bar as displayed in the images below).</b></p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_q9t1tnbfpt dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/q9t1tnbfpt/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Set the bar at a height where it’s challenging for you to complete 3 sets of 8 reps with two minutes of rest between sets.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Clench your butt and keep your abs tight and body straight throughout the exercise.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pull your shoulder blades down and back towards each other (like you’re trying to pinch a pencil between them behind your back).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Focus your mind on PULLING with your arms.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pull until your chest touches the bar (not your neck).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As soon as you can complete all 3 sets of 8 reps, set the bar heigh lower to make the exercise more difficult.</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you need to make the exercise less challenging, bend your knees and put your feet flat on the ground:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585388\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/inverted-row-bent-knee.gif\" alt=\"Bending your knees like so can be helpful to start doing inverted rows. \" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>Level 2 sample workout routine:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b>Monday </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">– 3 sets of 8 reps of overhand bodyweight rows</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585405 \" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/overheand-row.gif\" alt=\"Alternate between an overheand and underhand bodyweight row.\" width=\"485\" height=\"273\" /></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b>Wednesday</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> – 3 sets of 8 reps of </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">underhand bodyweight rows</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> (hands reversed)</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585390\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/bodyweight-row.gif\" alt=\"Alternate between underhand and overhand when doing bodyweight rows.\" width=\"485\" height=\"273\" /></span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Friday </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">– 3 sets of 8 reps of overhand bodyweight rows</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(And then go underhand, overhand, underhand the following week)</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As soon as you’re doing bodyweight rows where your body is at a 45-degree angle or lower, you can <a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=9278#level_3_pull_up\">progress to Level 3</a>.</span></i></p> \n<p><b>OPTION B: IF YOU DON’T HAVE ACCESS TO A GYM FOR INVERTED ROWS</b><b>:</b></p> \n<p><b>You have 3 paths here: </b></p> \n<p><b>1) Purchase a door frame pull-up bar, hang a pair of gymnastic rings from them. And then follow the same advice as above!</b></p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_6tocuupzsd dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/6tocuupzsd/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>2) Use your kitchen table for rows (BE CAREFUL):</strong></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"How to Do a Bodyweight Row | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/OYUxXMGVuuU?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><strong>3) Move up to Level 3 and progress with caution there.</strong></p> \n<p><b>If you are struggling with rows, you’re not sure you’re doing them correctly, or you’re not sure how to progress to the next level, check out our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 coaching program</a>.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>It’s the type of program that helped single mom Leslie lose 100+ pounds and start training with gymnastic rings and handstands!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3577194\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/07/Leslie-Before-After-713x427.png\" alt=\"How did Leslie transform? Strength training. with pull-ups\" width=\"713\" height=\"427\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/07/Leslie-Before-After-713x427.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/07/Leslie-Before-After-300x180.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/07/Leslie-Before-After.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/07/Leslie-Before-After-600x359.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Want to get results like Leslie? Let us help you get your first pull-up ASAP! Learn more: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"level_3_pull_up\"></a>Level 3 Pull-Up Workout: Assisted Pull-Ups</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585410\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/assisted-pull-up-band-steve.gif\" alt=\"Steve doing an assisted pull-up, a perfect precursor to a regular pull-up! \" width=\"681\" height=\"383\" /></p> \n<p><b>Okay! It’s time to get to ACTUAL pull-ups here! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Personally, I don’t like using the assisted pull-up machine in a gym as it doesn’t give you the full feeling of a pull-up, but it’s certainly better than nothing.</span></p> \n<p><strong>Instead, I recommend doing one of these alternatives:</strong></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>#1) Assisted Pull-ups with chair</strong></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585411\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/assisted-pull-up-chair.gif\" alt=\"A chair can be a great tool to help you get your first pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></strong></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Either one foot or two on the chair, depending on your needs. Your feet are ONLY there for support, use your upper body as much as possible.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can also use a box or similar sized object for the same result:</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585412\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/assisted-pull-up.gif\" alt=\"A box can be used instead of a chair for a pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>#2)Assisted Pull-ups with exercise band:&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585413\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/assisted-pull-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"Staci using a band for an assisted pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">You can get different types of exercise bands with different levels of strength, <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">or a variety pack for easy progression.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">Put your foot in the exercise band and pull yourself up.</p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><strong>#3) Assisted pull-ups with a partner:</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585414\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/pull-up-friend.gif\" alt=\"A friend can be a great asset when you're trying to do a pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">Have a friend hold your feet behind you and help you complete each rep. Have them use the least amount of help possible to get you through your workouts.</p> \n<p><strong>Here’s how to do an assisted pull-up:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>Clench your butt and keep your abs tight throughout the exercise – try not to swing like crazy.</li> \n <li>Keep your shoulder blades pinched behind you throughout the movement and focus on PULLING the bar down with your arms.</li> \n <li>Use the least amount of assistance that you can handle – as soon as you can do multiple pull-ups with both feet on the chair, switch to just one foot.</li> \n <li>If you’re using an exercise band, try to get a few bands of varying tension so you can decrease the resistance as you get stronger.</li> \n <li>As soon as you can do 3 sets of 8 with assistance, it’s time to move on to <a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=9278#level_4_pull_up\">Level 4</a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>A workout that includes&nbsp;Level 3 pull-up exercises</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Monday</strong> – Assisted Pull-ups – 3 sets of 8 reps</li> \n <li><strong>Wednesday – </strong>Inverted&nbsp;Bodyweight Rows – 3 sets of 8 reps</li> \n <li><strong>Friday – </strong>Assisted Chin Ups – 3 sets of 8 reps</li> \n</ul> \n<p><iframe title=\"72 - Assisted Chin Up Video\" src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/embed/iframe/s4lg3qdhr9?dnt=1\" allow=\"autoplay; fullscreen\" allowtransparency=\"true\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" class=\"wistia_embed\" name=\"wistia_embed\" allowfullscreen=\"\" msallowfullscreen=\"\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\"></iframe><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.net/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<p><b>This is probably the TOUGHEST level before getting your pull-ups.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> If you get stuck on “assisted pull-ups” and “assisted chin-ups”, you’re not alone. This is where most people get stuck.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We work hand-in-hand with people like you to get them their first pull-up in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Online Coaching Program</a>. If you don’t know how to fit these movements into your workouts, or you just want somebody to give you the exact workout to follow every day, we got you!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> No guesswork. No confusion. Just a workout program that’s customized for you. </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"level_4_pull_up\"></a>Level 4 Pull-Up Workout: Negative Pull-Ups</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585415\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/negative-pull-up.gif\" alt=\"Staci jumping up to do a negative pull-up.\" width=\"670\" height=\"377\" /></p> \n<p><b>Okay! We are now DANGEROUSLY close to getting our first pull-up!</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The big step at this level is doing a negative pull-up:</span></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grab onto the bar with overhand grip</span></li> \n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Jump so your chest is touching</span></li> \n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Slowly</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;lower yourself under control&nbsp;until you’re at the bottom of the movement.</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_xhbopbw3tg dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/xhbopbw3tg/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">WARNING: This can be very dangerous if you’re very overweight, which is why I’d recommend moving slowly through steps 1-3 first.</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">However, once you have a decent amount of back strength (which you got from Level 1, 2, and 3), doing negatives is a great way to build arm and back strength.</span></i></p> \n<p><b>You have two options for negative pull-ups:</b></p> \n<ol> \n <li>Hop up on a chair to get above the bar and then lower yourself back down. The name of the game is “in control.”</li> \n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Jump above the pull-up bar, and then begin to lower yourself back down IN CONTROL.</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You don’t need to lower yourself so slowly that one repetition destroys you…lower yourself in a controlled speed – Counting to “three Mississippi” during the movement is a good tempo.</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are the exercises you can include for your Level 4 Workout Routine:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Monday</strong> – Assisted Pull-ups – 3 sets of 8 repetitions</li> \n <li><strong>Wednesday</strong> – Body Weight Rows – 3 sets of 8 repetitions</li> \n <li><strong>Friday </strong>– Negative Pull-ups – 3 sets to failure – capped at 5 repetitions for each set.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Once you’re doing 3 sets of 5 repetitions on your negative pull-ups, along with your assisted chin-ups and body weight rows…<a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=9278#level_5_pull_up\">you’re ready <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">to do a pull-up</span></a>.</p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As you’ll see above, we’re giving you the “pull” exercises if you are <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">building your own workout</a>. If you want a good <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">beginner gym workout program</a>, these movements will fit in perfectly.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Alternatively, we can do all of the heavy lifting for you (well, not ALL the heavy lifting) – we’ll create a specific workout so all you have to do is log into your <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">NF Coaching App</a> each morning and do the workout your coach prescribed!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Never wonder what to do next. Learn how our coaching app can tell you exactly what to do every day! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"level_5_pull_up\"></a>Level 5 – Doing Your First Pull-up or Chin-up</h2> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_bjt84txk9w dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/bjt84txk9w/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>OH BOY! My dear Rebel, it’s time for a…</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585417\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/staci-pull-up.gif\" alt=\"We made it! Here's Staci doing a pull-up!!!\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>At this point you have two options:</b></p> \n<p><b>A <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">chin-up</span></b><b> is when you grab the bar with an underhand grip with your palms facing towards you.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585418\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/chin-up-staci.gif\" alt=\"A chin-up is a pull-up, but with your hands facing towards you.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Many find chin-ups slightly easier than…</span></p> \n<p><b>A pull-up</b><b> is when you grab the bar with your palms facing away from you. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Seeing as this is a pull-up guide…</span></p> \n<p><b>HOW TO DO A PULL-UP, STEP-BY-STEP:</b></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"How to Do a Proper Pull Up | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/IwlDSQx5u3A?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grab the bar with a grip slightly wider than shoulder width, with your hands facing away from you.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Start from a dead hang.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Engage your shoulders, pull them down and back towards each other (like you are pinching a pencil between your shoulder blades!)</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Flex your stomach, pull your body until your chest touches the bar.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Slight pause, yell out “I’m a champion!”</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Lower yourself <i>all</i> the way back down to a dead hang.</li> \n</ol> \n<p><b>We cover all of this and more in our post “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-do-a-proper-pull-up-and-why-you-need-to-do-them/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">How to Do a Proper Pull-Up</a>,” but the above will get you started</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Depending on your weight, your level of fitness and strength, and how far along you are in these progressions, you might be able to start with even more than one pull-up.</span></p> \n<p><b>At this point, you can be a full Gym Class Hero by <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">following a Gym Workout</a> with these movements in there for your “pull” exercises:</b></p> \n<p><b>&nbsp;Level 5 routine set up for a week:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Monday – </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Chin-ups – 3 sets for maximums repetitions</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Wednesday – </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Inverted Bodyweight Rows – 3 sets for max repetitions</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Friday –</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Pull-ups – 3 sets for maximum repetitions</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Congratulations! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You’re now doing pull-ups. Make sure you watch that video above to make sure you’re doing pull-ups with proper form. Nearly everybody does them incorrectly, with bad form.</span></p> \n<p><b>Want to make sure you have proper form with your pull-ups? </b>C<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">heck out our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">1-on-1 Coaching program</a>! Our spiffy mobile app lets you send video of your pull-ups directly to your coach, who will provide feedback so you can perfect your technique.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They’ll also build a workout program that’s custom to your situation, which will have you doing sets of 10 pull-ups in NO time!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Have your Nerd Fitness Coach build you a pull-up workout and check your form! Click here to learn more! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"level_6_pull_up\"></a>Level 6 – Advanced Pull-up Moves</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585445 size-full\" title=\"Weighted pull ups\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/weighted-pull-up-steve.jpg\" alt=\"Now you can move onto advanced pull-ups like Steve is doing here.\" width=\"637\" height=\"357\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/weighted-pull-up-steve.jpg 637w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/weighted-pull-up-steve-300x168.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/weighted-pull-up-steve-600x336.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 637px) 100vw, 637px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Once you’re able to do 3 sets of 10 pull-ups or chin-ups, you have a few options:</strong></p> \n<p><strong>OPTION #1: Continue to get better at doing more reps</strong> – 3 sets of 12, 3 sets of 15, 4 sets of 20, etc.</p> \n<p><strong>OPTION #2: Start doing other types of pull-ups&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p><b>WIDE GRIP PULL-UPS&nbsp;</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(grab the bar WAY out with both hands):</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585422\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/wide-grip-pull-up.gif\" alt=\"Maintaining a wide grip is a great advanced pull-up.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>SIDE TO SIDE PULL-UPS</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585423\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/side-to-side-pull-up.gif\" alt=\"Another form of an advanced pull-up for you. Shift your weight from arm to arm.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>RING PULL-UPS</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585424\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/ring-chin-up.gif\" alt=\"If you own some rings you can use them like so for some advanced pull-ups.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>TOWEL PULL-UPS (<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-improve-your-wrist-mobility-and-grip-strength/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Great for grip strength</a>)</b></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"How To Improve Grip Strength | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/AMdBQ1UXkLc?start=260&amp;feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>OPTION #3) Add weight with a weight belt and do </b><b>weighted pull-ups</b><b> or weighted chin-ups:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3585428\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/weighted-pull-up.gif\" alt=\"A weighted pull-up is great for progressive overload on your muscles. \" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Personally, my favorite thing to do in a gym is weighted pull-ups; if you’re at this level and interested in doing so, here’s what you need to do:</strong></p> \n<ol> \n <li><strong>Get a weight belt. </strong>I <a title=\"bought this one\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B001P0S3XU/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=nerdfitn-20&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;camp=217145&amp;creative=399349&amp;creativeASIN=B001P0S3XU\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">bought this one</a>&nbsp;on Amazon and it’s worked out incredibly well for me. I’ve tried doing the whole “put weights in a backpack” and it certainly works, but the angle of the weights hanging off your back is weird. With a weight belt, the weight hangs down between your legs (not a euphemism) so it feels more natural.</li> \n <li><strong>Add small amounts at a time. </strong>Most gyms will have 2.5 lb (roughly 1kg) weights; you might feel stupid putting on a big weight belt and only hanging a tiny weight off it, but you need to start somewhere.</li> \n <li><strong>Consistently add more weight. </strong>I’ll warm up with two sets of 5 pull-ups with no extra weight, and then do 3 sets of 5 weighted pull-ups. If I can complete all 3 sets of 5 reps (with my chin over the bar for every rep), I’ll make a note to add 2.5 or 5lbs (1 or 2kg) to my weight belt for the next time.</li> \n</ol> \n<p><b>Here’s how to incorporate these Level 6 exercises into your <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-the-gym-everything-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">gym workout routine</a>: </b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Monday</strong> – <a title=\"weighted chin ups\" href=\"http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KkA3Gi8vN3U\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Weighted Chin Ups</a> – 3 sets of 5 reps</li> \n <li><strong>Wednesday </strong>– <a title=\"Elevated Feet Body Weight Rows\" href=\"http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6AptmglPQ30\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Elevated Feet Body Weight Rows</a> – 3 sets of max repetitions</li> \n <li><strong>Friday </strong>– Wide Grip Pull-ups – 3 sets of maximum repetition</li> \n <li>(The following week, I’d alternate by doing the chin-ups without weight, and then doing weighted pull-ups</li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Where do you go from here? How about working towards one of the most impressive exercises of all time? The MUSCLE UP (warning: uber advanced)!</b></p> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_73pe1v8eft dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/73pe1v8eft/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p><b>We have a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/rings-and-handstands-superpack/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">20-level Gymnastic Rings Course</a> that will help you get your first muscle-up, including telling you exactly how to get there.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>You can learn more about our course by clicking on the box below:</b></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/rings-and-handstands-superpack/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Get your first muscle up by following our Beginner Gymnastic Rings Course! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><b>Lift Yourself Up (A Life With Pull-Ups)</b></h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585446 size-full\" title=\"PeruPullUps\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/steve-pull-up-stairs.jpg\" alt=\"The world can be your pull-up bar as Steve is showing here. \" width=\"705\" height=\"368\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/steve-pull-up-stairs.jpg 705w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/steve-pull-up-stairs-300x157.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/steve-pull-up-stairs-600x313.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 705px) 100vw, 705px\" /></p> \n<p><b>No matter your starting point, you CAN do pull-ups.</b></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And you WILL do pull-ups with this guide.&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You don’t need to follow the progression above exactly – it’s merely one path that you can take in order to reach the promised land…where the pull-ups flow like wine and the women instinctively flock like the Salmon of Capistrano.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3585432\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/pull-up.gif\" alt=\"High Five! </div></span></p> \n<p><span id=\"more-3026\"></span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"what_is_dip\"></a><strong>What Is the Dip Exercise? What Muscles Does the Dip Train?</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3584336 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/lego-bass-guitar-dip-713x482.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"713\" height=\"482\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/lego-bass-guitar-dip-713x482.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/lego-bass-guitar-dip-300x203.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/lego-bass-guitar-dip-768x519.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/lego-bass-guitar-dip-600x406.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/lego-bass-guitar-dip.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>The dip is a compound, bodyweight exercise.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You grab two parallel bars, hoist yourself up, and then lower your entire body by bending your elbows.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3594828 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/dips.gif\" alt=\"Bodyweight dips are a great exercise to include in an strength training practice.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you hear “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-12-best-compound-exercises-for-beginners-how-to-train-efficiently/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">compound exercise</a>,” it’s referring to multi-joint movements that work several muscles or muscle groups at the same time.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>The dip exercise trains your:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Chest</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Shoulders</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Tricep</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Back</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Abs</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You may be thinking, “abs?”</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yep! You need to stabilize your body as you raise and lower yourself.</span></p> \n<p><b>Which is one of the reasons bodyweight dips are so great!</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Some would even argue that dips are the best chest exercise out there, even better than the <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/what-do-you-bench-strength-training-101-the-bench-press/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">bench press</a>.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3478456 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Owl.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"320\" height=\"220\" /></p> \n<p><b>There’s some logic to it.</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you think about it, the bench itself offers a lot of support during the bench press. So do your legs.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">With the dip exercise, your upper body is supporting your entire body. Thus a fuller workout.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Instead of isolating your chest for 5 exercises, your shoulders for 5 exercises, and triceps for 5 exercises, just do dips!</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"how_to_do_dip\"></a><strong>How to Do a Proper Dip Exercise</strong></h2> \n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p> \n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\"> \n <div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\"> \n  <div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_gcx6mlvv5w dnt=1 videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\"> \n   <div class=\"wistia_swatch\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;opacity:0;overflow:hidden;position:absolute;top:0;transition:opacity 200ms;width:100%;\">\n    <img src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/gcx6mlvv5w/swatch\" style=\"filter:blur(5px);height:100%;object-fit:contain;width:100%;\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\" onload=\"this.parentNode.style.opacity=1;\" />\n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p><b>First of all, make sure you can do a dip.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Don’t hop up there and then lower yourself unless you’re fairly confident you can get through at least one of these things. We can’t have you tearing any muscles or falling on somebody, because that would suck.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Head to our <a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3026#dip_progression_plan\">progression plan if you can’t do a full dip</a> yet.&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><strong>Here’s how to do a proper dip exercise:</strong></p> \n<ol> \n <li><strong>Grab the parallel bars (or rings), and hoist yourself up. </strong> At this point look straight ahead, and contract your stomach muscles (just like when you do <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">squats</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-the-deadlift/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">deadlifts</a>). If you’re keeping your abs tight for all of these exercises, you’ll never have to do a crunch again and you’ll still have washboard abs.</li> \n <li><strong>Bend your knees if you like </strong>(so your feet are behind you), for stability purposes, but keep your head up and look straight ahead.</li> \n <li><strong>Keeping your elbows at your side, lower yourself until your triceps are parallel to the floor. </strong> A lot of folks will recommend you go past parallel, but I think this puts too much strain on your shoulders at a weird angle and can cause injury/discomfort. I only go down to parallel and haven’t had any issues, so I’d recommend the same.</li> \n <li><strong>Once you hit parallel, explode back up until JUST before you’re able to lock your elbows.</strong> By not locking your elbows, you keep the tension in your muscles and don’t jack up your joints. w00t.</li> \n <li><strong>Now do another one. </strong>And then another!</li> \n</ol> \n<p>Those are dips.</p> \n<p>Keep your <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">elbows as tight as possible</span>, <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">engage your abs</span>, and hold your <span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">body in balance</span> as you go up and down.</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3840920\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/steve-ring-dips.gif\" alt=\"A gif of Steve doing bodyweight ring dips\" width=\"460\" height=\"251\" /></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Are you doing it right?</span></i></p> \n<p><b>Check your form by recording a video of yourself and matching it against the videos and gifs here.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> If it looks close then you’re doing great!</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Want to have an expert review your form? Our coaches can do just that in our spiffy app!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> Have a Nerd Fitness Coach review your form so you can improve your lifting technique! </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"dip_progression_plan\"></a><strong>What If I Can’t Perform a Dip? (Progression Plan)</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-3656101\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-map-713x428.jpg\" alt=\"Have no fear, with a proper plan we'll have you doing dips in no time.\" width=\"713\" height=\"428\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-map-713x428.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-map-300x180.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-map-768x461.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-map-600x360.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-map.jpg 2040w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>If you don’t quite have the strength to do a full bodyweight dip, follow our progression plan below.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You’ll be doing the complete dip movement before you know it!</span></p> \n<p><b>Level 1 Dip Progression: Knee Push-Ups</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3583789 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/knee-push-up.gif\" alt=\"Knee push-ups like this are a great way to progress to a regular push-up!\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re just starting to develop your push muscles, our first stop will be knee push-ups. We’ll build your strength up so you can start doing…</span></p> \n<p><b>Level 2 Dip Progression: Push-Ups</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3583748 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/push-up.gif\" alt=\"This gif shows Staci doing a push-up in perfect form.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Can you do a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">push-up with proper form</a> yet? If not, that’s our stop.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Push-ups will help you develop chest muscles for doing proper dips. Only after you can do 20 proper push-ups should you consider trying to do a dip.</span></p> \n<p><b>Level 3 Dip Progression: Assisted Dips</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-3594813 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/assisted-dips.gif\" alt=\"A resistance band is a great way to get started with this bodyweight exercise.\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s now time to do some dips! With a little bit of assistance…</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’ll use a <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/AmazonBasics-Resistance-Pull-Band-30-60/dp/B01FN7XBVO/ref=as_li_ss_tl?keywords=pull+up+band&amp;pd_rd_i=B01FN7XBVO&amp;pd_rd_r=79fb2b51-e517-41a0-972f-76032efe3347&amp;pd_rd_w=l3iXa&amp;pd_rd_wg=Y64jq&amp;pf_rd_p=be5d8dec-444e-4770-91df-1e16a8c46da8&amp;pf_rd_r=R405TBXSG7NGS76TQ5R7&amp;qid=1562757035&amp;s=gateway&amp;linkCode=sl1&amp;tag=nerdfitn-20&amp;linkId=4b1fd6ac02564c37835aacc7b7dc6dd3&amp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">resistance band</a> to help support your weight while you grow stronger. You can progress with weaker and weaker resistance bands until you feel comfortable trying a proper bodyweight dip.</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How about using an <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Body-Solid-Weight-Assisted-Chin-Machine/dp/B00HAVIE0A\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">assisted dip machine</a>?</span></i></p> \n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-3656582 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dip-machine.jpg\" alt=\"You may see these at the gym, but our advice would be to use a resistance band instead of this contraption.\" width=\"425\" height=\"491\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dip-machine.jpg 425w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dip-machine-260x300.jpg 260w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 425px) 100vw, 425px\" /></p> \n<p><b>We’re <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/rage-against-the-machine-how-to-switch-from-exercise-machines-to-free-weights/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">not huge fans of machines</a> here at Nerd Fitness.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here’s why: an assisted dip machine stabilizes your body during the movement, which means your own muscles don’t need to do any of that stabilization work!</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;We’d rather you stick with <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/AmazonBasics-Resistance-Pull-Band-30-60/dp/B01FN7XBVO/ref=as_li_ss_tl?keywords=pull+up+band&amp;pd_rd_i=B01FN7XBVO&amp;pd_rd_r=79fb2b51-e517-41a0-972f-76032efe3347&amp;pd_rd_w=l3iXa&amp;pd_rd_wg=Y64jq&amp;pf_rd_p=be5d8dec-444e-4770-91df-1e16a8c46da8&amp;pf_rd_r=R405TBXSG7NGS76TQ5R7&amp;qid=1562757035&amp;s=gateway&amp;linkCode=sl1&amp;tag=nerdfitn-20&amp;linkId=4b1fd6ac02564c37835aacc7b7dc6dd3&amp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">resistance bands</a> than mess with this contraption, as it still makes your muscles work together throughout the movement.</span></p> \n<p><em>You can check out some brands to buy, and how to train with them, in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-ultimate-resistance-band-workout-how-to-train-with-exercise-bands/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Guide to Resistance Bands</a>.</em></p> \n<p>Sure<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, if you don’t have bands and can ONLY do dips with the machine pictured above, it’s not the end of the world! Just make sure you are also doing other movements as well that DO recruit those stabilizer muscles (<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/proper-push-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">push-ups</a>, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-the-overhead-press/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">presses</a>, and so on).</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you find yourself getting stuck on “assisted dips,” you’re not alone. Lots of folks find it difficult to move beyond the support of the band.</span></p> \n<p><b>We work hand-in-hand with people like you to master bodyweight training in our </b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"><b>Online Coaching Program</b></a><b>.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> If you don’t know how to add dips into your workouts, or you just want somebody to give you the exact workout to follow every day, we got you!</span></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button red\"> No guesswork. No confusion. Just a workout program that’s customized for you. </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><strong><a name=\"tips_to_dip\"></a>Tips and Tricks for Performing the Dip Exercise</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3656591\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/man-doing-dip.jpg\" alt=\"In this section, we'll make sure you don't make any newbie mistakes when doing dips.\" width=\"820\" height=\"344\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/man-doing-dip.jpg 1075w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/man-doing-dip-300x126.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/man-doing-dip-768x322.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/man-doing-dip-713x299.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/man-doing-dip-600x252.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 820px) 100vw, 820px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Here are some extra tips on getting better at dips:</strong></p> \n<p><strong>#1) Get your setup correct at the start.</strong></p> \n<p>When people experience pain with their dips, it’s probably one of two things:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>When your arms go too far back, they can close off the shoulder and start to cause pain.</li> \n <li>If you allow your shoulders to round forward during the movement, it can again close off the area and create discomfort.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Coach Jim shows you how to avoid these two issues in the video “How to Do Pain-Free Dips,” which you can check out right here:</p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Pain-free dips\" width=\"500\" height=\"375\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/WuyD9EbwtyY?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><strong>#2) Don’t swing </strong>– this goes for practically every exercise. If you start swinging your body as you go up and down, you take the emphasis off the muscles you’re actually trying to work.</p> \n<p>Save swinging for the playground:</p> \n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-3656611 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dog-swingset.gif\" alt=\"This dog keeps his swinging to the playground.\" width=\"270\" height=\"260\" /></p> \n<p><strong>#3) Don’t flare out your elbows if you can avoid it </strong>– the more “out” your elbows are, the more emphasis on your chest. Elbows tight = emphasis on shoulders and triceps.</p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Nicholas Elorreaga does a good job showing the difference here:</span><br /> <iframe src=\"https://gfycat.com/ifr/TartUnimportantHarrier\" width=\"640\" height=\"404\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>#4) Don’t do half reps </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">– again, this could be another </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">universal</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> rule. Challenge your muscles by bringing your </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">triceps</span> <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">parallel</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> to the ground, then make sure you extend arms to </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">almost </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“elbows locked” at the top:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3656626 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/steve-dip.gif\" alt=\"You can see here that Steve is doing a complete rep when doing his dip.\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" /></p> \n<p><b>#5) Don’t go too fast </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;– you want to be slow and in control during your dip. When you go too quickly, proper form is often sacrificed. Make sure you train safely by going slowly…this isn’t a race!</span></p> \n<p><strong>#6) Don’t settle for cheap substitutes</strong> – don’t use dip machines or other <a href=\"https://muscledfitness.com/tricep-dip/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">isolation tricep machines:</a></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3656631 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dip-machine-II.jpg\" alt=\"Our advice is to not use machines like this. The bodyweight dip will provide a fuller workout.\" width=\"389\" height=\"471\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dip-machine-II.jpg 499w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dip-machine-II-248x300.jpg 248w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/dip-machine-II-496x600.jpg 496w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 389px) 100vw, 389px\" /></p> \n<p>These don’t recruit any of your stabilizer muscles, put your body at weird angles, and don’t give you full results. Stick with bodyweight dips!</p> \n<h2><a name=\"advanced_dip\"></a><strong>Variations on the Dip (Advanced Dip Moves)</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-3656968 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-dip.jpg\" alt=\"We'll show you some advanced dip variations in this section, so you can rock dips like this blue dude.\" width=\"628\" height=\"406\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-dip.jpg 628w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-dip-300x194.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/lego-dip-600x388.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 628px) 100vw, 628px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Once you can do 3 sets of 15 dips no problem, you have a few options to ramp up the difficulty:</strong></p> \n<p><strong>#1) Add weight</strong> to your bodyweight dips by:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>Picking up a dumbbell between your feet (challenging)</li> \n <li>Wearing a weighted backpack (awkward)</li> \n <li>Wearing <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Harbinger-Polypropylene-30-Inch-Steel-Chain/dp/B001P0S3XU/ref=as_li_ss_tl?keywords=weight+belt&amp;pd_rd_i=B001P0S3XU&amp;pd_rd_r=07572056-3ab4-497a-95f5-8371918b7650&amp;pd_rd_w=W7ZM6&amp;pd_rd_wg=Pq9HR&amp;pf_rd_p=91b604bb-c371-4573-970f-bed68a552852&amp;pf_rd_r=6BC05DHB3KDCT1M0GJHC&amp;qid=1560463573&amp;s=gateway&amp;linkCode=sl1&amp;tag=nerdfitn-20&amp;linkId=c7668854eb301fb3a516ea1a2cb26b9d&amp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">a belt with weights</a> hanging off it (what I do)</li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3657490\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/weighted-dip-gif.gif\" alt=\"My favorite method for doing weighted dips includes a special belt (shown here).\" width=\"460\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p><b>#2) Go Slower</b>: keep your abs tight, and lower yourself ridiculously slow.</p> \n<p>Your body will have to recruit every muscle in your chest, shoulders, and triceps (including all stabilizer muscles) to keep your body under control.</p> \n<p><b>#3) Try Ring Dips:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3634629 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/ring-dip.gif\" alt=\"The ring dip is a great way to build back and shoulder muscle.\" width=\"460\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p><b>Lower yourself down until your chest touches the rings (yes, that low!) and then push up until you are in a straight arm support position.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’ve never played with gymnastic rings before, the instability of the rings will provide a greater challenge than your standard dip </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">station</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can also lower the height of your rings to utilize some </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">support</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> from your feet:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3634630\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/assissted-ring-dip.gif\" alt=\"The floor can help a lot when doing ring dips!\" width=\"460\" height=\"259\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Raise the rings higher and </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">higher</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> as you grow stronger and stronger.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Make sure you check out our “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/lord-of-the-rings-how-to-get-in-great-shape-using-gymnastic-rings/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Guide to Training with Gymnastic Rings</a>” if you’d like to learn more.&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<h2><a name=\"home_dips\"></a>How to Do Dips at Home</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3627223\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/lego-tv-1.jpg\" alt=\"It's time to learn what triggers your habits\" width=\"724\" height=\"353\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/lego-tv-1.jpg 2037w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/lego-tv-1-300x146.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/lego-tv-1-768x374.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/lego-tv-1-713x348.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/lego-tv-1-600x292.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 724px) 100vw, 724px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>If you’re training at <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-a-home-gym-the-ultimate-guide-for-garage-gym-ideas/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">your home gym</a>, you can absolutely do bodyweight dips.</strong></p> \n<p>Here are two variations to try:</p> \n<p><strong>#1) Bodyweight Dips Between Two Chairs or Bar Stools:</strong></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Chair Dips\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/wjsbLgE3dvI?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p>This is all going to be about the chairs or barstools you can find.</p> \n<p>The important thing here is the stability of your furniture – don’t pick anything that’s wobbly. However, if you have a couple tall and sturdy chairs or bar stools, you can set them up on either side of you to perform your bodyweight dips.</p> \n<p>If they’re too high for you and you can’t quite get your feet on the ground for assisted dips, no problem. Just stand on a few books or a short stool to help you gain support.</p> \n<p><strong>#2) Bodyweight Dips Off a Countertop:</strong></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Countertop Dips\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/9u-hqQ15oSU?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p>Another great option is to perform dips on the corner of two sturdy countertops. As long as you can place your hands to the side so they can face forward, and you have plenty of room to maneuver between them, then you’re solid.</p> \n<p><strong>One thing you should be careful with is bench dips, which could be done off of a couch:</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3840909\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/bench-dip.gif\" alt=\"A gif of a woman doing a bench dip\" width=\"417\" height=\"263\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">The trouble with this comes from your arms being behind you</span>.</p> \n<p>As we covered in the “How to Do Pain-Free Dips” <a href=\"http://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=3026#tips_to_dip\">video above</a>, this position is a common problem area for causing pain in bodyweight dips. If it hurts when trying the bench dip, stick to the other two home variations above.</p> \n<h2><a name=\"getting_started_with_dips\"></a><strong>When Should You Do Dips in Your Workout? (Getting Started)</strong></h2> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-3656969\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/diver-sunset.jpg\" alt=\"This man clearly knows to &quot;dip&quot; when the occasion arrives.\" width=\"800\" height=\"434\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/diver-sunset.jpg 2031w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/diver-sunset-300x163.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/diver-sunset-768x416.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/diver-sunset-713x387.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/diver-sunset-600x325.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Now that you know </b><b><i>how </i></b><b>to do dips, let’s discuss </b><b><i>when </i></b><b>to do them.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Unless you’ve been strength training for years and know what you’re doing, we recommend that you pick a full-body routine that you can do 2-3 times a week.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So let’s<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-build-your-own-workout-routine/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"> build a full-body workout</a> right now!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>You want a workout routine that has at least one exercise for:</b></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Quads (front of your legs).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Butt and hamstrings (back of your legs).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Chest, shoulders, and triceps: (“push” muscles).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Back, biceps, and grip ( “pull” muscles).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Core (abdominals and lower back).</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dips would make a great addition to your “push” muscles (chest, shoulders, triceps).</span></p> \n<p><b>So a sample workout routine that includes dips could look like:</b></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-how-to-squat-properly/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Barbell squats</a>: 5 sets of 5 reps.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-the-deadlift/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Barbell Deadlifts</a>: 3 sets of 3 reps.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dips: 3 sets of 15 reps.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/do-a-pull-up/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Pull-ups (or chin-ups)</a>: 3 sets of 8 reps.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wy7QOQEZ8Rg\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Planks</a>: 3 sets, 1 minute hold each.</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That’s all!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Do your full-body workout and then go play some Nintendo.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3656984 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/mario-nintendo.gif\" alt=\"Mario earned his video game
