today.</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#commit_to_healthy_eating\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">None of this matters without your BIG WHY:</span></a></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#healthy_eating_next\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Healthy Eating: Next Steps.</span></a></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span id=\"more-11045\"></span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"healthy_eating\"></a>The Truth About Healthy Eating</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3568861\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/stuffed-veggies.jpg\" alt=\"What foods make up a healthy diet?\" width=\"622\" height=\"364\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/stuffed-veggies.jpg 622w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/stuffed-veggies-300x176.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/stuffed-veggies-600x351.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 622px) 100vw, 622px\" /></p> \n<p><b>It’s really easy to tell people the following advice:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“To lose weight, just eat more REAL food.”</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Just eat less fast food and junk food.”</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Try to eat more organic vegetables watered by unicorn tears, farm-to-table meals served by centaurs, and kale omletes made with eggs from chickens that you raised since birth.”&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Okay so maybe people don’t say the last one.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>But it’s not far from what healthy people say to people who can’t seem to get healthy.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In my opinion, these positions are completely out of touch with reality and it makes me plum dog mad.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603571\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/angry.gif\" alt=\"No one likes being told &quot;just eat better.&quot;\" width=\"468\" height=\"260\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For starters, fast food is crazy delicious and dirt cheap, and often the only way that many busy parents can feed themselves and their kids<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-1\" id=\"refmark-1\"><sup>[1]</sup></a>.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Next, applying morality and guilt to food consumption (“I’m being ‘so bad’ by eating this cookie”) creates an emotional rollercoaster – my </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">least</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> favorite kind of roller coaster.</span></p> \n<p><strong>I mean come on, we don’t need to be told that freshly grown fruits and veggies are better for us than junk food.</strong></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We don’t need to be told that organic grilled chicken and kale salad is healthier than a Double Whopper with Cheese.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603598\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/obviously.gif\" alt=\"Snape knows he should eat veggies to be healthy. But HOW DO YOU DO IT!\" width=\"378\" height=\"324\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We all know this!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>So rather than “trying harder” to eat healthier we’re going to use things like “science” and “human psychology” and “excessive quotation marks.”&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cool?</span></i></p> \n<p><b>Here’s what you need to know: If you’re just trying to be healthier and maybe lose some weight,</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> there’s no need to start funneling kale smoothies, mainlining chicken and broccoli, and abandoning your loyalty to the Burger King.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">can</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> lose weight and be healthy while still eating these foods occasionally.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Heck, people have lost weight by eating Twinkies<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-2\" id=\"refmark-2\"><sup>[2]</sup></a> and drinking soda and eating at McDonald’s 3 times per day<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-3\" id=\"refmark-3\"><sup>[3]</sup></a>.</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I share this info not to promote those foods, but rather make a big point:</span></i></p> \n<p><b>If you are terrified of giving up all “junk food”…</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You do not need to give up fast food if it brings you joy</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You do not need to feel shame for eating ice cream.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You don’t need to use terms like “cheat meal” or “guilty pleasure” when talking about a chocolate chip cookie.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Food isn’t good or evil, my dear friend!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s just food!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Let’s bring it all together:</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If we have certain health goals, we can give ourselves the best chance of success by getting strategic about what foods we say “YES” to, and what foods we say “SOMETIMES” to.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">These YES foods give us more energy and have fewer calories on average than “junk food,” which means we’re likely to eat fewer total calories without realizing it.</span></p> \n<p><b>And thus, we end up with the Triforce of Awesome:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A longer lifespan.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A smaller waistline.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A happier, healthier existence.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3603605\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Triforce.gif\" alt=\"Healthy eating can help you be awesome in multiple ways.\" width=\"500\" height=\"212\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So what are these magical foods we’re talking about?</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I thought you’d never ask.</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"what_is_healthy_eating\"></a>What is Healthy Eating?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3603716\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/stromtrooper-egg-713x533.jpg\" alt=\"IS this egg part of a healthy diet? Let's find out!\" width=\"713\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/stromtrooper-egg-713x533.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/stromtrooper-egg-300x224.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/stromtrooper-egg-768x574.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/stromtrooper-egg-600x449.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/stromtrooper-egg.jpg 1920w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Removing all the morality and science of food, let’s talk about a realistic definition of “healthy food”:</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Foods I can eat frequently that give me enough fuel to get through the day AND don’t make me miserable.”</span></p> \n<p><b>Most doctors, websites, and books have generally the same list of “healthy foods”:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Protein like meat and legumes.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fresh fruits and vegetables.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Healthy carbohydrates like rice, quinoa.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Healthy fats like almonds and olive oil.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Occasional cheese and dairy.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A more complete list of healthy foods is below).</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Why is it that these are the foods that happen to end up on every list on every website when it comes to “healthy eating?”&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3604380\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/pooh-thinking.gif\" alt=\"Why do all sites advise more of less the same foods for a healthy diet?\" width=\"350\" height=\"189\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Simple. </span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They are full of vitamins and nutrients while also being lower in calories than the processed foods that have been designed to be overeaten<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-4\" id=\"refmark-4\"><sup>[4]</sup></a>.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They also fill us up, making us feel satiated, and keep us under our calorie total for the day<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-5\" id=\"refmark-5\"><sup>[5]</sup></a>.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Now you’re starting to get it:</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If we can prioritize these foods on our plate even occasionally, we’ll feel full more often while eating fewer calories…&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Which leads to </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">sustainable weight loss and maintenance</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603637\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/yes.gif\" alt=\"This man is stoked he gets to lose weight sustainably through healthy eating...and punching his enemies. \" width=\"377\" height=\"236\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let me drive this point about calories vs energy into your brain (not literally).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are 4 foods in the exact same quantity, 200 calories (courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.wisegeek.com/what-does-200-calories-look-like.htm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">wiseGEEK</a>):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"wp-image-3500307 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/calories-in-a-sesame-seed-bagel-s.jpg\" alt=\"2/3 of a bagel is 200 calories.\" width=\"348\" height=\"248\" /><img class=\"wp-image-3500308 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/calories-in-uncooked-pasta-s.jpg\" alt=\"This handful of pasta is 200 calories.\" width=\"348\" height=\"248\" /><img class=\"wp-image-3500309 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/calories-in-sliced-smoked-turkey-s.jpg\" alt=\"This handful of turkey is 200 calories.\" width=\"348\" height=\"248\" /><img class=\"wp-image-3500315 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/calories-in-apples-s.jpg\" alt=\"This plate full of apples is 200 calories.\" width=\"348\" height=\"248\" /></p> \n<p>And here’s a huge plate of broccoli, also 200 calories:</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3574949\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli.jpg\" alt=\"A pic of 200 calories of broccoli\" width=\"605\" height=\"403\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli.jpg 605w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 605px) 100vw, 605px\" /></p> \n<p><b>In this context, the realization that we might overeat certain foods compared to others starts to become more clear:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If we accidentally overeat broccoli</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, we might eat an extra 20 calories. And who accidentally overeats broccoli?</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If we accidentally overeat spaghetti</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, we might eat an extra 500-1000 calories.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">If we accidentally eat a family-sized bag of Sour Patch Kids</span>,</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> we might eat an extra 2000 calories (and have no tastebuds left on your tongue)<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-6\" id=\"refmark-6\"><sup>[6]</sup></a>.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Which brings me to the next point:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>We humans are terrible at estimating how many calories we eat<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-7\" id=\"refmark-7\"><sup>[7]</sup></a>.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Like, really really bad at it. I bet the proportions of the above foods surprised you.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We consistently eat much more than we realize, by 40%+.</span></p> \n<p><b>To make matters worse, we also OVERestimate how many calories we burn through exercise.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">One study showed that Fitness trackers like AppleWatch or Fitbit overestimate exergy burned through exercise by 20% or more<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-8\" id=\"refmark-8\"><sup>[8]</sup></a>.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3596493\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/portlandia-fitbit.gif\" alt=\"Our Fitbit trackers might not be super accurate when reporting calories burned. Take this into account when referencing your calorie needs.\" width=\"449\" height=\"253\" /></p> \n<p><b>So when we “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">can’t lose weight</a>,” it’s not because we have a broken metabolism.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s not because we have bad genetics<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-9\" id=\"refmark-9\"><sup>[9]</sup></a>.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Or that we’re not eating for our blood type.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">It’s because we consistently eat too much food without realizing it</span>.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603642\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/deadpool-ugh.gif\" alt=\"Deadpool tries to match his calorie goals...when not saving the world and whatnot.\" width=\"298\" height=\"298\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Because we </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">always </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">have a ready supply of new energy from recently eaten food, more than we need, our body NEVER has to dip into our stored fat to burn for fuel.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And when we </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">think </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">we’ve out-exercised our bad diet, we really haven’t.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So it’s time to stop “trying harder” and instead “try differently”:</span></p> \n<p><b>In order for us to get healthy, we need to find ways to include more foods that fill us up AND taste good.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Luckily, I have that list riiiiight here!</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"healthy_food_list\"></a>How to Start Eating Healthy (Healthy Food List)</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3616724 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png\" alt=\"If your meal plate looks like this, you're doing great!\" width=\"720\" height=\"567\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png 720w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-300x236.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-713x561.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-600x473.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p> \n<p><b>There are three big macronutrients that we’re going to focus on as we build our plate like the image above:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Protein:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> building blocks for our muscles.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Carbohydrates:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> our bodies will burn as fuel.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Fats:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> can be burned as fuel, and also helps with nutrition absorption!</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>#1) </b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>PROTEIN</b></span><b>: Priority Numero Uno.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Protein is amazing.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your body uses protein to rebuild your muscles and keep you strong, especially if you are <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/25-ways-to-exercise-without-realizing-it/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">exercising</a> or <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">strength training</a> regularly.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Protein is both good for you AND satiating without being a calorie bomb.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Protein can come from any number of sources, including:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Meat (steak, bison, pork).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fowl (chicken, turkey, duck).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Eggs!<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-10\" id=\"refmark-10\"><sup>[10]</sup></a></span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fish and shellfish (salmon, tuna, shrimp).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Legumes (black beans, chickpeas).</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not a meat-eater? Read our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-eat-a-plant-based-diet-a-scientific-look-at-going-vegan-safely/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">massive plant-based guide</a>!</span></i></p> \n<p><b>A serving of protein is about the size and thickness of your palm.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3610479 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-713x475.png\" alt=\"A serving of protein should be about the size of your palm, like so.\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size-600x400.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-serving-size.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>*The 4 oz serving is for an uncooked piece of meat. Cooking reduces about 25% of the weight, bringing it down to about 3 oz.</em></p> \n<p><b>When building a plate, aim for the following amount of protein:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dudes: 1-2 servings (6-8 oz or about 170-228 g): two palms</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dudettes: 1 serving (3-4 oz or about 85-114 g): 1 palm.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>If you’re curious, here’s how much protein is in a serving of food:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">4 oz (113 g) serving of chicken has around 30 g of protein.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">4 oz (113 g) serving of salmon has 23 g of protein</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">4 oz (113 g) of steak has 28 g of protein.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As we cover in our “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/protein-shakes-for-newbies-what-to-buy-when-to-drink/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">how much protein should I eat per day?</a>” you can target anywhere from 80% to 100% of your bodyweight in pounds per gram of protein, with an upper limit of 250g<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-11\" id=\"refmark-11\"><sup>[11]</sup></a>:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you weigh 150 pounds (68 kg), target 120-150g of protein.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you weigh 200 pounds (90 kg), target 160-200g of protein.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you weigh 250 pounds (113 kg), target 200-250g of protein.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you weigh more than 250 pounds (113 kg), target 250g of protein.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>#2: </b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>VEGETABLES</b></span><b>: The </b><b>difference-maker when it comes to healthy eating and weight management.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603421 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/dancing-broccoli.gif\" alt=\"Vegetables are the key to healthy eating.\" width=\"500\" height=\"261\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">They are nutrient-dense: full of all the good nutrients that your body can use to function at optimal performance.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Next, they are energy-dense but calorie-light, which means you can eat lots of them, you’ll feel full, but you’re unlikely to over-consume calories.</span></p> \n<p><b>A serving of veggies is about the size of your fist.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3606769 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-713x475.png\" alt=\"A serving of veggies should be the size of your first (or greater).\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size-600x400.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/vegetable-serving-size.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Remember this is what just 200 calories of broccoli looks like (holy crap). This is at least 5 full servings:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3574949\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli.jpg\" alt=\"A pic of 200 calories of broccoli\" width=\"393\" height=\"262\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli.jpg 605w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/what-200-calories-look-like-food-broccoli-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 393px) 100vw, 393px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Here’s a quick, non-complete list of veggies that can fill your plate:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Broccoli</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Broccolini</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cauliflower</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Spinach</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Kale</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Spaghetti squash<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-12\" id=\"refmark-12\"><sup>[12]</sup></a></span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Brussels sprouts</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Zucchini</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cucumber</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Carrots</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Onion</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Asparagus</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Target 2 servings of vegetables on your plate – it should take up ½ the plate!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“But Steve, I don’t like vegetables…yet!”&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That’s cool, I didn’t eat vegetables until I was 22. Now, they’re a main staple of every meal I eat.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If this is you, read our guide on “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/vegetable-haters-how-to-start-eating-vegetables/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">how to make vegetables taste good</a>.”</span></i></p> \n<p><b>To recap portion sizes of protein and vegetables:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3610480 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-veggies-1-456x600.png\" alt=\"A reminder of the protein and veggie serving sizes.\" width=\"456\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-veggies-1-456x600.png 456w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-veggies-1-228x300.png 228w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-veggies-1-600x790.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/protein-veggies-1.png 719w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 456px) 100vw, 456px\" /></p> \n<p><b>#3) </b><b>HEALTHY CARBOHYDRATES</b><b>: Fuel and fiber!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">These are the foods that can be an important part of a diet, provided you </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">eat them in the right quantities</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> for your goals.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">These foods are also great to consume right after a strenuous <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/strength-training-101-where-do-i-start/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">strength training workout</a> to help your muscles and liver refill their glycogen stores (their energy tanks<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-13\" id=\"refmark-13\"><sup>[13]</sup></a>, essentially).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Examples of healthy carbohydrates:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rice, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/is-rice-healthy-for-me-does-white-vs-brown-rice-matter/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">brown or white</a></span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Legumes, lentils</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Quinoa</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Potatoes</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Sweet potatoes</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yams</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pasta</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whole grain bread</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is a list of REAL food, minimally processed, that also have plenty of fiber<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-14\" id=\"refmark-14\"><sup>[14]</sup></a>.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>If you’re wondering how fruit factors into this equation, </b><a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#fruit\"><b>that’s the next section</b></a><b>.</b></p> \n<p><b>Back to healthy carbs:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> when consumed in proper proportion, these are great foods that can help you feel full and give you energy and all that jazz.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Just make sure you know what an </b><b><i>actual</i></b><b> portion of these foods are!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">EVERYBODY accidentally overeats carbohydrate-heavy foods, even healthy ones, and then wonders <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/why-cant-i-lose-weight-heres-the-truth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">why they aren’t losing weight</a>.</span></p> \n<p><b>To help you get better at eyeballing serving sizes:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3606899\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-713x475.png\" alt=\"Showing you a serving of carbs\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-300x200.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1-600x400.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-size-1.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1 serving of a starchy carbohydrate is 1 cupped hand (uncooked), or your two hands forming a cup (cooked).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Here are some images to help you learn proper portion sizes (thanks to <a href=\"https://www.safefood.eu/Healthy-Eating/Food,-Diet-and-Health/Eating-In/Serving-sizes.aspx\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">SafeFood</a>):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603859 size-large\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-sizes-713x281.png\" alt=\"This pic will give you an idea of how carbs should fit on your plate, so you can start eating healthy!\" width=\"713\" height=\"281\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-sizes-713x281.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-sizes-300x118.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-sizes-768x302.png 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-sizes-600x236.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/carb-serving-sizes.png 1044w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>#4) </b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>HEALTHY FATS</b></span><b>: No longer the enemy!</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fat had a bad rep in the 70s, 80s, and 90s, but now things are swinging wayyyyy back in the other direction.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In some circles, fat is now considered the healthiest thing on the planet, will do your taxes for you, and is considered a superfood.</span></p> \n<p><b>Let’s get to the truth:</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fat is neither a superfood nor evil.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603668\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/dr-evil.gif\" alt=\"Fat can be part of a healthy diet, and is not evil, to the frustration of Dr. Evil.\" width=\"443\" height=\"188\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s just a macronutrient that you can eat that can help you reach your goals in the right quantity, or keep you from your goals if it’s overconsumed.</span></p> \n<p><b>When your doctor tells you to eat more healthy fats, she’s referring to polyunsaturated and monounsaturated fats</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-15\" id=\"refmark-15\"><sup>[15]</sup></a><strong>.</strong></span></p> \n<p><b>Healthy fat can be found in foods like:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Avocado&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Almonds&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Walnuts</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Macadamia nuts</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Olive oil</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Almond butter&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Peanut butter</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Now, science has recently come around on saturated fat too</b><a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-16\" id=\"refmark-16\"><sup>[16]</sup></a>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">– once completely vilified, but now cautiously considered okay for moderate consumption.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Saturated fats can come from things like:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whole milk</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Full fat dairy</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Coconut oil</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grass-fed butter</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Lard</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fatty cuts of meat</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fat can be good for you provided you’re eating the right quantity for your goals.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">However, like carbs, fats can be overconsumed accidentally too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>To help you gauge: a serving size of fat is roughly the size of your thumb!</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3606783\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size-713x475.png\" alt=\"A serving of fat should be about your thumb!\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size-713x475.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-serving-size.png 720w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>THIS is a single serving of almonds (162 calories):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603871\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-713x475.jpg\" alt=\"Knowing the correct amount of almonds to eat can help you with your calorie goals.\" width=\"476\" height=\"317\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/almonds.jpg 960w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 476px) 100vw, 476px\" /></p> \n<p><b>THIS is a serving of olive oil (119 calories, taken from <a href=\"http://runtastic.com/blog/en/hand-portion-size/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Runtastic</a>):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3742707\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb.jpg\" alt=\"Your thumb is about one serving of olive oil\" width=\"479\" height=\"220\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb.jpg 995w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-300x138.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-768x353.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-713x327.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/olive-oil-thumb-600x276.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 479px) 100vw, 479px\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As you can see, if you’re not careful – you can accidentally eat an extra 500 calories of “healthy fats” by absentmindedly eating too many “heart-healthy” fats.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Many folks in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Coaching Program</a> had us analyze why they weren’t losing weight, even though they “only ate grilled chicken and veggies.”&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When we dug into it, they had been preparing all of their food in an extra 500-600 calories worth of olive oil they weren’t accounting for.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603643\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/doh.gif\" alt=\"Homer just realized he eats too much olive oil. \" width=\"376\" height=\"287\" /></p> \n<p><b>To recap fats and starchy carbs:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> feel free to include a starchy portion to your plate in the form of rice, potatoes, pasta, or legumes, and healthy fats can help spice up a meal too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3606905\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-and-carb-serving-sizes-2-453x600.png\" alt=\"A reminder of the serving sizes of carbs and fat.\" width=\"453\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-and-carb-serving-sizes-2-453x600.png 453w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-and-carb-serving-sizes-2-227x300.png 227w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-and-carb-serving-sizes-2-600x795.png 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/fat-and-carb-serving-sizes-2.png 712w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 453px) 100vw, 453px\" /></p> \n<p><b>I realize that was a CRAZY amount of info, so let’s put it all on the same Healthy Plate:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3616724 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png\" alt=\"If your meal plate looks like this, you're doing great!\" width=\"720\" height=\"567\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2.png 720w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-300x236.png 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-713x561.png 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/healthy-eating-plate-2-600x473.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1-2 servings of protein (¼ of plate)</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">2 servings of vegetables (½ of plate)</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1 serving potatoes, rice, or pasta. (1/4th of plate)</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1 serving of fat (size of your thumb)</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1 zero-calorie or low-calorie beverage (water, diet soda, tea)</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>I know that not all of your meals are going to be perfectly segmented like a bento box. For example:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A fatty cut of meat like chicken thighs means your fat and protein are commingling. Cool.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Lentils and legumes mean your protein and your carbs are attached at the hip. Swell.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A burrito bowl with chicken, rice, guacamole, and cheese means all of your macros are cohabitating. Neato!</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Salmon cooked in olive oil and coated in almond flakes means your fat and protein have fused. Stupendous!</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>This plate and serving size stuff above is just to help you get started thinking about healthy food differently and in <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-portion-control-how-to-lose-weight-with-portion-control/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">proper portion sizes</a>:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Trying to </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-not-suck-at-losing-weight/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">lose weight</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">? Reduce your portions of carbs and fats.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Trying to </span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/13-tips-for-guaranteed-weight-gain-the-skinny-nerd-manifesto/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">gain weight</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">? Increase your portions of carbs and fats!&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Remember, </b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>all calories count</b></span><b>.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I can already understand your next series of questions:</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li><b>“What about beverages?” <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Simple. Liquid calories count too. So stick to low or zero-calorie drinks like water, tea, coffee, and diet soda.&nbsp;</span></b></li> \n <li><strong>“How about condiments?” </strong><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grilled chicken slathered in 1000 calories of buffalo sauce means you’re still eating a calorie bomb!</span></li> \n <li><strong>“But what about things like Paleo or Keto? I thought low carb = healthy?”</strong> <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I address that in the “<a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#best_diet\">which diet is right for me?</a>” section. Keep reading.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<h2><a name=\"fruit\"></a>What’s the Deal with Fruit? Is Fruit Healthy?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3603730\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-fruit-healthy-eating-713x473.jpg\" alt=\"Yes, fruit can be healthy, as this LEGO has figured out by cutting into it.\" width=\"713\" height=\"473\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-fruit-healthy-eating-713x473.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-fruit-healthy-eating-300x199.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-fruit-healthy-eating-768x510.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-fruit-healthy-eating-600x398.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-fruit-healthy-eating.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>As we lay out in our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/is-fruit-healthy-for-you/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">“Is Fruit Healthy?” Guide</a>, fruit is absolutely healthy and can help you reach your goals – in the right quantities.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fruits are full of nutrients, packed with fiber, and can make for a great snack or part of a protein-focused breakfast!</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3603675\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/dancing-watermelon.gif\" alt=\"Watermelon can be part of a healthy diet. Just maybe don't eat the kind that dances.\" width=\"480\" height=\"303\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Personally, I blend up frozen mixed berries in my <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/protein-shakes-for-newbies-what-to-buy-when-to-drink/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">post-workout smoothie</a>.</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Just remember that fruit, like every other food, obeys the laws of thermodynamics.</span></i></p> \n<p><b>So, simply be aware of the calories (and carb and fiber content if you’re following a lower carb diet):</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Apple: 95 cal, 25g carbs, 4.4g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Banana: 105 cal, 27g carbs, 3.1g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Orange: 45 cal, 11g carbs, 2.3g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pear: 100 cal, 28g carbs, 3g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Peach: 59 cal, 14g carbs, 2.3g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Strawberries (1 cup): 47 cal, 11g carbs, 3g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pineapple (1 cup): 82 cal, 22g carbs, 2.3g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grapes (1 cup): 62 cal, 16g carbs, 0.8g fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Raspberries (1 cup): 65 cal, 15g carbs, 8 fiber.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Fruit is a better, healthier alternative to nutrient-empty food from a vending machine.</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603648\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/homer-vending-machine.gif\" alt=\"Fruit is healthier than what you'll find in a vending machine, plus you'll lower your chance of getting stuck in one.\" width=\"408\" height=\"308\" /></p> \n<p><b>Where fruit can get you in trouble is if you start to move in the direction of “fruit-like”:</b></p> \n<p><b>#1) <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/is-drinking-fruit-juice-healthy-is-fruit-juice-really-as-bad-as-soda/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Fruit juices</a></b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> (cranberry juice, orange juice, grape juice): these are high calorie, sugar-filled beverages.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>For example, here are the calories in one </b><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><b>8 oz</b></span><b> </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-17\" id=\"refmark-17\"><sup>[17]</sup></a></span><b> serving of:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Apple Juice: 103 calories, 22 g of sugar</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Orange Juice: 103 calories, 18 g of sugar</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grape Juice: 136 calories, 32 g of sugar</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>#2) Dried fruit:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> notoriously easy to overeat because they are so small. Since the water has been taken out, all that’s left is the sugar and fiber.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here’s 1 serving of raisins, which is 108 calories and 21 g of sugar:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603882\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/raisins-713x475.jpg\" alt=\"Since the water is taken out, raisins have a lot of sugar and calories. \" width=\"501\" height=\"334\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/raisins-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/raisins-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/raisins-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/raisins-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/raisins.jpg 960w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 501px) 100vw, 501px\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you are saying </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“oh man, I eat 5x that many raisins when I eat them…</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">” then multiply those calorie and sugar numbers by 5!</span></p> \n<p><b>3) Fruit Smoothies:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Just because it’s a fruit smoothie doesn’t mean it won’t make you fat! Have you seen the calorie count and sugar content of smoothies and ‘green drinks’? Yikes.</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Green Machine Naked Juice (15.2 oz or 450 ml bottle): 270 calories, 53 g of sugar.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Smoothie King Banana Boat (20 oz or 591 ml smoothie): 450 calories, 70 g of sugar.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3604321\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/spit-up-drink.gif\" alt=\"A man realizing how much sugar is in his drink.\" width=\"298\" height=\"205\" /></p> \n<p><b>To recap: fruit is healthy, provided you stick to fresh or frozen and not fruit-like food, dried fruit, or canned fruit packed in syrup.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you enjoy a small glass of orange juice occasionally, or you pack a serving of raisins in your lunch and it makes life worth living, by all means!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Just don’t chug OJ by the gallon, drink a 64 oz “real fruit smoothie,” and eat raisins by the handful and then wonder why you’re not losing weight.</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"dairy\"></a>Are Cheese and Dairy healthy?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3603731\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-with-cheese-713x475.jpg\" alt=\"Is cheese and dairy part of a healthy diet? This LEGO is clearly skeptical.\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-with-cheese-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-with-cheese-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-with-cheese-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-with-cheese-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>We get questions about these two types of food frequently.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let me start by saying I’m assuming you’re not doing <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-paleo-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Paleo</a> (which says “NO dairy and NO cheese”), or <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-eat-a-plant-based-diet-a-scientific-look-at-going-vegan-safely/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">plant-based</a> (which says NO to all animal products).</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I’ll also assume you’re not doing <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-keto-diet-or-ketogenic-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Keto</a>, which almost requires you to load up on dairy and cheese to eat enough fat every day!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Let’s pretend you’re just curious if cheese and/or dairy can be consumed on a “healthy diet:”:</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">YES</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, you can still eat cheese and be healthy.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">YES</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, you can still eat dairy and be healthy.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And there was much rejoicing:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603650\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/school-hooray.gif\" alt=\"Yes, both dairy and cheese can be part of a healthy diet. Rejoice!\" width=\"385\" height=\"268\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Like the healthy carbs and fats listed above, it all comes down to your calories consumed in a day, and if these foods fit into your <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">daily calorie goals:</a></strong></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Want to put cheese on top of your salad of chicken and vegetables? Great!&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Want to eat greek yogurt, a <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/protein-shakes-for-newbies-what-to-buy-when-to-drink/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">scoop of protein powder</a>, and frozen berries for your breakfast? Amazing!&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Want to eat a bowl of cereal with skim milk (or whole milk) in the morning with your kid before school? No problem.</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is true for higher-fat cheeses or full-fat dairy too – the food just needs to fit into your goals!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Luckily, all dairy comes labeled, and most cheese will come with a nutrition label on it too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Just make sure your portions are in line. For reference, here are four different servings of cheddar cheese (about 113 calories a serving):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603906\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/serving-of-cheddar.jpg\" alt=\"A serving of cheddar cheese is about 113 calories. \" width=\"395\" height=\"263\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/serving-of-cheddar.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/serving-of-cheddar-300x200.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 395px) 100vw, 395px\" /></p> \n<p><b>And here’s a serving of greek yogurt (100 calories in 170 grams):</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603907\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/greek-yogurt-713x535.jpg\" alt=\"a cup of greek yogurt is about 100 calories,\" width=\"409\" height=\"307\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/greek-yogurt-713x535.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/greek-yogurt-300x225.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/greek-yogurt-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/greek-yogurt-600x450.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/greek-yogurt.jpg 800w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 409px) 100vw, 409px\" /></p> \n<p><b>And although nobody in the history of the world has ever eaten an actual serving…here is a serving of ice cream:</b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603913\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/ice-cream-713x559.jpg\" alt=\"A serving of ice cream is about the size of a tennis ball, cleverly shown here.\" width=\"437\" height=\"343\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/ice-cream-713x559.jpg 713w,
