437px\" /></p> \n<p><em><b> (A scoop of ice cream the size of a tennis ball is about 127 calories, cleverly shown above.)</b></em></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So, dairy and cheese are both perfectly acceptable health food options! Just make sure they fit into your goals.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you are NOT losing weight, and you consume a lot of dairy and/or cheese, consider measuring your intake and see if it’s in line with your expectations!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"best_diet\"></a>What’s the best diet for me? Keto vs Paleo vs Plant-based.</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3568866\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/yoda-and-r2.jpg\" alt=\"Yoda knows a lot about healthy eating (and fixing R2)\" width=\"635\" height=\"387\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/yoda-and-r2.jpg 635w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/yoda-and-r2-300x183.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/yoda-and-r2-600x366.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 635px) 100vw, 635px\" /></p> \n<p><b><i>“Low fat diets? Low carb diets? No carb diets? I don’t know which one is the BEST diet!”&nbsp;</i></b></p> \n<p><b><i>“Help me, Steve Kamb, you’re my only hope.”</i></b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Okay, you’re probably not saying that, but it’s an excuse to pay homage to Star Wars so I can use the great photo above.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You probably do have questions though about what’s healthier, a low fat diet or a low carb diet.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Low carb diets are all the rage right now, but are they healthy and will they help you <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-not-suck-at-losing-weight/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">lose weight</a>?&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3603654\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/maybe-1.gif\" alt=\"Will a low carb diet help you lose weight? Maybe!\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><b>Maybe. </b></p> \n<p><b>It depends on h</b><b>ow your body regulates glucose (blood sugar)</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-18\" id=\"refmark-18\"><sup>[18]</sup></a>:</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Some who don’t regulate glucose well do better on a lower carb diet.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Others who do regulate glucose well might do better on a lower fat diet.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Studies show that people who follow </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">EITHER</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> a low fat </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">OR</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> a low carb diet will still lose weight, as long as they are in caloric restriction and can adhere to the diet for at least a year<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-19\" id=\"refmark-19\"><sup>[19]</sup></a>.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So, it comes down to: “which diet are you more likely to stick with for a year or longer?”</span></p> \n<p><b>I personally lost <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/losing-the-last-20-pounds-7-lessons-learned-while-still-eating-carbs/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">22 pounds over 6 months on a lower fat diet</a> (and eating plenty of carbs), but everybody is different.</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This means you’ll need to experiment and see which is better for your lifestyle, and your day to day well-being.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3601635\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/science-experiment.gif\" alt=\"Experiment with different kinds of diet until you find one that works for you!\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But I bet you have questions about the big popular diets too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>I’ve written </b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/paleo-keto-slow-carb-vegan-how-to-determine-the-perfect-diet-for-you/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><b>a huge guide that covers all popular weight-loss diets together</b></a><b>, but we’ve also written individual ultimate guides that cover:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-keto-diet-or-ketogenic-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Keto Diet (Ketogenic Diet)</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-beginners-guide-to-intermittent-fasting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Intermittent Fasting</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-paleo-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Paleo Diet</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-beginners-guide-to-the-mediterranean-diet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Mediterranean Diet</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-eat-a-plant-based-diet-a-scientific-look-at-going-vegan-safely/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Vegan and Plant-Based Diets</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/should-you-try-the-carnivore-diet-5-questions-addressed/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Carnivore Diet</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/does-the-military-diet-actually-work/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Military Diet</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Let’s look at each of these diets and explain why they will help you lose weight, at least temporarily:</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><b>Truth #1:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp; Every diet works in the short term.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><b>Truth #2:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Nearly every diet fails in the long term.</span></p> \n<p><b>Let’s address these two truths individually:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Why does </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">every diet work</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> in the </span><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">short term</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">?&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3604349\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/thinking-ape.gif\" alt=\"Why DO diets work in the short term? This ape wants to know so he can eat healthy.\" width=\"353\" height=\"282\" /></p> \n<p><b>All the diets above have a clever way of restricting calories without you needing to count calories, which leads to weight loss:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Paleo Diet:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> eliminate everything but veggies, meat, fruit, and nuts.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Intermittent Fasting:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> skip an entire meal!</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Keto Diet:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> remove an entire macronutrient from your diet (carbs).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Military Diet: </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Only eat specific foods in certain quantities.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Plant-based Diet:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Only eat vegetables and foods from plants.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Carnivore Diet:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Only eat meat! Eliminate everything else.&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Of course there are plenty of benefits from following certain diets for certain groups of people. For example, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-larry-beat-rheumatoid-arthritis-and-got-strong-as-hell/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Larry went Keto</a> and it helped him reduce inflammation from rheumatoid arthritis.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">However, 99% of the reason why these diets result in short term weight loss is that they get us to eat fewer calories!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>The problems arise when we get to Truth 2:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Nearly every diet fails in the long term.”</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Put another way:&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Temporary changes create temporary results.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If somebody “goes Keto” for 60 days, they’ll most likely lose weight, and might even feel better! This is cool.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">BUT!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(There’s always a but…)</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If they spend those 60 days in misery, dreaming of carbs, counting down the meals until they can “go back to eating like normal,” they will put all of the weight back.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603657\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/luke-no.gif\" alt=\"The weight loss you obtain through diet will only stick as long as you stay on that diet.\" width=\"423\" height=\"238\" /></p> \n<p><b>In order for restrictive diets to create permanent results for somebody, they need to be adopted PERMANENTLY!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For most of us mere mortals, we can’t stick with a restrictive diet for 30 days, let alone a year or a decade.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For these reasons, I strongly advise you to change how you think about dieting.</span></p> \n<p><b>You need to determine how likely you are to stick with a restrictive diet permanently:</b></p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How averse are you to change?</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How likely are you to stick with your changes?</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Have you tried a restrictive diet in the past and failed?</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Do you have a healthy relationship with food?</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Do you have an “All or nothing?” mindset?</span></li> \n</ol> \n<p><b>Like playing a video game, you need to determine what level of difficulty you are willing to attempt.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Playing on “Ultra Hard Difficulty” (like Keto) gives you less room for error, but it can also produce impressive results quickly – if you don’t rage quit.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And 99% of people rage quit restrictive diets like Keto.</span></p> \n<p><b>So what’s the best diet for you?</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I’ll give you the same answer that I give people when they ask me, “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-determine-your-perfect-workout-plan/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">What’s the best workout plan?</a>”:&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/paleo-keto-slow-carb-vegan-how-to-determine-the-perfect-diet-for-you/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The best diet</a> is the one that helps you reach your goals, that you ENJOY, and that you’ll actually stick with permanently!</span></i></p> \n<p><b>Personally, I don’t follow any sort of restrictive diet</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I’m a big fan of small changes that eventually produce big results, like my boy Optimus Prime:</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3568867\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/optimus-prime.gif\" alt=\"Optimus Prime wants you to eat healthy.\" width=\"400\" height=\"308\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is why I’ve SLOWWWWLY <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/paleo-keto-slow-carb-vegan-how-to-determine-the-perfect-diet-for-you/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">adjusted my diet over the past decade</a>, so that no change was too drastic and I could stick with it permanently.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s not a diet. It’s a lifestyle change. Permanently.</span></p> \n<p><b>And that’s what I would recommend for you:</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Small, non-scary, permanent changes over a long time period!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You need to start thinking in terms of “days and years,” not “weeks and months:”</span></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Want to get in shape? Think in days and years, not weeks and months\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/ieY_8ZL0v78?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<h2><a name=\"meal_prep\"></a>How to Grocery Shop, Cook and Meal Prep!</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3603741\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-store-713x446.jpg\" alt=\"Marge knows how to buy food to eat healthy, Yoda is just here for moral support. \" width=\"713\" height=\"446\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-store-713x446.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-store-300x187.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-store-768x480.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/lego-store-600x375.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>Okay! Now that you’ve determined your healthy eating strategy, it’s time to take action.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>There are three big steps you’ll want to master if this is your path:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>Step #1: Grocery Shopping! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can read our full guide on “</span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/cooking-101-how-to-navigate-a-grocery-store/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><b>How to grocery shop</b></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">”, and we even have a video that keeps things fun too:</span></p> \n<p><iframe title=\"Grocery Store\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/bLvkCoWhAI8?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><b>Here’s how to grocery shop like a pro:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Stick mostly to the outer rim.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> This means you’re mostly buying meat, fruit, and veggies<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-20\" id=\"refmark-20\"><sup>[20]</sup></a>.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Read the nutrition label!</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Just because it says it’s healthy on the front doesn’t mean it is. <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-read-a-nutrition-label-part-1/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Read the nutrition label</a> and learn portion sizes. This can help keep you below your <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-many-calories-should-i-eat-every-day-a-look-at-total-daily-energy-expenditure-tdee/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">daily calorie goal</a>.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Don’t shop hungry!</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Seems silly, but you end up buying way more junk food accidentally if you shop while hangry (a mix of hungry-angry, never a great emotion).</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Make a list.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Before you go grocery shopping, write down everything you should get. You can even put “non-healthy” food items on the list. But then you can </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">only</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> buy what’s on your list! This means no candy in the check-out aisle. Or because Oreos are on sale! Plan ahead. Stick to the script, sister.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Step #2: Learn to cook! </b></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3558839 size-full\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/chef_gif-1.gif\" alt=\"Once you get cooking you'll feel like the Swedish Chef. \" width=\"500\" height=\"200\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In the next section, we share recipes for <a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#healthy_eating_meals\">basic healthy meals</a> that you can cook at home.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here’s why cooking at home is amazing:&nbsp;</span></p> \n<ol> \n <li><b>You know all of the ingredients.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> When you eat at restaurants or pick up fast food, there are often hidden calories in the cooking oils and sauces that are sabotaging your healthy efforts. Because of this, it’s really hard to have an idea of how many calories you’re consuming. When you prepare food at home, you know what you’re getting.</span></li> \n <li><b>You can recreate healthier versions of your favorite foods. <span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Making homemade tacos or pizza with homemade dough can be a great date-night experience, makes your stomach happy, AND can help you reach your goals! </span></b></li> \n <li><b>You save money.</b> If your budget is tight, grocery shopping and cooking your own meals is a great way to balance your budget and free up some cash! Our most successful <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">coaching clients</a> work with their coaches on building the habit of cooking at home.</li> \n</ol> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Now, if you’re somebody who only ever uses your kitchen to heat up microwave meals, that’s no problem.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3604350\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/microwave.gif\" alt=\"You can get by eating healthy with just a microwave!\" width=\"416\" height=\"234\" /></p> \n<p><b>Here are the guides you should check out:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/cooking-101-your-essential-kitchen-tools/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Cooking 101: Essential Kitchen Tools</a>: Not sure what kind of knives to get, or what you REALLY need? I’ve been there. Which is why we created this guide for you!&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/lost-at-the-grocery-store-introducing-the-nerd-fitness-pantry/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">How to Stock Your Pantry</a>: If you’re not sure what to stock your shelves with, and how to set yourself up for long term success.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Step #3 (BONUS): Meal Prep and Batch Cooking! </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;This step isn’t necessary, but if your goal is to make healthy eating a habit for you and your family, batch cooking can be the difference maker!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">By “batch cooking,” I simply mean setting aside time to prepare larger quantities of food at the start of the week, so that throughout the week you already have meals to eat!&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Personally, <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/losing-the-last-20-pounds-7-lessons-learned-while-still-eating-carbs/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">batch cooking changed my life</a>.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603676\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/sheep-giving-thumbs-up.gif\" alt=\"Batch cooking can change your life, as this sheep knows!\" width=\"309\" height=\"243\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And every single success story we’ve featured on Nerd Fitness (</span><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-mark-adjusted-his-mindset-learned-to-meal-prep-and-lost-65-pounds/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">like this one</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">) involved some sort of batch cooking (planning your meals for the week ahead).&nbsp;</span></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Here’s our guid</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>e</strong> on “<a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/a-step-by-step-guide-to-meal-planning-and-prep/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">How to start Batch Cooking and Meal Prep.</a>”&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Let me walk you through <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/super-simple-batch-cooked-chicken-for-lazy-people/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">how I batch cook chicken for the week</a>.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> There’s even a video too:</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><iframe title=\"Super Simple Chicken For Lazy People | Nerd Fitness\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/oX-wTkhvRjE?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://www.nerdfitness.com\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Follow these rules, and you will </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">crush it </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">in the Healthy Eating Department<a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-21\" id=\"refmark-21\"><sup>[21]</sup></a>!</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"healthy_eating_meals\"></a>19 Healthy Eating Meals You Can Cook Today</h2> Check out <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/15-easy-meals-you-can-cook-at-home-during-the-apocalypse/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">26 Easy Meals You Can Cook</a>.&nbsp;</em></p> \n<p><b>Just remember, quantity counts:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>If your goal is <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/how-to-not-suck-at-losing-weight/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">weight loss</a></strong><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>:</strong> Keep an eye on the fat and carbs portion of your plate!&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>If your goal is <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/13-tips-for-guaranteed-weight-gain-the-skinny-nerd-manifesto/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">weight gain</a>,</strong><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> then you can ratchet up your total calories consumed by increasing your fat and carbohydrate portion of your plate!&nbsp;</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not sure how to make these meals work or how to adjust them for your goals?&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>This is exactly what we do with our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Online Coaching Program</a>!</b></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> <a target=\"\" href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\"> <button class=\"cta-button yellow\"> Let us help you make better food choices! Our Online Coaching Program rocks: </button> </a> </span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"commit_to_healthy_eating\"></a>Will You Commit to Healthy Eating?</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3568874\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Batman-knows-his-big-why-713x400.jpg\" alt=\"When not fighting crime, Batman eats healthy.\" width=\"713\" height=\"400\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Batman-knows-his-big-why-713x400.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Batman-knows-his-big-why-300x168.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Batman-knows-his-big-why-768x431.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Batman-knows-his-big-why-600x337.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Batman-knows-his-big-why.jpg 2048w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>As we start to wrap up this guide, I have one BIG final question for you:</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Why the hell are you reading this?”&nbsp;</span></i></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Sorry to be so blunt, but your answer matters!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>If you are trying to eat better because somebody </b><b><i>told you to</i></b><b>, or because you think you </b><b><i>should</i></b><b>, you’re setting yourself up to fail.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You might be excited and motivated to eat healthy today, and that’s great!&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-3604351\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/apes-dancing.gif\" alt=\"The start of a new activity, even a diet, can be very exciting as these apes know!\" width=\"480\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But next week, Oscar in Accounting will put cake in front of you at work, and ask you to “live a little” and eat some cake “just this once.”&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And then you’ll discover apps are half-priced at Chatchki’s during happy hour, and you figure “well I already had cake, might as well split some shrimp poppers and extreme fajitas with Meredith.”</span></p> \n<p><b>This is how it always happens: <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/motivation-youre-doing-it-wrong/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Motivation abandons us</a> when we need it most.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And then one “ehh” choice becomes three bad choices which becomes “crap, I failed at my diet! I’m a loser. Okay I’ll just try harder next month…”</span></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you are committed to this goal of eating healthier, you need a DAMN good reason to start eating healthier in the first place!</span></i></p> \n<p><b>Here are some examples you can build off of:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“I want to look better naked and start dating again.”</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“I want to do epic stuff like running my first 5K.”</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“I don’t want to die early like my dad did.”</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“I want to find out what I’m capable of.”</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“I want to feel pride, not shame, when I look in the mirror.”</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>There are many tough days ahead, many happy hours, and sabotaging coworkers.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Having a great reason WHY can be the light in the darkness that helps you navigate the maze of temptation.</span></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603785\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Frodo.gif\" alt=\"Frodo isn't afraid of the dark...or eating unhealthy.\" width=\"364\" height=\"238\" /></p> \n<p><b>In our <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Nerd Fitness Coaching program</a>, we call this “The Big Why,” and <a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/blog/the-10-key-differences-between-weight-loss-success-and-failure/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">having a reason can be the difference</a> between success and failure:</b></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s our Big Why</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> that stops us from living emotionally and chasing instant gratification from a donut or six slices of pizza when we’re sad or stressed.</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s our Big Why</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> that allows us to say “Yes, I can have a slice of pizza, because I planned for it in my ‘calorie budget’ today. I’m not gonna feel bad about it either, because my breakfast tomorrow is gonna be great.”</span></p> \n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s our Big Why</span></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> that allows us to get back on track after a vacation or after just one day of poor eating, instead of letting things slide for a week or a month.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>Have your Big Why, and remind yourself of it constantly!</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Write it down, put it on a post-it note on your bathroom mirror, staple it to your forehead.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But have a REASON you’re committing to change.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It will be crucial when life starts to get busy next week and you want to give up. So let’s talk about next week (and beyond!)</span></p> \n<h2><a name=\"healthy_eating_next\"></a>Healthy Eating: Next Steps!</h2> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-3603742\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/restaurant-table-with-dinner-713x475.jpg\" alt=\"You now know what it takes to eat healthy!\" width=\"713\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/restaurant-table-with-dinner-713x475.jpg 713w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/restaurant-table-with-dinner-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/restaurant-table-with-dinner-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/restaurant-table-with-dinner-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/restaurant-table-with-dinner.jpg 1920w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 713px) 100vw, 713px\" /></p> \n<p><b>This guide has provided you with all of the tools you need to start making healthier choices, but if you are looking to go a bit further…</b></p> \n<p><b>#1) Our </b><a href=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/coaching-overview-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><b>1-on-1 Online Coaching</b></a><b> program: </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">a coaching program for busy people to help them make better food choices, stay accountable, and get healthier, permanently.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can schedule a free call with our team so we can get to know you and see if our coaching program is right for you. </div>\n    </form>\n   </div></img>\n </div>\n <div class=\"clearme\"></div>\n</div> \n<p><b>Healthy eating will change your life.&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But it needs to fit INTO your life too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Small changes, not dramatic shifts!</span></p> \n<p><b>You don’t have to give up the foods you love, you just need to PLAN for them.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Learn how to make a plate like we <a href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#healthy_food_list\">lay out in this guide</a>.</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Prioritize protein, and always put a fruit or vegetable on your plate before filling the rest of it up!</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This will get you 90% of the way towards a great healthy eating strategy.</span></p> \n<p><strong>And when in doubt, whenever you’re not sure if you should eat a particular food, ask yourself “What would Batman do?”</strong></p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-3603663\" src=\"https://www.nerdfitness.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/batman.gif\" alt=\"Ask yourself &quot;What would Batman eat?&quot;\" width=\"412\" height=\"270\" /></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Seriously, this has been studied with children, and it helped them make healthier food choices by giving the decision making over to somebody they looked up to <a class=\"fn-ref-mark\" href=\"http://nerdfitness.com/blog/?p=11045#footnote-22\" id=\"refmark-22\"><sup>[22]</sup></a>. It’s called “self-distancing,” and there’s no reason it can’t work for you too.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Oh, and when you eat a bad meal – who cares?! “Never two in a row,” right? Make the next meal healthy.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<p><b>YOUR MISSION, SHOULD YOU CHOOSE TO ACCEPT IT:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><b>Start eating healthy today with literally one change:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Try a new vegetable.</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cut one soda out of your day.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Prioritize protein in your next meal.&nbsp;</span></li> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Swap out one high-calorie drink for a zero-calorie drink.</span></li> \n</ul> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I don’t care what the change is, just as long as you make one!</span></p> \n<p><b>Okay enough about me, let’s talk about you:&nbsp;</b></p> \n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">What’s the ONE change you’re going to make today?</span></i></p> \n<p><b>For the Rebellion!</b></p> \n<p><b>-Steve</b></p> \n<p><b>PS: Make sure you read the rest of the articles in our “How to Lose Weight 101” Series!&nbsp;</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li
